<p>102b.5</p>chags la sogs pa rnams lta smos ci dgos/ de'i phyir rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi rgyan zhes bya ba rnal 'byor chen po'i rgyud las rnam pa mang por kun rdzob kyi bden pa rnam par bzhag nas yang gsungs pa/ dngos med nyid kyi phyogs la yang / /las kyi 'bras bu la sogs pa/ /
<p>102b.6</p>rmi lam bzhin du nyams myong ba/ /'di ni mngon sum dag tu 'byung / /zhes bya ba la sogs pas rgya chen don dam pa'i bden pa mngon du ma gyur gyi bar du kun rdzob bden pa la gus pas gnas par gsungs so/ /'di ni kun rdzob nyid du yang ma dag pa med par smra ba 'ga' zhig byung na
<p>102b.7</p>ni mngon sum du rigs pa sbyin zhing bden pa gnyis la gnas pa'i/ theg pa rab kyi mchog 'di ni/ /tshul la gnas na thob par 'gyur/ /zhes bya ba la sogs pa rgyud rnams tshig med par 'gyur te/ de'i tshe don dam pa'i bden pa kho na la gnas pa'i phyir ro/ /gzhan yang
<p>103a</p>
<p>103a.1</p>ji ltar dug sngags kyis rims mi 'phel ba zhes bya ba thos pa tsam dang / gzung ba dang de shes pa la dug mi gnod par shes pa tsam gyis ni dug chen po rnams zhi bar nus pa ma yin gyi yongs su bsgrubs pa'i skyes bus zhi bar byed do/ /de bzhin du de kho
<p>103a.2</p>na'i rnam par dag pa thos pa dang / der 'gyur ba'i lam ston pa gzung ba dang / rnam par dag pa dang ldan pa rnams 'ching bar mi 'gyur/ shes pa tsam gyis 'dod chags la sogs pas mi gnod par 'gyur ba ni ma yin no zhes bya ba'o/ /shin tu spros pas chog go/ /rang
<p>103a.3</p>gi brjod par bya ba nges par gzung ste/ rnal 'byor spyod pa dang / dbu ma pa'i dbye bas zab pa tsam dang ldan pa'i theg pa ni rnam pa gnyis yin la/ rnal 'byor spyod pa rnams kyang / shes pa rnam pa dang bcas pa dang / rnam pa med pa'i bye brag gis rnam pa gnyis so/ /
<p>103a.4</p>de bzhin du dbu ma pa yang kun rdzob shes pa'i rnam par smra ba dang / de bag chags su smra ba'i bye brag gis rnam pa gnyis so/ /da ni de dag gi 'dod pa'i rang bzhin brjod de/ shes pa rnam pa dang bcas pa rnams ni sems rang rig pa skad cig ma'i bdag nyid mi rtag pa rgyun
<p>103a.5</p>ma chad par 'byung ba 'di nyid kyi phyi rol lta bur rnam par gnas pa'i don nyams su myong ba yin gyis 'di na bdag dang skyes bu la sogs pa'i 'dzin pa po gzhan ni 'ga' yang med la/ phyi rol na dum bur gyur pa ltar gnas pa'i don rnams ni rang gi rnam par shes pa nyid kyi
<p>103a.6</p>rnam pa de ltar nam mkha' la brten nas snang ba 'byung gi /gzhan dbang phyug gis phyung ba la sogs pa'i don gzung bar bya ba ni 'ga' yang med pa'o/ /thams cad rang gi rnam par shes pa'i bdag nyid kho na bas gang la yang rjes su ma chags pa dang khong khro ba la sogs pa'i
<p>103a.7</p>skabs mi 'byed par tshogs yongs su rdzogs par byas nas/ sems de nyid rnam par dag pa'i ye shes tha mal pa'i mngon par zhen pa dang bral ba'i bdag nyid skad cig ma rjes su 'brel par 'byung bar gnas gyur pa ni 'bras bu sangs rgyas zhes rtog pa'o/ /shes pa
<p>103b</p>
<p>103b.1</p>rnam pa med par smra ba rnams ni sems rang rig pa rgyun 'brel par 'jug pa skad cig ma'i bdag nyid rnam pa dang bral ba 'ga' yang rig par mi byed pa de dag gcig dang tha dad las grol ba'i bag chags rnams rab tu dag cing / rnam pa thams cad dang bral ba rang rig
<p>103b.2</p>pa'i bdag nyid kyi bems po ma yin pa'i ye shes su gnas yongs su gyur pa 'di ni 'bras bu yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su rnam par dpyod par byed do/ /dbu ma pa kun rdzob shes pa'i rnam par smra ba rnams ni don dam pa'i rigs pa'i tshogs kyis sems dang
<p>103b.3</p>ye shes dag yod pa ma yin par smra la/ kun rdzob tu 'di ltar rnam par gzhag pa thams cad sems dang yid kyi rnam pa yul du gnas pa kho nar rtog go/ /de bzhin du kun rdzob bag chags su smra ba rnams kyi 'dod pa ni don dam pa'i bden pa snga ma lta bu las kun
<p>103b.4</p>rdzob tu rnam par gzhag pa rnams ni bag chags rnams kho na yin gyi/ sems ni rnam pa dang / 'gro ba'i bdag nyid du snang ba ma yin no zhes par ro/ /'di gnyis rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i bdag nyid 'dod pa dang / sems dang rang rig pa 'gog /rigs pa
<p>103b.5</p>bsgrub pa ni mthun no/ /kha cig na re 'di gnyis kyis lta ba gzhan sel ba na rim pa bzhin du/ yod dang med dang yod med dang / /yod med gnyi ga min pa ste/ /zhes pa dang / rtag dang mi rtag rtag mi rtag /rtag dang mi rtag gnyi ga min/ /zhes pas go rims bzhin du mu
<p>103b.6</p>bzhi rnam par rtog pa mi 'dra'o zhes zer ro/ /zab cing rgya che ba dang ldan pa'i theg pa ni bya ba dang / spyod pa dang / rnal 'byor dang / rnal 'byor chen po dang / rnal 'byor bla na med pa zhes bya bas rnam pa lngar 'gyur ro/ /'dir 'di dag gi rang gi ngo bo ni rnam par gsal bar
<p>103b.7</p>bla ma rnams kho na las shes par nus kyi/ gzhung gi tshig rnam par sbyar bas ma yin pa dang / rags pa rnams ni de kho na la 'jug pa la sogs pa'i gzhung rnams su yang rnam par gtan la phab pas/ 'dir bdag gis gsal bar dbye bar mi bya bar gzhag go/ /'di ni
<p>104a</p>
<p>104a.1</p>zab cing rgya che ba'i theg pa'i rnam par gzhag pa'o/ /gal te theg pa gsum kho na yin na theg pa gcig tu rnam par bshad pa de ji ltar 'gyur/ 'di ni nges pa med de 'bras bu la dang / rgyu la brten pa'i phyir te/ theg pa thams cad nges par nye ba dang ring ba
<p>104a.2</p>rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su 'gyur bas 'bras bu la brten pa bshad pa ste/ de bas na mtshan yang dag par brjod pa las/ theg pa gsum gyis nges 'byung la/ /theg pa gcig gi 'bras bur gnas/ /zhes gsungs pa nyid theg pa thams cad 'bras bu yang dag par rdzogs
<p>104a.3</p>pa'i sangs rgyas su 'gyur bar dgongs la/ bcom ldan 'das 'jam dpal yang gdul bya'i dbang las theg pa gsum char la zhon cing / chos kyi sku las kyang ma g.yos pa'o zhes bstod pa brjod pa'o/ /rgyu las kyang theg pa thams cad ni bdag dang gzhan la spong zhing / 
<p>104a.4</p>'bras bu sangs rgyas nyid skyed pa dang / chos kyi dbyings la tha dad pa med pa na ste/ don 'di la dgongs nas/ theg pa gcig cing tshul yang gcig yin te zhes bya ba la sogs pa rgya cher gsungs so/ /gal te 'ga' zhig theg pa bsam gyis mi khyab par bsgrub pa bcom ldan 'das kyi
<p>104a.5</p>bka' lang kar gshegs pa la sogs pa'i mdo las shes so zhe na/ 'dir/ ji srid sems ni 'jug gi bar/ /theg pa dag la thug pa med cing bya ba 'di ni theg pa gsum rnam par gzhag pa zhon pa'i theg pa pa rnams nyid kha cig rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba mngon du byed pa dang / 
<p>104a.6</p>la la mi sdug pa sgom pa dang / la la zad par gyi skye mched sgom pa'i bar gyis zhugs pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa la gzigs pa yin gyi rnam par gzhag pa gsum gyis bsdus pa'i theg pa gzhan ni mi 'byung ste/ de dag las gzhan pa'i lta ba ni nges par phyi rol mu stegs par
<p>104a.7</p>'gyur ba'i phyir ro/ /de ltar theg pa gsum rnams gsal bkod pas/ /'gro rnams gus bcas theg gsum myur zhon nas/ /srid mtsho las rgal bde ba chen po'i bdag /stug po bkod pa nyid du 'gyur bar shog /theg pa gsum rnam par gzhag pa zhes bya ba slob dpon
<p>104b</p>
<p>104b.1</p>mkhas pa chen po rin chen 'byung gnas zhi ba'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so// //rgya gar gyi mkhan po kr-iSh+Na pa dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o// /[ ]@##/ /rgya gar skad du/ yo ga a nut+ta ra
<p>104b.2</p>ya tan+t+rAr+tha a ba tA ra saM gra ha nA ma/ bod skad du/ rnal 'byor bla na med pa'i rgyud kyi don la 'jug pa bsdus pa zhes bya ba/ bcom ldan 'das 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /gang zhig thugs rje 'gro ba kun la mkha' ltar khyab/ /byin rlabs
<p>104b.3</p>theg pa la sogs gsung gi 'od zer gyis/ /mngon par mtho dang nges par legs pa sgrub pa'i thabs/ /ston mdzad rgyud dang mdo sde bcas pa'i tshogs la 'dud/ /bde gshegs yon tan kun gyi 'byung gnas kyis/ /thog mar thugs bskyed bar du tshogs gnyis
<p>104b.4</p>bsags/ /tha mar chos sku brnyes nas gzhan don ni/ /skye med ngang las gzugs kyi skur bstan te/ /'og min gnas su longs spyod rdzogs sku dang / /sprul pa'i sku yis 'dzam bu'i gling la sogs/ /gdul bya skal mos dbang po tha dad la/ /dgongs nas rnam thar
<p>104b.5</p>bsam gyis mi khyab gsungs/ /de la bcom ldan 'das kyis chos kyi phung po brgyad khri bzhi stong bka' stsal pa de dag kyang 'bras bu'i tshul gyis theg pa gcig tu 'dus te/ theg pa chen po'o/ /de yang mtshan yang dag par brjod pa las/ theg pa gsum gyis nges
<p>104b.6</p>'byung la/ /theg pa gcig gi 'bras bur gnas/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / slob dpon phyogs kyi glang pos kyang / 'di ni mya ngan 'das 'gro lam gcig pu/ /bde gshegs nyi ma'i gsung 'od snang ba can/ /bdag med rang bzhin 'phags pa stong phrag 'jug
<p>104b.7</p>rnam par rgyas pa blo dman gyis mi mthong / /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /de dag kyang spyir dus de re zhig pa'i dbang du byas na/ theg pa ni gnyis su gzhag ste/ mngon par mtho ba'i theg pa 'jig rten pa dang / nges par legs pa'i theg pa 'jig rten las 'das pa'o/ /de yang / 
<p>105a</p>
<p>105a.1</p>lha dang mi yi theg pa ni/ /bcu drug char yang mi phod do/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /'jig rten las 'das pa'i theg pa la yang rnam pa gsum ste/ nyan thos kyi theg pa dang / rang rgyal ba'i theg pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa'o/ /de yang
<p>105a.2</p>lang kar gshegs pa'i mdo las/ byis pa rnams ni drang ba'i phyir/ /theg pa tha dad ngas bshad do/ /zhes gsungs so/ /theg pa de dag gi don mdor bsdu na rnam pa gsum du 'gyur te/ yul dang / dus dang / 'bras bur gzhag pa yin no/ /de yang 'di skad du/ 
<p>105a.3</p>mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan las/ yul gyi rgyu ni gsum dag dang / /sbyor ba bzhi yi bdag nyid dang / /chos sku phrin las 'bras bu ni/ /mdor bsdus gzhan de rnam pa gsum/ /zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o/ /de la nyan thos dang rang rgyal ba'i 'jug pa ni ye shes la
<p>105a.4</p>'jug pa la sogs pa mngon pa sde bdun dang / bye brag tu bshad pa chen po la sogs pa gzhan du grags par zad do/ /de la byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa ni bdag dang gzhan gyi don phun sum tshogs par 'gyur bas theg pa chen po'i don ni mchog tu blang bar bya ba yin te/ 
<p>105a.5</p>smon lam la sogs pas bla na med pa'i bde bar gshegs pa'i go 'phang thob par 'gyur ba ni theg pa chen po'i don yin pa'i phyir ro/ /de yang ji skad du tshul gsum gyi sgron ma las/ smon pa dang ni 'jug pa dang / /de bzhin zab dang rgya che nyid/ /mi ldog 'bras bu thob pas
<p>105a.6</p>kyang / /theg pa chen po khyad par 'phags/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / theg pa chen po nyi shu pa las kyang / rtog pa'i chu bos gang ba yi/ /'khor ba'i rgya mtsho chen por ni/ /theg chen gru la ma zhugs par/ /su zhig pha rol 'gro bar 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs so/ /de la
<p>105a.7</p>byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa la yang rnam pa gnyis te/ sa dang pha rol tu phyin pa'i theg pa dang / gsang sngags 'bras bu rdo rje'i theg pa'o/ /de la sa dang pha rol tu phyin pa'i theg pa ni mdo sde'i don bsdus pa mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan la sogs pas don gyi 'grel pa rgyas
<p>105b</p>
<p>105b.1</p>par gsungs pa yin no/ /de yang ji skad du/ mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan las/ rnam kun mkhyen nyid lam shes nyid/ /de nas thams cad shes pa nyid/ /rnam pa kun rdzogs rtogs pa dang / /rtse mor phyin dang mthar gyis pa/ /skad cig gcig mngon rdzogs byang chub/ /
<p>105b.2</p>chos kyi sku dang de rnams brgyad/ /ces gsungs pa yin no/ /de la gsang sngags 'bras bu rdo rje theg pa ni de kho na nyid du smra zhing dbang po rnon po'i don du gsungs pas na sa dang pha rol tu phyin pa'i theg pa las khyad par du 'phags pa yin te/ de kho na'i don phyin ci ma log pa'i
<p>105b.3</p>dka' ba med par myur du bsgrub pa'i phyir ro/ /de yang sgyu 'phrul dra ba las/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas gang 'das dang / /de bzhin gang dag ma byon dang / /da ltar byung ba'i mgon po rnams/ /'gro la phan phyir bzhugs pa dag /de dag kun gyis gsang sngags kyi/ /
<p>105b.4</p>cho ga mchog bzang 'di brnyes nas/ /dpa' bos byang chub shing drung du/ /thams cad mkhyen pa mtshan med brnyes/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / gzhan yang tshul gsum gyi sgron ma las/ don gcig na yang ma rmongs pa dang / /thabs dang dka' ba med pa dang / /dbang
<p>105b.5</p>po rnon po'i don gyi phyir/ /sngags kyi bstan bcos khyad par 'phags/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /gsang sngags 'bras bu rdo rje theg pa la ni 'jug pa'i sgo rnam pa bzhi ste/ bya ba'i rgyud dang / spyod pa'i rgyud dang / rnal 'byor chen po'i rgyud ces spyir grags pa yin no/ /
<p>105b.6</p>de dag kyang gsang zhing sbas pas 'grub la snod ma yin pa rnams kyi spyod yul ma yin pas na gsang ba'o/ /de ni sngags kyi theg pa zhes kyang bya ste/ sngags dang phyag rgya'i sgo nas dngos grub rnams sgrub pa'i phyir dang / /des yid skyob par byed cing 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal dka' ba
<p>105b.7</p>med par myur du sgrol ba'i phyir dang / nyan thos la sogs pa blo dman pa rnams skrag par byed pa'i phyir dang / sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis bstod cing bkur la bsngags pa'i phyir dang / de kho na nyid kyi don phyin ci ma log par ston pa la sogs pa'i phyir
<p>106a</p>
<p>106a.1</p>sngags so/ /de ni sku dang longs spyod dang gnas dang mdzad pa yongs su dag pa'i tshul gyis 'jug pas na 'bras bu ste/ lam thams cad kyi 'bras bu phyag rgya chen po'i dngos grub yin pa'i phyir ro/ /de nyid ni 'tshe ba med cing yang dag pa'i don thogs pa med par
<p>106a.2</p>thob par byed pas na rdo rje'o/ /de ni theg pa yang yin te/ lam des dka' ba med par myur du yid la byed pa'i phyir ro/ /de yang ji skad du/ gsang bas grub phyir gsang sngags te/ /rdo rje theg pa 'bras bu che/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /de la gsang sngags kyi theg pa'i sde
<p>106a.3</p>snod ni theg pa gsum du ma gtogs par 'dod de/ de ni rig 'dzin gyi sde snod ces bya bar grags pa byang chub sems dpa'i sde snod gzhan yin no/ /de yang ji skad du/ phyi nang gsang ba theg pa gsum/ /dam chos yongs su gzung bar bya/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /yang na
<p>106a.4</p>sde snod gsum du 'dus par yang 'chad de/ gsung rab yan lag dgu ni theg pa chen po'i sde snod yin la/ gsang sngags kyi theg pa'i sde snod kyang gsung rab yan lag dgur 'dus shing / bslab pa rnam pa gsum ston pa'i phyir sde snod gsum du gzhag pa'o/ /de yang ji skad du bzhi
<p>106a.5</p>brgya lnga bcu pa las/ gdul byas bskyod pa sna tshogs mchog /dam chos gsung rab yan lag dgu// zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /de la bya ba'i rgyud ni rig pa mchog dang rab tu grub pa'i rgyud la sogs pa ste/ rgyas par ni dbye ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa yin no/ /de'i gdul
<p>106a.6</p>bya zab mo'i don la 'jigs par lta zhing shin tu gtsang sbra byed la/ ye shes sems dpa'i bde ba spangs shing / lha'i snyems pa med pa rmad du byung ba'i yul la skyon gyi rgyu'i rtog pa'i rab tu rtog pa'i spyod pas sgrub par byed pa'i don gsungs pa yin no/ /de la spyod pa'i rgyud la ni mngon par byang
<p>106a.7</p>chub pa la sogs pa ste/ mdor bsdu na stong phrag brgyad yin la/ rgyas par ni dbye ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa yin no/ /gang dag las kyi bya ba sna tshogs rgya chen po phyag rgya dmigs pa'i mtshan nyid la sogs pa dang / rnal 'byor gnyis kas dngos grub kyi don la sgrub par byed
<p>106b</p>
<p>106b.1</p>pa'i don du gsungs pa yin no/ /de la rnal 'byor gyi rgyud ni de kho na nyid bsdus pa la sogs pa gsungs te/ mdor bsdus na stong phrag drug pa yin la/ rgyas par ni dbye ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa yin no/ /gang dag lha'i dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lo dgod pa dang / de las byung ba'i
<p>106b.2</p>las sgrub pa de kho na nyid rnam pa bcu rab tu dpyad pas de rnal 'byor dang phyi'i bya bas kyang ting nge 'dzin gyi yan lag tu bsgyur bas dngos grub thams cad thob par 'dod pa'i don du gsungs pa yin no/ /rnal 'byor chen po'i rgyud ni gdul bya dbang po mchog dang / rnal 'byor gtso
<p>106b.3</p>bor byed pa'i don gsungs pa yin te/ mdor bsdu na stong phrag bcu gnyis yin la/ rgyas par ni dbye ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa yin no/ /de la rnal 'byor chen po'i rgyud ni rnam pa gnyis te/ rang bzhin gyis rgyud dang brtag pa'i rgyud do/ /de la rang bzhin gyi rgyud ni mdor bsdu
<p>106b.4</p>na rnam pa gsum ste/ rgyu'i rgyud dang / 'bras bu'i rgyud dang / thabs kyi rgyud do/ /de yang gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgyud phyi ma las/ rgyud ni rgyun ces bya bar grags/ /de ni rnam pa gsum du 'gyur/ /gzhi dang de bzhin rang bzhin dang / /mi 'phrogs pa yi rab phye ba/ /gzhi dang
<p>106b.5</p>rang bzhin rgyu yin te/ /de bzhin mi 'phrogs 'bras bu'o/ /gzhi ni thabs zhes bya ba ste/ /gsum gyis rgyud kyi don bsdus pa'o/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /btags pa'i rgyud kyang rnam pa gnyis te/ rnal 'byor thabs kyi rgyud dang / rnal 'byor shes rab kyi rgyud do/ /
<p>106b.6</p>de dag kyang rnam pa gnyis su 'dod de/ rnal 'byor mchog gi rgyud dang / rnal 'byor bla na med pa'i rgyud ces bya ste/ rig pa'i rgyud dang / rtsa ba'i rgyud ces btags pa yin no/ /de la thabs dang shes rab kyi rgyud kyi dbye ba ni/ de kho na nyid ston pa dang / gdul bya dang / rnam
<p>106b.7</p>dag dang / thun mong du mngon par grags pa la sogs pas tha dad par gzhag par bya'o/ /de yang rgya che ba'i de kho na nyid gang du gtso bor ston pa'i rgyud ni thabs kyi rgyud do/ /gang du zab pa nyid gtso bor byas te ston pa ni/ shes rab kyi rgyud do/ /gang du skyes pa dang / rang gi sde pa
<p>107a</p>
<p>107a.1</p>'dul ba'i phyir lha pho'i rnam pa mang bar ston pa'i dkyil 'khor ni thabs kyi rgyud do/ /gang du bud med dang / phyi rol mu stegs can 'dul ba'i phyir de dag dang rjes su mthun pa'i lha mo'i rnam pa mang ba'i dkyil 'khor ston pa ni shes rab kyi rgyud do/ /gang du phyi
<p>107a.2</p>nang gi phung po dang khams dang skye mched kyi rnam par dag pa'i lha ston pa ni thabs kyi rgyud do/ /gang du phyi nang gi rtsa dang / byang chub kyi sems rnam par dag pa'i lha ston pa ni shes rab kyi rgyud do/ /gang du 'jig rten dang rjes su mthun pa'i lha'i rnam pa ston pa ni thabs kyi rgyud do/ /
<p>107a.3</p>gang du 'jig rten dang 'gal ba'i lha'i rnam pa ston pa ni shes rab kyi rgyud ces bya ba la sogs pa btags pa yin no/ /de yang / shes rab kyi ni dbye ba yis/ /rnal 'byor pa ni gnyis su 'dod/ /ces gsungs pa yin no/ /de la thabs dang shes rab kyi rgyud de dag gi don
<p>107a.4</p>mdor bsdu na snga ma bzhin du rnam pa gsum yin te/ yul dang / 'bras bu dang / rgyu'i rnam pas so/ /de la gang dag de kho na nyid kyi don mthong bar 'dod pa rnams kyis rtogs shing khong du chud par bya ba'i yul ni mdor bsdu na rnam pa gnyis yin te/ kun rdzob kyi bden pa
<p>107a.5</p>dang don dam pa'i bden pa'o/ /de la kun rdzob kyi bden pa la yang rnam pa gnyis te/ yang dag pa dang yang dag pa ma yin pa'o/ /de yang yang dag pa'i kun rdzob ni sems kyi rang bzhin 'od gsal ba ste/ rnam grangs kyi don dam par 'dod pa yin no/ /de yang ye shes rdo rje
<p>107a.6</p>kun las btus pa las/ sems ni nam mkha' mtshan nyid can/ /rnam pa med pa'i ngo bor khyab/ /'gro dang 'ong ba dang bral ba'o/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /yang dag pa ma yin pa'i kun rdzob ni de las bzlog pa'i chos thams cad yin no/ /de dag gi mtshan nyid
<p>107a.7</p>thun mong du bstan pa ni/ rlung gi dbang gis sna tshogs snang zhing nyams su myong bar byed pa yin no/ /de yang dgongs pa lung bstan pa las/ ji srid 'jig rten gyis brtags dang / /de bzhin brtags pa sna tshogs rnams/ /rnam rtog byang chub sems zhes pa'i/ /rlung ltar rtag
<p>107b</p>
<p>107b.1</p>tu 'byung ba yin/ /bde sdug la sogs chos rnams kyi/ /sa bon lta bur bshad pa yin/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / gzhan yang ye shes rdo rje kun las btus pa las/ rigs kyi bu kun rdzob ni mi brtan pa dang g.yo ba'o/ /de'i bden pa ni chu zla lta bu'o/ /yang de nyid las
<p>107b.2</p>rnam par shes pa ni 'od gsal ba las 'byung ngo / /de ni sems dang yid ces bya ste/ kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba'i chos thams cad ni de'i rtsa ba can yin no zhes gsungs pa dang / rgyud thams cad kyi bla mar gyur pa las/ 'gro ba 'di kun sangs rgyas lnga
<p>107b.3</p>bdag nyid/ /gar mkhan dag dang rol mo bzang ltar snang / /gang du bde chen zhes bya gcig pu nyid/ /gcig pu nyams ni du mar gar mdzad do/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / dgongs pa lung bstan pa las kyang / byang chub sems las rlung 'byung zhing / /nam mkha' las
<p>107b.4</p>ni rnam gnas pa/ /sems can kun gyi srog gyur cing / /lnga yi bdag nyid bcu ming can/ /rten 'brel bcu gnyis zhes grags pa/ /ngo bo nyid rnams gsum du 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / yang de nyid las/ snying por gyur pa rang srog las/ /khams gsum na ni
<p>107b.5</p>gzhan med de/ /khams gsum rlung gi sprul pa ste/ /rmi lam rmi ba bzhin du blta/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / yang de nyid las/ skye dang gnas dang 'jig pa dang / /srid pa bar mar gnas pa ste/ /ji snyed 'jig rten gyis brtags pa/ /sems dang rlung gi rnam 'phrul lo/ /
<p>107b.6</p>zhes gsungs pa dang / gzhan yang snang ba'i phreng ba las kyang / sems tsam la ni brten nas su/ /phyi rol don la mi brtag go/ /de bzhin nyid la dmigs nas su/ /sems tsam las ni bzla bar bya/ /sems tsam las ni bzlas nas su/ /snang ba med la gnas par 'gyur/ /
<p>107b.7</p>snang med gnas pa'i rnal 'byor pa/ /de yis theg pa chen po mthong / /zhes gsungs pa dang / rin po che phreng ba las kyang / ngar 'dzin las byung phung po rnams/ /ngar 'dzin de ni don du brdzun/ /gang gis sa bon brdzun pa de/ /skye ba bden pa gang la zhig /ces gsungs
<p>108a</p>
<p>108a.1</p>pa dang / ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyal po las kyang / dper na chu shing rlon pa'i phung po las/ /snying po 'dod pa'i skyes bus rnam btsal na/ /phyi dang nang na'ang snying po yod ma yin/ /chos rnams thams cad de 'drar shes par gyis/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / 
<p>108a.2</p>yang de nyid las/ dper na gzhon nu rmi lam nang gnas tshe/ /des ni bu skyes shi bar gyur pa mthong / /skyes pas dga' la shi bas gdung bar 'gyur/ /chos rnams thams cad de 'drar shes par gyis/ /zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs pa yin no/ /don dam pa'i bden
<p>108a.3</p>pa yang rnam pa gnyis te/ rnam grangs pa dang rnam grangs ma yin pa'o/ /de la rnam grangs pa ni ye shes dang / de kho na nyid la dmigs pa'i tshul gsum pa'i rtags las skyes pa la sogs pa'o/ /rnam grangs ma yin pa ni chos thams cad rang bzhin gyis ma skyes pa ngo bo nyid
<p>108a.4</p>kyis gdod ma nas ma grub pa las dang skye ba thams cad dang bral ba/ rnam par rtog pa'i yul las 'das pa spros pa thams cad rnam par chad pa tsam ste/ bden pa gnyis gnyis su med pa'i ngo bo nyid do/ /de yang ye shes rdo rje kun las btus pa las/ don dam pa'i
<p>108a.5</p>bden pa ni stong pa bco brgyad de yang dag pa'i mtha'o zhes gsungs pa dang / dpal gsang ba 'dus pa las kyang / dngos po med pas sgom pa'i dngos/ /bsgom par bya ba bsgom pa min/ /de bas dngos po dngos med pas/ /bsgom pa dmigs su med pa'o/ /zhes bya ba la
<p>108a.6</p>sogs pa gsungs pa dang / gzhan yang de nyid las/ rang sems sems ni dmigs pa las/ /chos rnams thams cad rab tu gnas/ /nam mkha'i rdo rje gnas sems 'di/ /chos med chos nyid med pa'o/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / tshigs su bcad pa dgu pa las/ spros
<p>108a.7</p>pa med cing snang ba med/ /rnam rtog med cing shin tu phra/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / mngon par byang chub pa las kyang / thams cad nam mkha'i mtshan nyid de/ /nam mkha' la yang mtshan nyid med/ /gang zhig de rtogs 'dod pa ni/ /byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya'o/ /zhes
<p>108b</p>
<p>108b.1</p>gsungs pa dang / glang po mtshan bcings kyi mdo las kyang / gang gis skye ba 'byung ba ni/ /dngos po gang la'ang rnyed mi 'gyur/ /dngos po med pa'i ngo bo la/ /byis pa rnams ni 'byung bar 'dod/ /ces gsungs pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yul la 'jug pa ye shes
<p>108b.2</p>snang ba'i rgyan las kyang / rtag tu skye med chos ni de bzhin gshegs/ /chos rnams kun kyang bde bar gshegs dang 'dra/ /byis pa blo can mtshan mar 'dzin pa yis/ /'jig rten dag na med pa'i chos la spyod/ /ces gsungs pa dang / theg pa chen po nyi shu pa las kyang / 
<p>108b.3</p>gang tshe sgyu mkhan sgyu ma ni/ /spangs shing nye bar bsdus pa na/ /de tshe ci yang mi snang ste/ /de ni chos kyi chos nyid do/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / byang chub kyi sems bshad pa las kyang / rtogs pa po yis rtogs bya gang / /shes bya med pas shes pa med/ /de ltar shes dang
<p>108b.4</p>shes bya gang / /dngos po med par cis mi 'dod/ /rtogs bya rtogs byed rnam par sems/ /de bzhin gshegs pas ma gzigs so/ /zhes pa la sogs pa gzhung sna tshogs las gsungs pa yin no/ /de lta bas na de kho na mthong bar 'dod pa rnams kyis khong du chud cing
<p>108b.5</p>rtogs par bya ba'i yul thams cad ni bden pa gnyis su 'dus pa kho na yin no/ /de yang bden pa gnyis rnam par bstan pa las/ sangs rgyas rnams kyis chos bstan pa/ /bden pa gnyis la yang dag gnas/ /'jig rten kun rdzob bden pa dang / /dam pa'i don gyi bden pa'o/ /
<p>108b.6</p>zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /de ltar bden pa gnyis kyi mtshan nyid rtogs na 'bras bu sku gsum gyi rang bzhin la mngon par 'dod pa 'byung bas thams cad mkhyen pa yon tan gyi dbang phyug dang ldan pa bden pa gnyis kyi rang bzhin can bde ba chen po'i rnam pa chos thams cad kyi sku ste/ 
<p>108b.7</p>bde ba chen po'i sku zhes rnal 'byor chen po'i grub pa'i mtha' las 'dod do/ /de yang ji skad du/ rnal 'byor chen po'i bshad pa'i rgyud las/ dbang phyug brgyad kyis bcom ldan 'das/ /bde ba chen po'i gnas na bzhugs/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / dpal gsang ba 'dus pa
<p>109a</p>
<p>109a.1</p>las kyang / sngags kyi skyes bu ji snyed pa/ /rdo rje gsum gyi ye shes rdzogs/ /dbang po gnyis kyi sbyor ba yis/ /dngos po thams cad brtag par bya/ zhes gsungs pa dang / gzhan yang bshad pa'i rgyud las/ yon tan brgyad dang nyer ldan pas/ /
<p>109a.2</p>sems can thams cad rig 'gyur zhing / /'jig rten khams ni ma lus par/ /bdag nyid ye shes lus kyi rgyu/ /gtso bo gang du rgyu ba yi/ /de yi khyim ni nam mkha' nyid/ /bde ba chen po'i ting 'dzin gyis/ /de nyid du ni rtag tu dgyes/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / bde mchog
<p>109a.3</p>'khor lo las kyang / rnal 'byor thams cad bcom ldan 'das/ /rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs/ /khams gsum pa ni ma lus kun/ /de yi nye bar longs spyod nyid/ /ces gsungs pa dang / yang de nyid las/ lha dang mi yi bde ba ni/ /bsdus byas rdo rje 'dzin pa
<p>109a.4</p>yi/ /bcu drug char yang mi phod do/ /zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs pa dang / de kho na nyid rin po che snang ba las kyang / longs spyod rdzogs pa kha sbyor bde chen rang bzhin med/ /snying rjes ngas gang rgyun mi 'chad pa 'gog pa med/ /yan lag bdun po nyid dang ldan pa'i
<p>109a.5</p>bsgrub bya 'di/ /tshad mar yongs bsgos blo yis sngags pa bdag nyid 'dod/ /ces gsungs pa dang / gzhan yang / chos sku bde ba chen po ni/ /sku gnyis la ni khyab par gnas/ /zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs pa yin no/ /de la longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku ni chos kyi
<p>109a.6</p>sku dmigs pa med pa'i thugs rje chen po'i dbang gis mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis dang / dpe byad bzang po brgyad cus rnam par brgyan pa snang bar gyur pa yin no/ /de yang rdo rje rtse mo las/ thub pa'i ngo bo nyid sku las/ /slar yang longs spyod rdzogs par 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs pa
<p>109a.7</p>yin no/ /de ni 'og min du dbang phyug chen po'i gnas zho'i spri lta bur gyur pa snying bo byang chub tu mngon par byang chub pa bstan nas byang chub sems dpa' chen pos bcu pa rnams la chos kyi longs spyod par mdzad pa yin no/ /de yang ji skad du/ 'dod pa'i khams dang gzugs med du/ /
<p>109b</p>
<p>109b.1</p>sangs rgyas rnam par 'tshang mi rgya/ /gzugs kyi khams kyi 'og min du/ /'dod chags bral khyod 'tshang rgya'o/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /gzhan yang chos kyi sku dang / longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku ni byin gyi rlabs las byung ba sprul pa'i skus kyang 'dod pa'i khams
<p>109b.2</p>su sangs rgyas pa'i tshul gyis 'gro ba dang rjes su mthun par sku bstan pa yin no/ /de yang ji skad du/ gtsang ma'i gnas ni rnam spangs nas/ /'og min gnas ni nyams dga' bar/ /yang dag sangs rgyas der sangs rgyas/ /sgrub pa po dag 'dir sangs rgyas/ /
<p>109b.3</p>zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /sprul pa'i skus kyang 'khor ba ji srid ma stongs kyi bar du 'jig rten gyi khams mtha' yas par gdul bya rnams kyi mos pa dang / skal pa ji lta ba bzhin du sprul sku 'dra ba dang / mi 'dra ba dang / nges pa dang / ma nges pa dang / rtag pa dang / 
<p>109b.4</p>mi rtag pas don mdzad cing bzhugs pa yin no/ /de yang ji skad du rdo rje dra ba las/ gang dang gang gi gzugs kyis ni/ /mi rnams yid kyis 'jug 'gyur ba/ /de dang de yi gzugs kyis ni/ /sna tshogs nor bu ji bzhin no/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /de ltar na sku
<p>109b.5</p>gsum gyis lam thams cad kyi 'bras bur gyur pa bsdus pa yin te/ bdag dang gzhan gyi don phun sum tshogs pa'i rab kyi mthar thug pa'i phyir ro/ /de yang ji skad du/ lus dang ngag sems rnam dag pas/ /sku gsum du ni bstan pa yin/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /de
<p>109b.6</p>ltar bden pa gnyis kyi mtshan nyid shes shing 'bras bu sku gsum gyi spyi'i rang bzhin rtogs na de la mngon par 'dun cing de'i thob pa'i thabs la 'jug par 'gyur ro/ /de bas na de'i rgyur gyur pa ni sngags kyi lam rnam pa gnyis su 'dod de/ smin par byed pa'i lam dang / 
<p>109b.7</p>grol bar byed pa'i lam mo/ /smin par byed pa'i lam la yang bzhi ste/ bum pa'i dbang bskur ba dang / gsang ba'i dbang bskur ba dang / shes rab ye shes kyi dbang bskur ba dang / bzhi pa'i dbang bskur ba'o/ /de yang dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgyud phyi ma las/ dbang
<p>110a</p>
<p>110a.1</p>bskur ba la gsum du 'byed/ /bum pa'i dbang ni dang po ste/ /gsang ba'i dbang bskur gnyis pa yin/ /shes rab ye shes gsum pa ste/ /de ltar de bzhin bzhi pa yang / /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /yang na/ dbang bskur ba la gsum du 'byed/ /ces
<p>110a.2</p>gsungs pa'i dgongs pa ni bum pa'i dbang bskur ba'o/ /gsang ba'i dbang dang / shes rab ye shes te gsum yin no/ /de yang ji skad du/ bzhi brgya lnga bcu pa'i rnam par bshad pa las/ chu dang cod pan rdo rje bdag po dang / /ming zhes btags dang bum pa zhes bya ba/ /gsang
<p>110a.3</p>ba dang ni shes rab ye shes te/ /dbang bskur rnam pa gsum du shes par bya/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /de'i don 'di yin te/ byang chub tu sems bskyed cing dam tshig dang dbang bskur ba thob par ma gyur pas ni de kho na nyid 'ba' zhig tsam la 'bad cing phyin ci ma log par bsgrubs
<p>110a.4</p>kyang 'bras bu mchog 'dod pa bzhin du 'byung bar mi 'gyur ro/ /de yang ji skad du/ dkyil 'khor du ni ma zhugs shing / /dbang bskur thob par ma gyur dang / /gsang ba'i de nyid mi shes la/ /bsgrubs kyang ci yang mi 'grub bo/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /de ltar dbang bskur zhing
<p>110a.5</p>yongs su smin par byas kyang sgrub pa po grol bar byed pa byang chub kyi sems 'phel bar byed pa'i snod du ma gyur na 'dod pa bzhin du 'bras bu 'byung bar mi 'gyur ro/ /de bas na dad pa dang / brtson 'grus dang / thos pa dang / sbyin pa dang / sdom pa la sogs pa nges par bsten par
<p>110a.6</p>bya'o/ /de yang rdo rje rtse mo las/ byang chub sems bskyed gyur nas ni/ /lha gzhan la ni mi mos par/ /gsod dang rku dang 'khrig pa dang / /chang dang brdzun ni rnam par spangs/ /khyim pa'i tshul du gnas nas ni/ /rig sngags rgyal po bsgrub par bya/ /gal te de rab tu byung na/ /
<p>110a.7</p>sdom pa gsum la gnas par bya/ /so sor thar dang byang chub sems/ /rig 'dzin rang gi sdom pa'o/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / yang de nyid las/ byang chub sems ni ma bskyed cing / /gang gis bka' stsol mi nyan dang / /the tshom yod pa nyid dang ni/ /ma dad pas ni mi 'grub po/ /
<p>110b</p>
<p>110b.1</p>zhes gsungs pa dang / gzhan yang sgyu 'phrul dra ba las/ brtan zhing dul la blo gros ldan/ /bzod ldan drang la g.yo sgyu med/ /sngags dang rgyud kyi sbyor ba dang / /de nyid bcu ni yongs su shes/ /dkyil 'khor bri ba'i las la mkhas/ /'di ni slob dpon yin zhes bya/ /de yis
<p>110b.2</p>bstan pa'i gsang sngags rnams/ /'grub 'gyur 'di la the tshom med/ /ces gsungs pas na slob ma'ang yon tan de lta bu'am/ cung zad dman pas gsol ba btab na/ thar rgyal 'dod pas bstan par bya'i/ /gzhan du slob dpon slob ma dag /gnyis ka nyams pa nyid
<p>110b.3</p>du 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / gshin rje nag po'i rgyud las kyang / brtan zhing dul la snying rje gcig pu sems/ /dad ldan lhag pa'i bsam pas bzod pa 'dzin/ /slob ma bla ma la ni gus pa dang / /dad pas gshin rje gshed la gus pa dang / /brtul zhugs ldan
<p>110b.4</p>zhing yongs su smin pa yin/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /de lta bas na lung dang man ngag ji lta ba bzhin du bsgrub par bya ba'i don la the tshom rnam par bsal te 'jug par bya ba'i sgra ji bzhin pa la brten nas rang dgar gyur pas srog gcod pa la sogs pa bsten pas ni 'bras bu
<p>110b.5</p>mtho ris kyang 'byung bar mi 'gyur na thar pa lta smos kyang ci dgos te/ bdag dang gzhan la phan par 'dod pa rnams kyis lung gi don la gus pa tsam gyis 'jug par mi bya'o/ /de yang bcom ldan 'das kyis dgongs pa lung bstan pa las/ gsang ba'i bdag po don rgyas pa'i/ /
<p>110b.6</p>tshul chen 'di ni rnyed gyur nas/ /ji bzhin don ni rnyed bzung na/ /des na lam ngan dag tu ltung / /zhes gsungs pa dang / yang de nyid las/ gang gis phung stsogs dngos med par/ /zhi gnas las byung sems kyis bya/ /de ni srog gcod bya ba ste/ /theg pa mchog la gnas
<p>110b.7</p>pa yin/ /nang dang de bzhin phyi rol dag /brten 'byung gnyis su ston pa yin/ /de ni brdzun smra dga' ba ste/ /gnas med la gnas rnal 'byor pa'o/ /rdzogs sangs rgyas kyi ye shes gang / /de ni rdzas su shes bya ste/ /de 'phrog dang tshul gang yin pa/ /gzhan gyi nor la chags
<p>111a</p>
<p>111a.1</p>par 'dod/ /de bzhin nyid la rtag sbyor ba/ /sems can de ni 'dod la dga'/ /sgrub pa mchog la dam par 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / dpal 'khor lo sdom pa las kyang / 'khar sil chos gos lhung bzed dang / /chu tshags sbyangs pa'i yon
<p>111a.2</p>tan gyis/ /yan lag lung bzhin mi spong ste/ /lung ma rtogs par rnal 'byor par/ /sangs rgyas mu stegs can du 'gyur/ /zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs pa dang / mngon par byang chub pa'i rgyud las/ rdo rje theg par khas 'che zhing / /mnyam pa'i don nyid mi shes par/ /
<p>111a.3</p>gsang sngags dam tshig mnyam zer zhing / /thug thub dag tu spyad byas na/ /dmyal khams dag tu brgyud par 'gyur/ /zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs pa yin no/ /de lta bas na dam tshig dang dbang bskur ba thob cing / snying rje chen pos rgyud brlan pa/ /mchog gi byang chub kyi
<p>111a.4</p>sems la gnas shing / drang ba dang nges pa'i don gyi bye brag shes pa/ de kho na'i don la brtson 'grus 'bar ba dang ldan pa rnams ni theg pa chen po 'di'i snod yin no/ /de yang ji skad du/ dgos pa sgrub la mkhas rnams sran thub pas/ /dka' ba rnams kyang dga' ba med par
<p>111a.5</p>dga'/ /zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o/ /de ltar yongs su smin cing snod du gyur pas ni grol lam ste rnal 'byor la mngon par brtson par bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin gyi gegs su gyur pa rnam par g.yeng ba sna tshogs bdud kyi spyod yul gyis yid mgu ba rnams kyis ni tshogs pa tsam
<p>111a.6</p>bsags par 'gyur gyis mchog gi dngos grub la sogs pa'i 'bras bu 'dod pa bzhin du 'byung bar mi 'gyur ro/ /de yang bzhi brgya lnga bcu pa las/ thos pa tsam gyis sangs mi rgya/ /'jug tsam gyis kyang ma yin te/ /ji srid bsams par gyur pa dang / /bsgom pa nyid kyis
<p>111a.7</p>'gag par 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / gzhan yang / de ltar rtogs pa'i snying rjer ldan pa'i bdag /ye shes bsam yas skad cig gis bsgrubs pa/ /dpal ldan kun du bzang po'i rang bzhin gyi/ /ngo bo su zhig nges par sgom mi byed/ /ces gsungs pa yin no/ /
<p>111b</p>
<p>111b.1</p>sdong po brgyan pa las kyang / yang dag sangs rgyas bstan pa 'di/ /thos pa tsam gyis mi 'grub po/ /la la stobs med chu klung gis/ /nan gyis khyer bar gyur pa dag /sgom zhing shi bar gyur pa bzhin/ /ma bsgoms chos kyang de bzhin no/ /ji ltar 'gro ba mang
<p>111b.2</p>po la/ /zas dang skom dag byin byas kyang / /bdag nyid bkres pas shi ba ltar/ /de bzhin chos la ma bsgoms pa'o/ /ji ltar sman pa la la zhig /sman rnams tha dad gtong bzhin du/ /lto yi nad kyis shi ba bzhin/ /chos la ma bsgoms de bzhin no/ /ji
<p>111b.3</p>ltar dbyig gi mdzod dag tu/ /rin chen mang po bgrang byed kyang / /nam phyed tsam yang mi 'thob pa/ /chos la ma bsgoms de bzhin no/ /ji ltar bde ba kun ldan pa'i/ /rgyal po'i pho brang 'khor skyes kyang / /zas dang skom dag mi bdog pa/ /de bzhin
<p>111b.4</p>chos la ma bsgoms pa'o/ /ji ltar 'on pa rol mo yi/ /sil snyan sgra la mkhas pa zhig /gzhan dag de yis dga' byed pa/ /chos la ma bsgoms de bzhin no/ /ji ltar dmus long ri mo mkhan/ /tshong 'dus dbus su 'drir bcug kyang / /bdag nyid kyis ni mi
<p>111b.5</p>mthong ba/ /ma bsgoms chos kyang de bzhin no/ /ji ltar mtsho chen mnyen pa zhig /skye bo mang po sgrol byed kyang / /bdag nyid de yi nang 'chi ba/ /chos la ma bsgoms de bzhin no/ /zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs pa dang / snang ba'i phreng ba las kyang / rtag tu brtson
<p>111b.6</p>'grus ldan pa yis/ /'di ltar lam gyi rjes 'jug na/ /ring por mi thogs chos kun ni/ /stong pa nyid du rtogs par 'gyur/ /chos kyi chos nyid thob pa'i phyir/ /yongs su ma bsgoms pas mi 'gyur/ /chu ma 'thungs par thos pa dang / /mthong bas skam pa sel
<p>111b.7</p>'gyur ram/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /de la grol ba'i lam la yang gnyis te/ bskyed pa dang rdzogs pa'i rim pa'o/ /de yang gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgyud phyi ma las/ sangs rgyas rnams kyis chos bstan pa/ /rim pa gnyis la yang dag gnas/ /bskyed pa yi ni
<p>112a</p>
<p>112a.1</p>rim pa dang / /rdzogs pa'i rim pa nyid yin no/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /de dag kyang sgrub pa po rnams kyi rnal 'byor gyi bye brag gis rim gyis gong nas gong du sems sbyang bar bya'i cig car ni ma yin no/ /de la shes rab kyi rgyud kyi man ngag gi rim
<p>112a.2</p>pa ni sngon gyi slob dpon du ma'i dgongs pa tha dad par 'dod do/ /de yang slob dpon kha cig gis ni 'di skad du bskyed pa'i rim pa dang / rang la byin gyis brlabs pa'i rim pa dang / bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rim pa zhes bya ba gsum du gzhag pa yin no/ /kha cig gis ni
<p>112a.3</p>rgyud kyi rim pa zhes bya ba la sogs pa'am/ rnam pa gzhan du 'dod pa yin no/ /rnal 'byor thabs kyi rgyud kyi rim pa la yang sngon gyi slob dpon du ma'i man ngag gi rim pa tha dad pa gsungs so/ /de yang kha cig gis ni sangs rgyas kyi theg pa la bslab pa dang / 
<p>112a.4</p>theg pa gsar la dran pa gcig pa'i ting nge 'dzin dang / rtog pa'i rnal 'byor dang / lus rnam par dben pa dang / ngag rnam par dben pa dang / sems rnam par dben pa dang / kun rdzob kyi bden pa dang / don dam pa'i bden pa dang / zung du 'jug pa'i rim pa ste rnam pa
<p>112a.5</p>dgur gsungs pa yin no/ /gzhan dag gis ni las dang po pa dang ye shes cung zad dbang ba zhes bya ba la sogs pas bskyed pa dang / rdzogs pa'i rim pa rnam pa gzhan du gsungs pa yin no/ /kha cig gi ni rim pa bzhi la sogs pa rnam pa du mar gsungs te/ rim gyis
<p>112a.6</p>bslab par bzhed pa yin no/ /de yang snang ba'i phreng ba las/ sems can dang po'i las can rnams/ /dam pa'i don la 'jug pa'i phyir/ /thabs 'di rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyis/ /skas kyi rim pa du mar gsungs/ /zhes bshad pa yin no/ /de ltar sgrub pa la gnas pa
<p>112a.7</p>de dag kyang yang dag pa'i lta ba ste/ phyin ci ma log pa'i blo sngon du 'gro bar bya'o/ /de yang ji skad du lha mo bzhis zhus pa las/ bskal pa bye ba brgyar yang ni/ /de nyid bral bas 'grub mi 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /de la lta ba ni sngar yul bshad pa'i skabs su
<p>112b</p>
<p>112b.1</p>bden pa gnyis mdor bstan pa yin no/ /lhag ma ni man ngag las ji lta ba bzhin du khong du chud par byed de/ phyag rgya chen po'i dngos grub kyi rgyu'i gtso bo yin pa'i phyir ro/ /de yang de kho na nyid bsdus pa las/ lta ba ngan cing chags med la/ /gsang ba 'di ni mi rigs so/ /
<p>112b.2</p>zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /de dag kyang brtul zhugs kyi rang bzhin sngags kyi spyod pa dang ldan pa de kho na nyid mthong zhing 'dod pa bzhin du dngos grub mchog tu 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /de yang ji skad du/ mngon par byang chub pa las/ tshul khrims zin pa'i lta spyod rnam
<p>112b.3</p>gnyis ni/ /lag mthil bsnyal nas 'dag pa ji bzhin du/ /gcig gis gcig dag zin pa rnam gnyis dang / /ldan na byang chub 'thob par rgyal bas gsungs/ /spyod pa lta bral 'dam gyi glang chen 'dra/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / gzhan yang gsang ba 'dus pa
<p>112b.4</p>las/ sngags kyi spyod mchog spyod pa rnams/ /chos kyi yi ge mchog brnyes so/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /de sngags kyi spyod pa ni mdor bsdu na rnam pa gnyis te/ kun du spyod pa dang sngags kyi spyod pa'o/ /de yang bla ma'i lung las shes par bya ba'i spyod pa'i dbye ba rnam
<p>112b.5</p>pa du ma'i gzhung snang bas 'dir bsdu ba ma byas pa yin no/ /de yang / spros bcas la sogs spyod pa yis/ /rnal 'byor pa ni 'dir slob bo/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /gzhan yang spyod pa dang rjes su 'brel pa'i dam tshig dang / sdom pa dag kyang lhag pa'i tshul khrims
<p>112b.6</p>yin pas dngos grub thams cad kyi yan lag tu gyur pa yin no/ /de ni sdom pa'i tshul khrims dang / dge ba chos sdud pa'i tshul khrims dang / sems can gyi don byed pa'i tshul khrims dang rnam pa gsum du 'dus pa yin no/ /de yang ji skad du/ tshul khrims kyi ni bslab pa dang / /
<p>112b.7</p>dge ba'i chos ni sdud pa dang / /sems can don byed tshul khrims gsum/ /bdag gis brtan por gzung bar bya/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /de dag kyang thog mar nyes pa 'byung ba'i gzhi dang / nyes pa lci ba dang / yang ba'i bye brag dang / nyes pa phyir bcos pa'i thabs
<p>113a</p>
<p>113a.1</p>la mkhas pa chen po dang / 'bring dang / chung ngu'i dbye bas shes bzhin dang ldan pas bsrung ba la mngon par brtson par bya'o/ /de yang dpal 'khor lo sdom pa las/ shin tu mnyam gzhag sgrub pa pos/ /rtag tu dam tshig bskyang bar bya/ /dam tshig
<p>113a.2</p>nyams pas dkyil 'khor du/ /dbang bskur dngos grub thob mi 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /de yang sngar snod du rung bar bya ba'i phyir skabs su gnang ba dang / bkag pa'i dgongs pa dang bcas par bshad pa yin no/ /de la dam tshig ni mdor bsdu na chags pa rnam pa
<p>113a.3</p>gsum ste/ dad pas lha la chags pa dang / gus pas slob dpon la chags pa dang / snying rjes sems can la chags pa yin no/ /de yang lha'i rnal 'byor ni rnam pa gnyis te/ zab pa dang rgya che ba'i skur grags pa yin no/ /de la zab pa ste spros pa'i mtha' thams cad spangs
<p>113a.4</p>pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyis ni de kho na'i don phyin ci ma log par myur du 'dod pa bzhin du mthong bar 'gyur gyis gzhan du ni ma yin no/ /de yang thams cad gsang ba'i rgyud las/ 'bras bu rgyus ni rgyas btab cing / /rgyu yang 'bras bus rgyas btab par/ /sgom gyi gzhan na dngos grub ni/ /
<p>113a.5</p>bskal pa bye bar 'byung mi 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / rtog pa kun las btus pa las kyang / dag pa'i sems ni bzung gyur nas/ /rdo rje'i lus ni rnam bsgoms pas/ /brtan lus khong stong ma yin pas/ /rdo rje'i sku ni nges thob 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / byang chub kyi
<p>113a.6</p>sems bshad pa las/ gang gis stong nyid mi shes pa/ /de yis thar pa'i skal can min/ /rmongs pa de ni 'gro drug gi / srid pa'i btson ra 'dir 'khyam 'gyur/ /zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs pa yin no/ /de la rgya che bsgoms pas ni tha mal pa'i 'du shes 'gog par
<p>113a.7</p>'gyur zhing / rnam par grol ba dang rjes su mthun par byin gyis brlabs pa yin no/ /de yang kun du bzang po sgrub pa'i thabs las/ tha mal rnam rtog rgyun las gzhan pa yi/ /srid pa'i sdug bsngal gzhan dag yod ma yin/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / dpal gsang ba 'dus pa
<p>113b</p>
<p>113b.1</p>las kyang / sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje rnams/ /lus dang ngag sems bsgom pa ni/ /byang chub thams cad thob pa'i phyir/ /ye shes rdo rje dag gis bya/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / yang de nyid las/ mdor na phung po lnga rnams ni/ /sangs rgyas lngar ni rab tu
<p>113b.2</p>grags/ /rdo rje skye mched nyid dag ni/ /byang chub sems dpa'i dkyil 'khor mchog /sa ni spyan zhes bya bar grags/ /chu yi khams ni mA ma kI/ gos dkar ma dang sgrol ma ni/ /me dang rlung zhes bya bar grags/ /gzugs sgra la sogs sngags pa yis/ /lha
<p>113b.3</p>nyid du ni rnam par bsgom/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / dpal sangs rgyas thams cad dang mnyam par sbyor ba las kyang / bdag nyid sangs rgyas thams cad dang / /dpa' bo thams cad bdag yin no/ /de bas bdag nyid lhar sbyor bas/ /bdag nyid rab tu bsgrub
<p>113b.4</p>par bya/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / dgyes pa'i rdo rje las kyang / tha mal rnam rtog gnyen po'i tshul/ /sangs rgyas skur ni yongs brtags pa/ /lha yi skur ni goms byas na/ /des ni sna tshogs rgya chen 'grub/ /ces gsungs pa dang / dpa' bo gcig tu grub pa
<p>113b.5</p>las kyang / lha nyid gsang sngags tshul du ni/ /dngos grub thams cad stsol mdzad pas/ /sngags pa lha nyid bsgoms nas ni/ /de grub na ni de 'grub 'gyur/ /rim pa 'di yis 'di la ni/ /sa la sogs pa 'thob bo kye/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / gzhan yang / rdo rje
<p>113b.6</p>sems dpa' la sogs pa/ /lha rnams mngon du mthong ba las/ /bsod nams rtag pa ji lta ba/ /phyis byas pa yang de bzhin no/ /zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs pa yin no/ /de la gus pas slob dpon la chags par bya ba ni skyabs gsum yongs su gzung
<p>113b.7</p>ba'i rtsa ba yin te/ dngos grub thams cad ni gnas skabs gsum du/ slob dpon la rag las par gyur pa'i phyir ro/ /de yang ye shes grub pa las/ bla ma sangs rgyas chos gyur cing / dge 'dun yang ni de nyid de/ /'di la drin gyis shes gyur pas/ /de bas dkon mchog
<p>114a</p>
<p>114a.1</p>gsum yin no/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / gzhan yang sgyu 'phrul dra ba las/ /slob dpon ci 'dra bar lta zhe na/ bla ma sangs rgyas kun dang mnyam/ /de bas rtag tu rdo rje 'chang / /de bzhin gshegs pa rin chen tog /de ni ye shes rgya mtsho che/ /yid bzhin
<p>114a.2</p>nor bu rin chen sbyin/ /slob dpon gyi ni yon tan bzung / /skyon rnams nam yang ma yin no/ /yon tan gyis ni dngos grub cing / /skyon rnams kyis ni dngos grub nyams/ /de phyir kun nas rab bsgrims te/ /bsam yas 'bras bu smin byed pa/ /sangs rgyas 'bras bu
<p>114a.3</p>'dod pa yis/ /sems can dad pas de mchod cing / /zhes gsungs pa dang / gzhan yang rgyud thams cad kyi dgongs pa bsdus pa bla ma lnga bcu pa la sogs par gsungs pa yin no/ /de la snying rjes sems can la chags par bya ba ni theg pa chen po'i don la zhugs pa
<p>114a.4</p>rnams kyis thabs kyi mchog tu gsungs pa yin no/ /de yang mngon par byang chub pa las snying rje ni rtsa ba yin no zhes gsungs pa dang / gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgyud phyi ma las/ thabs ni byang chub sems dpa' yi/ /'gro la snying rje chen po ste/ /de yang dmigs pa'i bye brag gis/ /
<p>114a.5</p>rnam pa gsum du bshad pa yin/ /zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs pa yin no/ /de ltar bcom ldan 'das kyi gsung thams cad ni gdul bya'i dbang po mos pa dang skal ba tha dad pa la dgongs nas thugs rje chen pos gsungs pa yin no/ /de yang ji skad du/ bsam pa gang dang gang gis
<p>114a.6</p>ni/ /mi rnams yid ni yang dag sbyor/ /des ni de yi rang bzhin 'gyur/ /sna tshogs nor bu ji bzhin no/ /zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o/ /de la dbang po dman pa'i don du ni mngon par mtho ba'i theg pa dang nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi sde snod gsungs pa yin no/ /de yang / nyan thos rnams ni
<p>114a.7</p>'jug pa'i phyir/ /sdug bsngal stsogs bden nyid gsungs pa/ /med du zin kyang thugs rje yis/ /bdag yod ces gsungs lta bu yin/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /dbang po 'bring gi don du pha rol tu phyin pa'i theg pa'i sde snod gsungs pa yin no/ /de yang ji skad du/ thub pa chen
<p>114b</p>
<p>114b.1</p>po'i chos rnams kyi/ /phung po brgyad khri bzhi stong la/ /gang gis de nyid mi shes pa/ /de yi thams cad 'bras bu med/ /ces gsungs pa lta bu'o/ /de la dbang po rnon po'i mos pa dang skal ba dang ldan pa rnams kyi phyir ni gsang sngags kyi theg pa'i sde snod gsungs pa yin no/ /
<p>114b.2</p>de yang bya ba'i rgyud la sogs pa dang po gsum gyis rnal 'byor pa'i sems sbyangs shing de kho na mthong bar 'gyur ba dang 'brel pa'i tshogs yongs su bsags nas gong nas gong du lam sbyangs te/ rnal 'byor bla na med pa'i rim pas de kho na'i don la 'jug par 'gyur ba yin no/ /de
<p>114b.3</p>yang ji skad du/ yul dus la sogs bstan pa ni/ /mun du bsgribs pa rnam 'khod pas/ /de dag nges par gzung ba'i phyir/ /cho ga 'di ni bstan pa yin/ /zhes bstan pa yin no/ /de la rnal 'byor bla na med pa'i rgyud kyi rim pa'i smin pa dang / grol bar byed pa'i lam gyis ni
<p>114b.4</p>dka' ba med par myur du 'bras bu 'dod pa bzhin 'grub par 'gyur ro/ /de nyid tshigs su bcad pa ni/ /rigs dang brtul zhugs skye gnas yan lag ris/ /las dang nyon mongs yul dus 'ching ba med/ /ces bya ba yin no/ /de yang dpal gsang ba 'dus pa las/ mtshams
<p>114b.5</p>med pa la sogs pa yi/ /sdig pa chen po byed pa yang / /theg pa bla na med pa yi/ /theg mchog 'di la 'grub par 'gyur/ /zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs pa yin no/ /de lta bas na rnal 'byor pa snod du gyur cing de kho na nyid kyi man ngag dang ldan pa rnams la ni rig pa'i gnas
<p>114b.6</p>lnga la yongs su sbyang ba ma byas kyang dngos grub rnam pa gnyis ji ltar 'dod pa bzhin du 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /de yang ji skad du/ gsang sngags smra rnams mang du ni/ /spros te smra bas ci zhig bya/ /khyad par du ni sems bsgrubs te/ /sems las rdzogs pa'i byang chub 'byung / /zhes
<p>114b.7</p>gsungs pa dang / gzhan yang / gang zag ji tsam yon tan chung bas kyang / /lhag pa'i bsam pas bskul nas byang chub 'thob/ /ces gsungs pa dang / nyal lam yang na 'dug pa'am/ /'chag pa'am yang na ci dgar gnas/ /dgod pa'am rab tu smra ba'am/ /gang dang
<p>115a</p>
<p>115a.1</p>gang du ji ltar gnas/ /rang lhar sbyor ba'i bdag nyid can/ /bsod nams chung yang 'grub par 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / bsod nams chung ba'ang sangs rgyas mchod/ /bsgrubs na dngos grub thob par 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /kye ma'o/ /
<p>115a.2</p>bde bar gshegs pa mya ngan 'das nas ring zhig lon/ /rgyal sras dam chos 'dzin pa rnams kyang dus kyis mi snang 'gyur/ /snyigs ma'i dus kyi tha mar gyur pas sde snod phal cher nub/ /des na dman pa'i 'jig rten 'di ni skyabs med dmus long bzhin/ /dmyal ba lta bur
<p>115a.3</p>sdug bsngal gyur kyang 'khrul pas bde bar 'dzin/ /yi dgas lta bur 'byor pas phongs kyang phun sum tshogs par sems/ /dud 'gro lta bur rmongs par 'gyur kyang blo yis mngon par dregs/ /lus srog rlung bzhin g.yo bar mthong yang 'chi ba'i 'jigs pa med/ /de ltar bstan
<p>115a.4</p>pa nyam chung 'khrul zhing mi lus thob pa'i tshe/ /dka' ba'i dus su phrad pas bsgrubs na 'bras bu mchog tu 'gyur/ /'gro kun bde gshegs snying po yod pas bdag gzhan phan pa'i phyir/ /don la brten nas dus dang sbyar te sgrub la brtson par bya'o/ /zab cing rgya che'i rang bzhin
<p>115a.5</p>theg pa mchog don la/ /mos pa yod kyang rmongs sdig mi dge'i grogs bcas kyis/ /spang dang blang ba'i rang bzhin mngon par mi rtogs pas/ /dang po'i las can rnams la rnam bsdus don du 'gyur/ /gang dag dbang po dman zhing thos pas phongs pa dang / /rnal 'byor don
<p>115a.6</p>la brtson pas rgyas bshad yul min dang / /mi shes log par rtog dang the tshom bzlog pa'i phyir/ /mdor bsdus 'di ni bdag gis dri med lung bzhin bris/ /rnal 'byor bla na med pa'i rgyud kyi don la 'jug pa bsdus pa slob dpon shrad+d+hA ka ra warmas mdzad pa rdzogs so// // 
<p>115a.7</p>rgya gar mkhan po shrad+d+hA ka ra wa rma dang / lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//[ ]@##//rdo rje theg pa'i mtha' gnyis sel ba bzhugs/ @##/ /sangs rgyas la phyag 'tshal lo/ /theg mchog rdo rje'i theg pa la/ /sgro 'dogs pa dang skur pa yi/ /mtha'
<p>115b</p>
<p>115b.1</p>gnyis rnam par spang ba'i phyir/ /gsang ba'i grub mtha' dbye bar bya/ /dang por re zhig lung gi gsang sngags kyi theg pa thub pa'i bka' nyid du bstan te/ 'phags pa yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa las/ bstan bcos sam rig sngags sam/ gsang sngags gang ci yang
<p>115b.2</p>rung ba de dag thams cad ni rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyis gsungs pa yin par shes par gyis shig ces gsungs so/ /yang 'phags pa gsang ba lung bstan pa'i mdo las/ rgyu la sbyor ba rgyu yi chos/ /'khor lo shin tu bskor byas nas/ /'bras bu'i theg pa nye
<p>115b.3</p>lam zhig /ma 'ongs pa na 'byung bar 'gyur/ /zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs so/ /de bzhin du 'phags pa lhag pa'i bsam pa bskul ba'i mdo las kyang / byang chub sems dpa' drug cu ma 'ongs pa'i dus na bstan dang gsang sngags la mkhas pa 'byung bar
<p>115b.4</p>'gyur bar lung bstan te/ de bas na thun mong gi lung nyid las gsang sngags kyi theg pa sangs rgyas kyi bka' nyid du grub bo/ /rigs pas kyang grub ste/ bden pa rnam pa gnyis la gnas shing bdag dang gzhan gyi don bsgrub pa'i phyir ro/ /da ni gsang sngags kyi che ba nyid
<p>115b.5</p>brjod pa'i mtshan bstan te/ dbyer med pa dang / 'bras bu nyid lam du gyur pa dang / thabs kyi che ba nyid dang / shin tu gsang bar bya ba'i phyir rdo rje'i theg pa dang / 'bras bu'i theg pa dang / thabs kyi theg pa dang / gsang ba'i theg pa zhes bya'o/ /de dag kyang thabs kyi
<p>115b.6</p>theg pa nyid las byung ba'i/ /de ni thabs kyi che ba zhes bya ba de nyid la bstan te/ gsang sngags kyi theg pa 'di pha rol tu phyin pa'i theg pa chen po dbu ma las kyang khyad par ci yod pa bstan te/ dmigs pa bla na med pa la dmigs pa'i thabs dang / sgrub pa bla na med pa dang / ye
<p>115b.7</p>shes bla na med pa dang / brtson 'grus bla na med pa dang / gdul bya ma lus pa 'dzin par nus pa dang / nyon mongs pa byin gyis rlob pa dang / byin gyis rlob pa myur ba dang / myur du 'byung ba dang / nyon mongs pa spong ba dang / bsam pa bla na med pa dang / spyod pa bla na med pa'i thabs
<p>116a</p>
<p>116a.1</p>mkhas pa ste/ de ltar thabs mkhas pa nyid rnam pa bcu gcig gis khyad par du 'phags so/ /de la ji ltar na dmigs pa bla na med pa la dmigs pa'i thabs mkhas pa yin zhe na/ lam der ni 'phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'bum pa dang / sdong
<p>116a.2</p>po bkod pa la sogs pa dmigs pa yin la/ lam 'dir ni de dag tu ma grags pa dpal dgyes pa'i rdo rje 'bum phrag lnga pa dang / dpal gshin rje dgra nag po 'bum nyi khri lnga stong pa dang / dpal nam mkha' dang mnyam pa 'bum pa la sogs pa thun mong ma yin pa'i
<p>116a.3</p>dmigs pa la dmigs pa'i phyir ro/ /sgrub pa bla na med pa ni lam der lus kyi bkod pa thos nas mngon sum ma yin pa'i don byed nus pa ltar 'dir ni der ma thob par ting nge 'dzin thob pas mngon sum ma yin pa'i don byed par nus pa'o/ /sems gnas par byed pa'i ting nge
<p>116a.4</p>'dzin khyad par can la brten pas/ rgyu dang ngo bo nyid dang / las dag las ye shes kyi rgyu myur ba nyid bla na med pa'o/ /dam tshig gi dbang gis brtson 'grus chen po rang dbang med par brtsam pas brtson 'grus bla na med pa'o/ /rigs ngan sme sha can la sogs/ /gsod pa don
<p>116a.5</p>du gnyer ba yang / /zhes bya ba la sogs pas gdul bya theg pa gzhan las spangs pa yang 'dir snang bas na gdul bya ma lus pa 'dzin par nus pa'o/ /lha'i kha dog dbyibs kyi dam tshig dang thams cad yul khyad par can du byas pas nyon mongs pa rang bzhin gyis spong
<p>116a.6</p>bas nyon mongs pa spong ba bla na med pa'o/ /mchod pa'i rang bzhin dang bde ba la brten pa'i rdzogs pa'i rim pas nyon mongs pa byin gyis rlob pa'o/ /lam der/ de bzhin gshegs pas dbang bskur ba/ /sa la zhugs nas thob par 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs pa lta bu ma yin gyis/ 
<p>116a.7</p>thabs mkhas pa la brten pas da lta nyid du nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams byin gyis rlob pas na byin gyis rlob pa myur ba'o/ /snga ma dang phyi ma'i khyad par la gnas pa de ni ches myur bar 'khor ba las 'byung bas na myur du 'byung ba ste/ dpal mchog dang po dang gsang ba'i
<p>116b</p>
<p>116b.1</p>mdzod las ji skad gsungs pa/ byang chub sems dpa' tshe bcu drug gis de bzhin gshegs pa'am rdo rje 'chang ba'i dngos grub thob po zhes pa dang / de yis skye ba bdun la ni/ /ma bsgrubs par ni dngos grub 'thob/ /ces so/ /yang gzhan las/ sangs rgyas tshe gcig gis
<p>116b.2</p>'thob bo/ /la sogs pa gsungs pa'o/ /bsam pa bla na med pa ni/ /sku gsung thugs la sbyor ba ste/ /de yang sku la sbyar bas ni yon tan bzhi bskyed de/ tha mal pa'i spros pa'i bag chags myur du ldog pa dang / las kyi rnam par smin pa myur du 'dod pa dang / bsod nams kyi tshogs chen po
<p>116b.3</p>skye ba dang / chos bdag med pa la rang bzhin gyis 'jug pa'o/ /de yang ji ltar zhe na/ tha mal pa'i rtog pa bzlog ste sangs rgyas kyi sku la gnas pas thog ma med pa'i dus can gyi lus dang ming dang rigs la sogs pa'i rtog pa myur du ldog pa'o/ /lha'i sku de ni zhi gnas dang lhag
<p>116b.4</p>mthong du 'brel pa'i lam gyi mchog yin la/ ting nge 'dzin de gnyis thob na sngon gyi las kyi 'bras bu myur du ldog pa ste/ ji skad du rnam par snang mdzad mngon par byang chub pa las/ rnam par smin pa 'dir smin pa/ /las rnams kyi ni 'bras bu thob/ /gang gi tshe na grub pa thob/ /
<p>116b.5</p>de yi tshe na las rnams bzlog /sems ni rang dngos med phyir dang / /'bras bu rgyu rnams spangs pa'i phyir/ /las kyi skye ba rnams las thar/ /skye ba nam mkha' lta bu yin/ /zhes gsungs so/ /sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa dang / sangs rgyas la shes nas dad par 'gyur ba dang / 
<p>116b.6</p>longs spyod rnams rtag tu mngon par 'gyur bas bsod nams kyi tshogs chen po skye ba'o/ /lha'i sku bsgom pa mngon du gyur pa na chos thams cad rang gi sems snang ba tsam du shes par 'gyur ba la/ yang sems de yang ma grub par shes pa 'byung ba'i phyir dang / gzhan yang
<p>116b.7</p>bsod nams dang ldan pa'i sems kyi rgyud la ye shes skye bas na bsod nams nyid ye shes kyi rgyu lta bur gnas pa ste/ ji skad du 'phags pa rgya cher rol pa las/ bcom ldan 'das byang chub chen po brnyes nas gsungs pa/ bsod nams ldan pa'i mi yis bsam pa rnams kyang
<p>117a</p>
<p>117a.1</p>'grub/ /ces pa la sogs pa bsod nams nyid sangs rgyas pa'i rgyur bsngags pa'o/ /de bas lha'i bsgom pa de/ chos bdag med pa'i don la rang bzhin gyis 'jug par byed do/ /gsung la sbyar bas ni yon tan bcu gnyis skyed de/ rgyal ba'i bka' dam
<p>117a.2</p>pa bton par 'gyur ba dang / chos rjes su dran par 'gyur ba dang / chos la shes nas dad par 'gyur ba dang / ngag bden pa'i tshig 'grub pa dang / shes rab dang ldan pa'i thabs dang ye shes dang dran pa thob pa dang / ting nge 'dzin rtse gcig pa 'thob pa dang / 'phags pa
<p>117a.3</p>mchod par 'gyur ba dang / 'gro ba'i don byas par 'gyur ba dang / lha nye zhing grub pa myur bar 'gyur ba dang / chos thams cad yi ge'i sgyu 'phrul du dbang sgyur bar 'gyur ba dang / sgra thams cad brag ca dang 'dra ba'i shes pa skye ba dang / chos bdag med pa la rang bzhin gyis 'jug
<p>117a.4</p>par 'gyur ba'o/ /de yang ji ltar zhe na/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsang ba'i snying po'i 'bru gcig pa zhig lan cig bton pas zab cing rgya che ba'i mdo sde dag bton pas kyang bskrun du med pa'i yon tan 'thob pas na bka' dam pa bton pa'i yon tan yod do/ /gsang sngags
<p>117a.5</p>kyi mthu yang dang yang du dran par 'gyur ba dang / de'i mthu la yid ches shing dang ba'i dad pa 'byung bas na chos rjes su dran pa dang / chos la shes nas dad par 'gyur ba'o/ /bzlas pa grub pa'i gsang sngags kyi tshig las su yang mi 'da' bas na/ ngag bden pa'i tshig grub pa'o/ /
<p>117a.6</p>gsang sngags dang rig sngags dang gzungs sngags dag gi mthu ni shes rab dang thabs dang / shes rab dang ye shes dang / shes rab dang dran pa thob par byed pas na yon tan de gsum thob pa'o/ /de yang lha pho'i ni gsang sngags/ mo'i ni rig sngags/ sngags gcig nyid lha pho mo
<p>117a.7</p>gnyi ga'i sngags su 'gyur ba ni gzungs sngags so/ /yang sngags gcig nyid la de gsum char tshang ba dang / lha gcig nyid la sngags de gsum char tshang ba yang yod la/ rig sngags dang gzungs sngags gnyi ga lha mor gzhag pa yang yod pas thams cad du ni gcig
<p>117b</p>
<p>117b.1</p>tu ma nges so/ /bzlas pa'i sngags kyi rnam par rtog pa'i rnam pa blo la snang ba rtse gcig pa de rdo rje bzlas pa la sogs pas thob pa/ de thob pa ni ting nge 'dzin rtse gcig pa yin pas na/ yon tan de thob bo/ gsung yig 'bru las 'od zer 'phros pas mchod par gyur pa des
<p>117b.2</p>'phags pa mchod pa dang / 'gro ba'i don ci rigs su byed pas na yon tan de gnyis 'grub po/ /spro bsdu dang bzlas pa'i mthus sgrib pa byang zhing sgrib pa byang ba na nye bar bya ba nye zhing bsgrub par bya ba 'grub pas na lha nye zhing grub pa myur ba'i yon tan 'thob bo/ /gsung yig
<p>117b.3</p>'bru la dmigs pa thob pa ni snang ba thams cad yi ge'i rang bzhin du mthong ba dang / yi ge'i sgyu 'phrul ston par nus pas na chos thams cad yi ge'i sgyu 'phrul du dbang sgyur bar nus pa'i yon tan 'thob bo/ /bzlas pa byed pa'i dam tshig ni sgra nyid brag ca lta bur shes par bya
<p>117b.4</p>ba yin pas na rang bzhin gyis 'dris pa'i dbang las sgra thams cad brag ca ltar shes pa'i yon tan 'grub bo/ /bzlas pa'i dmigs pa thob pa na chos thams cad rang gi sems snang ba tsam du shes par 'gyur la/ sems de yang rang bzhin med par shes par 'gyur ba'i
<p>117b.5</p>phyir dang / snying po 'di lan cig brjod pas kyang sdig pa thams cad nges par bsreg go zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs pas na/ bzlas pa ni sgrib pa zad par byed la/ de zad pa na de'i sems la rang bzhin gyis ye shes skye ba ste/ de bas na bdag med pa'i don la rang
<p>117b.6</p>bzhin gyis 'jug pa'i yon tan 'grub po/ /thugs la gnas pas ni yon tan thams cad bskyed pa ste/ de yang sngags pa dag gi thugs la sbyor ba ni/ dus dang gnas skabs thams cad du chos thams cad sgyu ma dang 'dra bar blta ba dang / mi 'bral bar gnas pa yin te/ 
<p>117b.7</p>ji skad du gsungs pa/ mang du smra ba ni 'dir ci dgos/ rdo rje theg pa'i de nyid ni/ /rnal 'byor pa yis gang gang dmigs/ /de dang der ni sgyu mar blta/ /zhes so/ /de ltar kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba'i chos thams cad la sgyu ma dang 'dra bar blta ba dang / ma bral bas
<p>118a</p>
<p>118a.1</p>nyon mongs pa tshegs med par spong ba dang / dge ba la rlom sems la sogs pa 'dor la/ de nyid kyis de'i 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i phun sum tshogs pa ma lus pa thob pas na thugs la gnas pa'i yon tan de 'thob bo/ /de lta na/ de nyid dbu ma
<p>118a.2</p>dag kyang 'dod pa nyid/ /bdag ni mnyam par gzhag ce'am langs zhes rlom sems med/ /ces pa dang / ji ltar dug dang 'dres pa'i kha zas bzang za ba/ /dkar po'i chos la dmigs pa'ang rgyal bas de 'drar gsungs/ /zhes bya ba la sogs pas dus dang gnas
<p>118a.3</p>skabs thams cad du kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba'i chos thams cad sgyu ma dang 'dra bar blta bar gsungs kyi de las gzhan du ma yin no zhe na/ de ni bden mod kyi 'on kyang lam der ni sdom pa'i dbang du byas te/ de ltar ma bltas na sdom pa 'di nyams pa zhes
<p>118a.4</p>ma bzhag la/ de nyid kyis de dag shin tu g.yel bas brgya lam na shes pa de 'byung ba dang 'dra ba yin la/ lam 'dir ni sku gsung thugs kyi dam tshig las shes pa de dang ma bral na thugs kyi dam tshig las nyams par bzhag pas na dam tshig nyams pas 'jigs pa
<p>118a.5</p>bskul te/ rtag tu ting nge 'dzin de dang 'bral bar mi byed cing bral bar spyad pas ni yang bag yod pas sdom zhing 'chags pa la yang sbyor ba na rtag tu mi 'bral ba ste/ de bas na ji ltar de bzhin gshegs pa'i thugs dngos por 'dzin pa las rtag par dben pa ltar sngags
<p>118a.6</p>pa'i shes pa yang rtag par dngos por 'dzin pa las grol zhing sgyu ma dang 'dra bar rang bzhin gcig pa las mi phyed pas 'di rdo rje'i theg pa zhes bya la/ lam gzhan pas myur ba yang yin no/ /de bas na theg pa chen po 'di ni dbang po rnon po'i dbang du byas pa yin no/ /de'i phyir
<p>118a.7</p>gsungs pa/ rgyal ba'i gzhi rnams ma thob kyang / /yid brtan par ni 'gyur ma yin/ /ji srid sa brgyad la gnas par/ /theg pa dman 'jigs de la yod/ /gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor chen po 'dir/ /rgyal ba'i sras po rab nges na/ /yid nges par ni gyur pa yis/ /theg
<p>118b</p>
<p>118b.1</p>pa che la gzhol ba yin/ /zhes so/ /spyod pa bla na med pa ni mi mthun pa'i spyod pa gsum spangs pa ste/ de la nus pa chung bar byed pa'i spyod pa ni/ dka' thub sdom pa mi zad pa/ /bsten pas grub par mi 'gyur gyi/ /'dod pa'i longs spyod thams cad la/ /brten nas myur
<p>118b.2</p>du 'grub par 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs pa ste/ lus 'di ni shin tu gsos shing stobs yod par byas la yid shin tu dga' bar byas te/ de nas de gnyis shin tu drag par dge ba spyad pas tshar gcad kyis/ lus nyam chung ba dang yid mi dga' bas ni rnal 'byor ga la 'grub/ blo'i
<p>118b.3</p>stobs chung ba dag ni lus shin tu gsos shing stobs can du byas kyang dge bas tshar gcod par mi nus kyi/ 'dod chags kyi mtha' la sogs par gyur du dogs nas sbyangs pa'i yon tan la sogs pa bsten par gsungs so/ /'dir ni blo'i stobs yod pa dag la dgongs pas longs
<p>118b.4</p>spyod nyid gnang ngo / /dge bas tshar gcod par mi nus pa ni sngags pa nyid kyang ma yin no/ /longs spyod kyang ma gnang ba nyid yin no/ /g.yeng bar byed pa'i spyod pa ni/ /gal te byang chub mchog 'dod na/ /glegs bam bklag par mi bya zhing / /mchod rten bskor ba mi bya'o/ /byas na
<p>118b.5</p>byang chub rnyed par dka'/ /zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs te/ 'dod pa'i 'bras bu byang chub sgrub pa la rgyu'i gtso bo ni/ sems yin pas dang por ni/ sems tshar gcad cing bya ba gzhan gtsor mi bya'o/ /sems la dbang ma thob pa dag ni glegs bam bklag pa la
<p>118b.6</p>sogs pa lus dang ngag gi bya ba spyod pa na sems g.yeng bar 'gyur bas bya ba thams cad btang ste/ ci bder gnas pas sems legs par blta ste/ sems kyi dmigs pa thob nas nyon mongs pa rags pa gcod pa'i dbang thob pa na bya ba phyi rol pa spyad pa'am/ yang na sems
<p>118b.7</p>stong pa nyid 'ba' zhig bsgom pas chog gi lus dang ngag gi bya ba ni dgos te/ rnam par snang mdzad mngon par byang chub pa las/ mtshan mar bcas pas mtshan bcas kyi/ /dngos grub rgyal ba dam pa bzhed/ /mtshan ma med la gnas pa ni/ /mtshan mar bcas pa'ang
<p>119a</p>
<p>119a.1</p>grub tu rung / /de bas rnam pa thams cad du/ /mtshan ma med la gnas par bya/ /zhes gsungs so/ /slob dpon ye shes snying pos kyang bden pa gnyis rnam par 'byed pa'i 'grel pa las/ chos kyi dbyings rtogs na 'jig rten dang 'jig
<p>119a.2</p>rten las 'das pa'i chos thams cad bos pa bzhin du 'du ste/ zad pa shes pa zag bcas kyang / /zhes pa'i lung dang ldan par bshad do/ /de bas na/ bdag gi nyon mongs pa spang ba dang / gzhan gyi don rtsol ba dang bcas pa 'byung bar bya ba la ni stong pa nyid 'ba'
<p>119a.3</p>zhig bsgom pa'am/ dang por sems 'ba' zhig dbang du byas la de'i rjes la bya ba gzhan spyad pa 'di ni thabs kyi mchog go/ /'di ni kr-i ya dang / yo ga dang / u pa yo ga dag la med pas/ rnal 'byor chen po'i tshul spyod pa rnam pa gsum las spros pa med pa'i
<p>119a.4</p>spyod pa'am/ shin tu spros pa med pa'i spyod pa dang mthun pa'o/ /dngos por 'dzin pa'i spyod pa ni/ /sha lnga dang ni bdud rtsi lnga/ /rnam rtog spang phyir ci rigs bsten/ /zhes brjod pa ste/ 'di ni gtsang ba'o/ /'di ni mi gtsang ba'o zhes rtog pa nyid 'ching ba yin pa'i phyir
<p>119a.5</p>sdig pa med pa'i sha shin tu smad pa mi dang rta dang / ba lang dang / khyi dang / glang po che dag dang / thabs kyis zin par spyod pa dag gis 'chi ba zlog pa'i bdud rtsi khu ba dang / khrag dang / bshang ba dang / gci ba dang / mi'i sha dag ci rigs pa'i tshul gyis stong par bsam zhing / 
<p>119a.6</p>yang de dag nyid lha'i bdud rtsi ltar bsams nas/ chags pa med par spyad na rim gyis mi gtsang ba dang / gtsang ba'i rnam par rtog pa mi 'byung la/ de'i tshe chos thams cad la tha dad pa'i rtog pa 'byung ba brdzun yin par nges pa'i shes pa 'byung ba dang / mi ma yin pa kha cig de
<p>119a.7</p>nyid kyis de la yongs su dga' ba 'byung zhing chos bzhin du skyob pa dang de'i gdams ngag 'dzin par 'gyur ba yod do/ /sha lnga bdud rtsi lnga ni mtshon pa ste/ yul gang na sha la sogs pa mi gtsang bar 'dzin pa de dag de nyid la ma chags par spyod do/ /mnyam pa'i shes pa mthong ba na bdag gi
<p>119b</p>
<p>119b.1</p>don du de dag spyad par bya mi dgos so/ /'di ni spyod pas myur ba'o/ /de ltar thabs mkhas pa bcu gcig po 'di dag gis 'phags pa na 'di thabs kyi theg pa zhes bya'o/ /theg pa chen po'i yang chen po zhes bya'o/ /thabs myur ba dang / sla ba dang / mang ba dang / mkhas pa zhes bya'o/ /gang
<p>119b.2</p>yang / don gcig nyid na'ang ma rmongs dang / /thabs mang dka' ba med phyir dang / /dbang po rnon po'i dbang byas pas/ /sngags kyi bstan bcos khyad par 'phags/ /zhes bshad pa dang / dmigs pa rnam par dag pa dang / /grogs kyi mthu dang spyod pa yis/ /blo ldan rnams
<p>119b.3</p>kyi theg pa ni/ /chen po'i chen po nyid du bsgrags/ /zhes pa la sogs pas theg pa 'di'i che ba nyid brjod pa yang tshul snga ma dag nyid du 'dus par blta'o/ /mdor bsdus pa 'di brjod de/ gsang sngags ni gnyis te/ ngo bo nyid kyi gsang sngags thabs dang shes rab gnyis su
<p>119b.4</p>med pa dang / btags pa'i gsang sngags lha dang sngags dang phyag rgya dang phrin las dang ting nge 'dzin gyi tshogs dang mchod pa dang / bstod pa la sogs pa'o/ /de'i dbang gis gdul bya yang gnyis te/ mchog dang mchog ma yin pa'o/ /mchog gis ni sngar bshad pa'i thabs
<p>119b.5</p>bcu gcig po ma lus pa bsgrub bo/ /mchog ma yin pas na re zhig rnam par byang ba'i sgo khyad par can la zhugs pa tsam las thabs de dag bsgrub par nus pa ma yin no/ /'on kyang de la yang brnyas par mi bya ste/ ji ltar gsungs pa/ dper na mar gyis gang ba'i snod/ /me yi dbus
<p>119b.6</p>su bzhag gyur na/ /mar sar steng du zhu 'gyur zhing / /snod kyi dri ma 'jig par 'gyur/ /de bzhin shrI he ru ka yi/ /mtshan gyis sdig pa 'jig par 'gyur/ /zhes dpal bde mchog phyi ma'i phyi ma las so/ /'di ni skur pa spang ba'o/ /'bras bu yang dag par 'grub pa dang / las la ni
<p>119b.7</p>khyad par med de/ ji srid nam mkha' khyab par sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes kyis khyab la/ ji srid ye shes kyis khyab pa de srid skus khyab pa'i phyir dang / dang po sems can ma lus pa dang / zhing ma lus pa sbyang ba'i phyir zhugs pa dang / spangs pa dang / ye shes la khyad med pa dang / 
<p>120a</p>
<p>120a.1</p>slob pa'i gnas skabs na yang sa dang po man chad/ bgrod pa tha dad pa srid kyang / sa dang po chos kyi dbyings mthong nas/ lam ma lus pa rang bzhin gyis nges par shes pa'i phyir ro/ /'di ni sgro 'dogs pa spang ba'o/ /de ltar gzhung 'di bkod pas bdag /spros dang bral
<p>120a.2</p>ba'i gnas thob shog /'gro ba'ang mtha' gnyis bral ba yi/ /lam du myur du 'jug par shog /rdo rje theg pa'i mtha' gnyis sel ba zhes bya ba slob dpon dz+nyA na shrIs bkod pa rdzogs so//[ ]@##/ /rgya gar skad du/ tat+t+wa mArgA daR+sha na nA ma/ bod skad du/ de nyid
<p>120a.3</p>mthong ba'i lam zhes bya ba/ spyan ras gzigs mgon de la phyag 'tshal lo/ /zhi zhing 'byor pa 'gro mgon thugs rje can/ /ri khrod zhabs la gus pas phyag 'tshal te/ /ston las rje yis byin brlabs rgyud kyi don/ /zhabs kyi rdul la ma reg chos 'di ni/ /dad brtson ldan dang bdag
<p>120a.4</p>nyid brjed 'jigs pas/ /de nyid mthong ba'i lam 'di 'dir bshad bya/ /thams cad mkhyen pas 'di gsungs pa/ /gdul bya'i rim pas gzhag pa ste/ /dang por gso sbyong sbyin par bya/ /de rjes bslab pa'i gnas bcu nyid/ /de nas bye brag smra la bslab/ /mdo sde pa yang de nas
<p>120a.5</p>bstan/ /rnal 'byor spyod pa de bzhin te/ /de nas dbu ma pa yang bstan/ /sngags kyi rim pa kun shes nas/ /dgyes pa'i rdo rje'i dbang bskur sbyin/ /dgyes rdor rgyud nas de bstan pas/ /gso sbyong gnas bcu bye brag dang / /chung ba'i mdo sde nyan thos lam/ /theg pa chen po'i
<p>120a.6</p>mdo sde dang / /rnal 'byor spyod dang dbu ma'i chos/ /sngags gzhan dgyes rdor brjod pa nyid/ /bde ba'i lam dang 'bras bur bsngags/ /de la dang po nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas pa dbang po rnon pos/ mdo dang 'dul ba ltar yang shes par bya'o/ /'dir rgyud ltar skal ba dang
<p>120a.7</p>ldan pas bla ma mnyes pas bsgrub ste/ de yang dang po/ thabs 'di rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyis/ /skas kyi rim pa lta bur gsungs/ /zhes pas theg pa gsum la bslabs par bya ste/ nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas gnyis la 'jug par 'dod pas dang po gso sbyong bya ba dang / 
<p>120b</p>
<p>120b.1</p>gnyis pa bslab pa bsrung ba dang / gsum pa chos la bslab pa'o/ /de yang byams pas zhus pa'i mdo las/ dang po skyabs dang gso sbyong bya/ /gnyis pa bslab pa'i rim pa bzhin/ /gsum pa chos dag de la bstan/ /zhes pas so/ /skyabs la bdun te/ dang po dang / lus
<p>120b.2</p>ngag yid kyi sbyor ba dang / rten dang / de la mchod pa dang / dus dang / yon tan dang / mi nyams par bya ba'o/ /dang po la gnyis te/ shes pa dag pa'i mkhan po dang / slob dpon no/ /sbyor ba ni lus gus pa dang / ngag 'jam pas brjod pa dang yid chos la dag pa dang gsum mo/ /
<p>120b.3</p>rten mchog tu gyur pa ni dkon mchog go/ /rten la mchod pa ni ci 'byor pa'i mchod pas lus dbul ba'o/ /dus ni 'di nas zhes pa dang / ji srid 'tsho'i bar gnyis so/ /yon tan ni sngon gyi sdig pa thams cad 'byang zhing phyi ma'i sdug bsngal thams cad zad pa bde ba'o/ /mi
<p>120b.4</p>nyams par bya ba la gsum ste/ sangs rgyas la skyabs nas 'jig rten pa'i lha spangs pa dang / chos la skyabs nas srog mi gcod pa dang / dge 'dun la skyabs nas mu stegs dang mi 'grogs pa'o/ /bslab pa bsrung ba la gnyis te/ rten dang bslab pa dngos so/ /rten la
<p>120b.5</p>gsum ste/ gzhan las skye ba dang / rang las skye ba dang / gnyi ga las skye ba'o/ /gzhan las skye ba la gsum ste/ mkhan po dang slob dpon te/ dang po bar chad med pas tshul khrims thob pa dang / nus pa dang ldan pas sdom pa la gnas pa dang / bdag dang gzhan gyi nyes
<p>120b.6</p>pa 'chos dgos pas mkhas pa ste/ de gsum dang ldan pa las bslab pa skye'o/ /rang las skye ba la gnyis te/ spyi dang bye brag go/ /spyi la drug ste/ 'gro ba khyad par 'phags pa ni mi tsam ma yin te/ gling khyad par du 'phags pa'i gling 'di tsam yin te/ rigs khyad par du
<p>120b.7</p>'phags pa rgyal rigs dang / bram ze'i rigs dang / rje'u'i rigs so/ /rigs tsam ma yin te/ gzugs khyad par du 'phags pa skyes pa dang bud med tsam yin te/ lus khyad par 'phags pa dbang po tshang ba tsam gyis mi chog ste/ shes pa dang sems khyad par du 'phags pa rgan
<p>121a</p>
<p>121a.1</p>gzhon spangs nas lus dar ba'o/ /bye brag spyi dang ldan pa des nam blangs pa'i dus der skye'o/ /gnyi ga las skye ba la gsum ste/ mkhan slob la the tshom med pa dang / chos dang chos kyi yon tan la the tshom med pa dang / bslab pa bsrungs pa dang thob par the tshom med
<p>121a.2</p>pas skye'o/ /bslab pa dngos la brgyad de/ rten gyi khyad par gyis bslab pa'i rim pa dang / bslab par bya ba'i ngo bo dang / nyes pa'i tshad dang / bcos pa'i thabs dang / nges pa skyes pa dang / dus ma nges par bslab pa dang / yon tan dang / thob pa'i dus bstan pa'o/ /
<p>121a.3</p>bslab pa'i rim pa la so so thar pa rigs bdun gyi rim pas bslab pa ste/ sde pa'i 'dod pa mi mthun te/ yang 'dir bsnyen gnas dang / dge bsnyen la bzhi ste lnga dang / dge tshul dang / dge slong dang bdun gyis bslab pa'o/ /ngo bo la gnyis te spyi dang bye brag go/ /spyi la
<p>121a.4</p>yang gnyis te rtsa ba'am rang bzhin gyi sdig pa sdom pa dang / yan lag gam bcas pa'i sdom pa'o/ /bye brag ni bsnyen gnas la rtsa ba bzhi ste brgyad do/ /sna 'ga' bsrung ba'i dge bsnyen la srog mi gcod pa dang / rtsa ba gzhan gang rung cig /phal cher bsrung ba la rtsa ba
<p>121a.5</p>gsum/ yongs su rdzogs pa la rtsa ba gsum dang 'dod log bsrung / tshangs par spyod pa'i dge bsnyen ni rtsa ba bzhi dang chang bsrung ba'o/ /dge tshul gyis rtsa ba bzhi yan lag bdun/ chang dang glu gar rtse 'jo dang / /rgyan dang kha dog 'chang ba dang / /mal stan chen po gser
<p>121a.6</p>dngul gyi khri dang / khri stan mthon po khru gang pa yan chad spang ba dang / phyi dro kha zas dang / gser dngul 'chang ba spang ba'o/ /mkhan po las thob pa'i rtags gsum ste/ khyim pa'i rtags gtsug phud dang / gos dkar po spangs te/ rab tu byung ba'i rtags skra dang kha spu bregs nas gos
<p>121a.7</p>ngur smrig gon pa'o/ /phyi rol mu stegs pa'i rtags stod gos g.yas la 'gel ba dang / smad gos dkris pa spangs nas nang ba sangs rgyas pa'i rtags stod gos g.yon du 'gel ba dang / smad gos che bas zur du spung ba'o/ /mi dge ba 'jig rten pa'i rtags de dag spangs nas dge ba dge 'dun gyi
<p>121b</p>
<p>121b.1</p>rtags gseg shang dang lhung bzed gri khab la sogs pa mkho ba'i rdzas bzung ba'o/ /dge slong gis shes rab can dang / dngos kyi rtsa ba bzhi dang / khu ba phyung ba la sogs pa lhag ma bcu gsum dben pa dang / skyabs ma nges pa gnyis dang 'chang ba 'bral ba la sogs spang ba'i ltung byed
<p>121b.2</p>sum cu dang / ltung byed dgu bcu dang / grong du nyal ba la sogs pa so sor bshags pa bzhi dang / sham thabs la sogs pa bslab par bya ba brgyad cu rtsa gnyis dang / mngon sum du nga rgyal mi bya ba la sogs te nyis brgya lnga bcu rtsa gsum bka' lung nas shes par bya'o/ /'dir 'og nas
<p>121b.3</p>ston pa'i lus ngag yid kyis mi bya ba dang bya ba rnams so/ /de nas bslab pa'i gnas bcu sbyin/ /zhes pas mi dge ba bcu spangs la dge ba bcu bsten pa'o/ /nyes pa'i tshad la gnyis te/ rtsa ba dang yan lag gi'o/ /rtsa ba la lnga/ rtsa ba dang 'dra bar sbyor ba dang / dngos dang mjug
<p>121b.4</p>tshang na ltung ba chen pos nyams/ dngos mjug gnyis byung na ltung ba sbom po ste nyams/ sbyor ba dang dngos byung na chung ngu na te nyams/ sbyor ba dang mjug byung na ltung ba phra mo ste nyams/ re re byung na ltung byed de nyams/ lhag ma dang ma nges pa la sogs pa'i yan lag rnams la yang
<p>121b.5</p>lnga ste/ sbyor ba dang / dngos dang mjug rdzogs na nyes pa chen po ste nyams/ dngos mjug gnyis byung na nyes pa sgom po ste nyams/ sbyor ba dang dngos byung na nyes pa chung ngu na te nyams/ sbyor ba dang mjug gnyis byung na nyes pa phra mo ste nyams/ re re byung na nyes pa med do/ /bcos
<p>121b.6</p>pa'i thabs la gnyis te/ thabs dngos dang dus so/ /thabs la bcu gcig ste rtsa ba dang yan lag gnyis yan chad dam/ bzhi man chad byung na 'gyod pas lan gsum du bskyar zhing blang / rtsa ba'i sbom po byung na sngon bzhin du blang / chung ngu na byung na slob dpon las de nyid blang / phra
<p>121b.7</p>mo byung na slob dpon la bshags pas thub/ ltung byed byung na 'gyod pa dang bsdams sems kyis thub/ nyes pa chen po byung ba sngon bzhin blang / nyes pa sbom po slob dpon las blang / nyes pa chung ngu na slob dpon la bshags/ nyes pa phra mo 'gyod pa dang bsdams sems kyis thub
<p>122a</p>
<p>122a.1</p>nyes med phyis ma byas pas thub/ chang rtsa ba dang 'dra'o/ /rtsa ba dang yan lag ltar kun btang sems kyis btang na blang du med/ rgas pa dang na ba dang gzhan gyi dbang la nyes pa med/ dus la bzhi ste/ bsnyen gnas kyi skabs dang ldan te/ nyin skabs med na zla gcig
<p>122a.2</p>gam phyed dam brgyad kyi dus de'o/ /dge bsnyen skabs dang ldan na thun gnyis pa la blang / skabs med na zhag lnga la blang / dge tshul skabs dang ldan na zhag lnga tshun chad la blang / mi ldan na zla ba gcig tshun chad na blang / dge slong skabs dang ldan na de nyid nas zhag bcu mi ldan na zla ba
<p>122a.3</p>bdun tshun chad/ nges bskyed pa dus de la rtsa ba dang / yan lag nyams pa/ thabs des bcos pas thar pa thob ste/ sgrung gi dpe re re bstan pa'o/ /de yang srog gcad pa las thar pa/ dge slong zla ba'i 'od bya ba rigs bram ze yin pas/ lo nyi shu rtsa gcig nas bzhi bcu'i bar nyi shur
<p>122a.4</p>sdom pa bsrungs te/ bzhi bcu lon nas pha kun du 'khor zhes bya bas snyan ngag yod pas rgyal po'i pho brang du snyan ngag bton pas/ rgyal po gzugs can snying po shin tu dga' nas/ go la bdun dang bcas pa byin nas bram ze gzhan cig gis gcig lam du khyer bas khros nas 'thabs
<p>122a.5</p>pas kun du 'khor ba gsod do/ /bu dge slong sems 'khrugs te sbyor ba gsang bas las kyi spu gri khyer te/ bram ze khrus byed sar bsgugs te spu gri mngad nas bdar ba dang / bram ze khrus las byung ba dang spu gris ske bcad de bsad do/ /mjug 'gyod pa med par dga' bar gyur te/ 
<p>122a.6</p>ro yang gar dgar gzhag go/ /der kun gyis ro mthong nas 'di sus bsad snyam nas ngas pha'i mi shar bsad ces bsgrags so/ /der kun gyis kyang dpyas par gyur/ rtags kyang gzhag pa las/ yul der nad 'go ba byung ste/ kun ka na ba dang / dka' thub med pa de yang na ba dang
<p>122a.7</p>nad drag pos gzir bas shin tu 'gyod pa'i sems skyes te/ lung nas sangs rgyas 'od ma'i tshal na bzhugs pa la gong gi nyes pa rnams zhus pas sangs rgyas kyis gnad nas bslab pa bskyar te/ dge slong dri ma dang bral bar gyur te ma ltung ngo / /yul yangs pa can gyi grong na rje'u'i
<p>122b</p>
<p>122b.1</p>rigs dge slong rin chen srung zhes bya ba cig yod pa la bsod snyoms la phyin nas khyim bdag gi mdzod mthong ste/ lha khang gi logs su sbyor ba la dong brkos te gnas de nas ma ga d+hAr sangs rgyas kyi spyan sngar 'gro zhes dge 'dun la bsgrags nas song ste/ de nub nam phyed na bang
<p>122b.2</p>mdzod phug ste/ be+e DUr+ya dang / pad+ma rA ga dang / gser dngul rkus nas da ci'i dong du sbas te/ mjug 'gyod pa med par dga' bar gyur te/ /de longs spyod spyod pa las nub mo rkun po rkun 'phyan gzhan dang phrad nas nor khyer ro/ /lus gtag pa las shin tu 'gyod nas sangs rgyas kyi
<p>122b.3</p>spyan sngar phyin te/ gong gi nyes pa bshags nas sdom pa blangs te sangs rgyas kyis gnang nas dge slong rin chen 'byung gnas su gyur te ltung ba med do/ /grong khyer ser skyar dge slong shes grags kyis bsod snyoms byed pa las/ re zhig na smad 'tshong ba 'byor pa rnyed bya ba'i sgor phyin te
<p>122b.4</p>bslangs nas yon byin pas/ smad 'tshong ma de shin tu legs par mthong ste/ chags pa'i sems kyis sbyor ba slar log nas ka bya ri'i ras g.yar nas gyon te/ 'gron bu ka ho na cig khyer nas srod la phyin te nga nyon byas pa las yar shog zer te phyin nas chags pa skye ba'i thabs sna
<p>122b.5</p>tshogs byas dngos su nyon mongs pa la zhen nas bsrubs te khu ba phyung ngo / /mjug bde bar tshor nas phyis kyang phrad do/ /ring zhig na ro mdze byung ste sdug bsngal bar gyur nas 'gyod de sangs rgyas kyi spyan sngar phyin nas sa la 'gyel te nyes pa rnams bshags nas bslab pa bskyar
<p>122b.6</p>te/ dge slong zhi ba'i ye shes su gyur te ltung ba med do/ /rgyal byed kyi tshal du dge slong byang chub 'byung gnas su grags pa rgyal rigs su gyur pa cig byung bas dad pa shin tu che nas khar+sa pa Nar phyin pas spyan ras gzigs mthong nas yul de la khar+sa pa Na zhes btags so/ /
<p>122b.7</p>slar log nas ma ga d+hAr phyin te/ bstan bcos mang po byas nas de nas nga la sangs rgyas mang pos bstan zhes bsgrags pas/ slob ma mang po yod pa las/ sangs rgyas kyis mkhyen nas ma btang ba las nor sa 'og tu sbas nas phyin pa dang / sgyu ma byas pa'i sbyor ba mang po
<p>123a</p>
<p>123a.1</p>byas nas chos 'chad pa'i sbyor ba dang / dngos su kun bsrubs pa mang ba dang / mjug 'gyod pa med par dga' bas longs spyod spyod pa la rgyal po'i chad pa byung la khad pa dang tshor nas shin tu 'gyod pa skyes te/ sangs rgyas kyi spyan sngar phyin te nyes pa kun bshags te
<p>123a.2</p>slar bslab pa gsos nas dge slong rdo rje snying por gyur te ltung ba med do/ /gzhan yang 'dul ba dang mdo nas 'gyod de/ slar gsos pas thar pa mang po dang / gtan gyi the tshom med par phyir bcos so/ /yan lag gi nyes pa tsho yang bcos pas yang bar shes par bya'o/ /chang rtsa ba
