<p>143a.3</p>man ngag tu 'dod do/ /sna tshogs su shes pas mngon sum gyis da lta shes zhes te/ de la skyon mang ste/ de gdod nas sam da ltar gdod nas na sngon du ma shes pa ci/ shes kyang ma phan na dgos pa med/ shes kyang dgos na thug pa med nas ma shes na rang rig nyams/ da lta na sngon du med phyis
<p>143a.4</p>med pas chad par thal/ yang na gnyis med de gnyis med du gang gis shes/ gzhan gyis shes sam de nyid kyis shes/ gzhan gyis shes na rang rig nyams/ de nyid kyis de nyid shes sam/ de las 'byung bas shes/ de nyid kyis de nyid shes na/ rtag nas sam mi rtag nas/ rtag na mi

<p>147b.1</p>dbul lo/ /rdzas bsag pa ni rgyud kun nas/ /rin chen gser dngul mu tig dang / /me tog la sogs rgyal srid bcas/ /gtor ma shing rtas bskyal ba dang / /dpa' bo'i ston mos dga' ston bya/ /zhes pas 'khor lo mchod pa la chu gtsang brgyad stong khri 'bum gyi bar du dgram/

<p>147b.3</p>dang / nang gi mchod pa dang / bcu gnyis bcu drug nyi shus mdzad pa de kho na'i mchod pa des kho na'i mchod pa bsag /bla ma mchod pa la yang de ltar mchod pa gsum dang / rgyun gyi bye brag bsag pa dang / chos skyong mchod pa'i yo byad 'bras chan la sogs pa tshan gyi rigs ji snyed
<p>147b.4</p>yod pa dang / sha dang nya'i rigs dang / tig tas bran pa'i tshod ma la sogs pa'i rigs dang / zho la sogs pa'i dkar gyi rigs dang / la du la sogs pa khur ba'i rigs dang / gur kum la sogs pa sman gyi rigs dang / na ri ke la sogs pa'i 'bras bu'i rigs dang / pog
<p>147b.5</p>phran la sogs pa la du'i rigs dang / ka ra la sogs pa mngar gyi rigs dang / la phug la sogs pa rtsa ba'i rigs dang / gzhan yang bca' ba dang / tsha ba dang / kha ba dang / skyur ba'i rigs kyi mchod pa'o/ /rdzas bsag pa dang / dga' ston bya ba yang rgyud nas/ /mchod 'os ma gyur
<p>147b.6</p>gtor ma dbang / /sde dang rigs rnams dga' bar bya/ /zhes pas dbang thon nas yo byad lhag pa la rnal 'byor pa dang / ku su lu'i tshogs dang / paN+Di ta dang / slob ma'i 'khor dang / dge 'dun dang / dge bsnyen gyi g.yog dang / rgyal po dang / rgyal rigs dang / bram ze dang / rig
<p>147b.7</p>byed kyi sde dang / rje'u rigs dang / gtsang ma rnams dang / dmangs rigs dang / rigs ngan rnams la ci rigs pas mchod pa dang / sbyin pa bya ba'i phyir bsag go/ /bsnyen pa zhu ba ni de ltar rdzas tshogs nas slob dpon bdag gi bsam pa sgrub par zhu zhes lan gsum brjod cing
<p>148a</p>
<p>148a.1</p>maN+Dal dang me tog gi phreng ba dbul lo/ /sdom pa gzung ba ni bsnyen pa'i dus te 'og nas ston to/ /slob dpon gyis las la shes pa dang dbang bskur ba ste/ shes pa la bzhi ste/ brgyad pa dang ldan pas sangs rgyas nas bar ma chad pa/ don dam rtog pa rab tu mi
<p>148a.2</p>gnas pa'i lta ba 'dod pa rtog pas sku bzhi man ngag gis sgrub pa'i don shes pa dang / byin rlabs dam tshig las 'byung bas dam tshig shes nas bsrung ba dang / rgyud dang dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga la mkhas pas ma tshang ba brgyad kyis kha skong ba dang / slob ma yongs su skyob pa dang / 
<p>148a.3</p>gzhan don la brtson zhing ma chags pas bsnyen pa dang ldan zhing 'byor pa la phan pa'o/ /cho ga la gsum ste/ bsnyen pa'i cho ga dang / dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga dang / dbang bskur ba'i cho ga'o/ /bsnyen pa la slob ma'i bsnyen pa dang / lha'i bsnyen pa gnyis las slob ma'i
<p>148a.4</p>bsnyen pa la yang sdom pa sbyin pa dang bsrung ba gnyis so/ /sdom pa sbyin pa la slob dpon rim gyis bstan pa slob ma srung du gzhug pa gnyis las/ slob ma srung du gzhug pa'i sdom pa la yang chung ba dang / che ba gnyis las chung ba ni sngon du bstan pa'i skyabs su gsol ba'i bye
<p>148a.5</p>brag bdun dang / rten dang bslab pa'i bye brag rnams rim pas bstan la srung du gzhug pa'o/ /theg pa chen po'i yang de bzhin du gong du bstan pa bzhin du srung du gzhug pa'o/ /bsrung ba la yang gnyis te/ mkha' gsang du rnam par snang mdzad du bya ste/ phyogs bcu'i sangs
<p>148a.6</p>rgyas thams cad kyis byin gyis brlabs nas gdon pa dang / rgyu gong bsnyen gyi bsrung ba sngags zlos su gzhug pa'o/ /lha'i bsnyen pa la bsnyen thabs dang / brtag gnyis las/ lha'i bsnyen pa'i thabs la rdzas kyis bsnyen pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / sngags kyis bsnyen pa
<p>148a.7</p>dang gsum mo/ /rdzas la maN+Dal phul bas 'khor bas 'khor lo bsnyen pa dang / gtor mas chos skyong bsnyen pa'o/ /ting nge 'dzin la rnal 'byor bzhis 'khor lo bsnyen pa dang dgug gzhug bskyed pas chos skyong bsnyen pa'o/ /sngags la gtso 'khor gnyis bsnyen pa dang / yi
<p>148b</p>
<p>148b.1</p>ge brgya mtshams sbyar ba'o/ /rtags la mngon sum dang / mtshan ma dang / grangs su bskyal ba'o/ /dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga la yang bzhi ste/ dkyil 'khor rgyu'i bya ba dang / lhag gnas dang / dkyil 'khor gyi ngo bo dang / cho ga dngos so/ /rgyu'i bya ba la bdun te/ sa btsal ba dang / 
<p>148b.2</p>brtag pa dang / bslang ba dang / gzung ba dang / gcad pa dang / sbyang ba dang / brtsig pa'o/ /lha gnas la bzhi ste/ sa'i lha mo dang / 'khor lo dang / bum pa dang / slob ma lhag par gnas pa'o/ /ngo bo la thig gdab pa dang / tshon dgye ba dang / rgyan dgod pa'o/ /sa btsal ba
<p>148b.3</p>la ting nge 'dzin sogs kyis lus lha/ yid gang 'dod kyi 'gro don la dmigs pa dang / ngag snying po'i sbyor ba dang / btsal ba dngos la las dang sbyar la phyogs btsal ba dang / rgyud ltar dben pa'am mi 'jigs pa'i sa btsal ba'o/ /brtag pa la yang sbyor ba dngos su
<p>148b.4</p>song ba las dang sbyar ba kha dog dbyibs brtag pa dang / rgyud ltar bum pa la sogs pa'i mtshan nyid brtag pa'o/ /bslang ba la yang bdag po dngos por snang ba las bslang ba dang / dngos po med pa las bslang ba'o/ /gzung ba la yang rnal 'byor bzhis gzung ba dang / sa'i lha mo
<p>148b.5</p>dpang bas gzung ba'o/ /gcad pa la yang ji tsam 'dod pa de sa'i lha mo mkha' la bteg la yid kyis gcad pa dang / khro bo'i phur bus phyogs ma nor bar gcad pa'o/ /sbyang ba la rdzas dang / lus dang / ngag dang / yid kyis sbyang ba lnga las/ rdzas la sa ro mang na legs par
<p>148b.6</p>bsal/ gzhan gyis dgang ba dang / rin po che'i bum pa bcud can sba ba dang / gtor ma gtang ba'o/ /lus rkang pa rdo rje brkyang bskum gyis bgegs bsal ba'o/ /ngag slob mas/ de bzhin gshegs kun zhi ba dang / /zhes pa la sogs pa dang / yak+Sha zhes brjod pas bgegs
<p>148b.7</p>bsal ba'o/ /yid dra ba dang / gur dang / gdod nas dag pa dang / rdo rje'i gdan ltar mi 'gyur bar bsam mo/ /rtsig pa la dri dang ba'i rnam pa lnga bsres la tshad dang ldan par brtsig pa dang / dri dang spos byug pa'o/ /sa'i lha mo lhag par gnas pa las bskyed pa dang / nam mkha'i spyan
<p>149a</p>
<p>149a.1</p>drang ba dang / mchod pa dang / gnyis med byas la bstim pa'o/ /'khor lo lhag gnas las me tog dgod pa dang / lha bskyed pa dang / gsol ba gdab pa gsum pa las/ me tog dgod pa la rdo rje slob dpon gyis lha'i gnas su mtshan ma gdab pa dang / las kyi
<p>149a.2</p>slob dpon gyis me tog dgod pa'o/ /lha bskyed pa ni sbyor ba gsum gyi rnal 'byor bzhi sgrub thabs kyi 'dod pas bskyed pa'o/ /gsol ba gdab pa la lnga ste/ slob dpon phyir byung la shar nas yid kyis blta ba dang / 'khor lo'i lha la gsol ba gdab pa dang / sangs rgyas dang byang chub
<p>149a.3</p>sems dpa' spyi la gsol ba gdab pa dang / chos skyong la gsol ba gdab pa dang / gsol ba btab la mkha' la gshegs pa'o/ /bum pa'i lhag gnas la mtshan nyid dang / phyi'i bya ba dang / nang gi bya ba gsum mo/ /mtshan nyid la grangs lha dang sbyor ba dang / rgyu rin po che'am
<p>149a.4</p>sa las byas pa dang / mu stegs kyi ma yin pa bre gang las mi chung / bre gsum las mi che ba/ rtsa ba med cing mi gnag pa'o/ /phyi'i bya ba la yang mtshan ma gdab pa dang / kha rgyan mgul rgyan gyis brgyan pa dang / gdan la gzhag pa'o/ /nang gi bya ba bcud la drug ste/ bcud blugs pa
<p>149a.5</p>dang / gzhal yas khang dang lhar bskyed pa dang / ye shes kyi lha dgug pa dang / mchod pa dang / sngags bzlas pa dang / bzhu bas bkang la gnas su gzhag pa'o/ /slob ma'i lhag gnas la slob dpon dang / slob ma 'brel ba'i bya ba bdun te/ spro ba bskyed pa dang / gnang ba sbyin pa
<p>149a.6</p>dang / sdom pa sbyin pa dang / bsrung ba dang / so shing dor ba dang / ku sha'i sngas dang stan sbyin pa dang / gzengs bstod la nyal du gzhug pa'o/ /spro ba bskyed pa la gsum/ slob mas khrus byas la maN+Dal dbul ba dang / slob dpon gyis sngags kyi dngos grub ces pa'i chos bstan pa dang / 
<p>149a.7</p>slob mas pha rol la dmigs te rgya che bar shes par bya'o/ /gnang ba sbyin pa la nod pa dang / sbyin pa gnyis las/ dga' chen zhes spro bas nod pa dang / bu tshur zhes brtse bas sbyin pa'o/ /spro ba la gsum ste/ sangs rgyas zhes skyabs su gzhug pa dang / skyabs pa'i yon tan sangs rgyas
<p>149b</p>
<p>149b.1</p>longs sku/ chos bde bas bsgrub pa dang / dge 'dun gtso bo'i ngo bo bstan pa dang / sdom pa dang ldan pas slob dpon de gsum dang ldan pa dang / khyod kyi dbang thob nas yin par 'gyur ro/ /sdom pa dngos la gnyis te/ mtshan nyid kyi dang sngags kyi'o/ /mtshan nyid la bdun sngon du song
<p>149b.2</p>ba'o/ /sngags la gnyis te/ slob dpon gyi dang rigs lnga'i sdom pa 'dzin du gzhug pa/ 'di ni sangs rgyas zhes pas gzhug pa'o/ /bsrung ba la 'byor bas bsrung ba dang / gdams pas bsrung ba'o/ /'byor ba la zhi sogs kyi sbyin sreg bya'o/ /gdams pas bsrung ba la slob
<p>149b.3</p>ma dang slob dpon gyi bya ba gnyis las/ slob mas bsrung ba la/ lus gus pas rkang pa g.yas pa'i pus mo sa la btsugs la bsdad pa dang / yid bya ba dran par bya'o/ /slob dpon gyis bsrung ba la ting nge 'dzin dang / mchod pa dang rdzas gsum gyis bsrung ba'o/ /ting nge 'dzin mkha'
<p>149b.4</p>gsang du slob ma rnam par snang mdzad du byin gyis brlabs la gdon pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad lus la gzhug pa'o/ /mchod pa la gnas gsum du dris mtshan ma bya ba dang / lha bskyed pa dang / phyi nang gi mchod pas dngos su mchod pa'o/ /rdzas la skud pa dang / gtor ma gnyis las/ 
<p>149b.5</p>skud pa'i rgyu dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / sngags dang / gdags sa bzhi las/ rgyu ras sam bal lam ring thung sum bsgril mdud ma bdun nam lnga gsum du bya'o/ /ting nge 'dzin la bdud rtsi 'khyil ba la sogs par bskyed/ ye shes dgug mchod/ gnyis med du byas te/ sngags de brgya
<p>149b.6</p>stong du bzlas te go char bsam pa'o/ /gdags sa skyes pa'i g.yon/ bud med kyi g.yas su'o/ /gtor ma la rgyu byin gyis brlabs pa/ mgron bsngo ba'o/ /rgyu snod ka pA la dang / rin po che'am/ de med na shing dang rdo kyong yang bzang / byin gyis brlab pa snod dang bcud las/ snod rlung me
<p>149b.7</p>bskyed pa ka pA lar ro/ /bcud bdud rtsi lnga dang sha lnga'o/ /mgron la gnas dang / lha gnyis la/ gnas chos 'byung pad+ma dang / lha la bskyed pa dang / dgug pa las/ bskyed pa bar du chos skyong / steng du lha chen po/ 'og tu klu ste gzhan ltar ro/ /so shing dor ba la bdun te/ so shing
<p>150a</p>
<p>150a.1</p>gi mtshan nyid dang / dor sa dang / slob ma'i kha lta phyogs dang / dor ba'i thabs dang / dgos pa dang / de la dgos pa dang / ltas brtag pa'o/ /ku sha'i sngas dang / stan sbyin pa la ku sha bsangs la gtso bo'i sngags kyis sngags su sbyin pa dang / las bum gyis
<p>150a.2</p>bsangs la las kyi sngags kyis stan du sbyin pa'o/ /gzengs bstod nas nyal du gzhug pa la/ gzengs bstod pa dang / nyal ba la gnyis te/ slob dpon gyis/ 'jig rten du ni kun mkhyen dag /ces nges par bstan pa dang / slob mas spro bas yid ches pas mnyan nas dga'
<p>150a.3</p>bar bya'o/ /nyal ba la sbyor ba dang / rmi lam brtags pa dang bzla ba'o/ /sbyor ba la lus seng ge'i nyal stabs kyis dkyil 'khor dang slob dpon la sngags bstan la nyal ba dang / ngag bsnyen pa'i dus kyi snying po bzlas pa dang / yid 'gro ba dang bdag gi don 'dod pas tha mal
<p>150a.4</p>la ma yengs pas nyal ba'o/ /rmi lam brtag pa ni bdag gi so shing gi ltas dang mthun pa'i thun mong dang mchog gi ltas shog cig /ston cig ces brjod do/ /rmi lam bzla ba la bzla ba dang brtag pa'o/ /bzla ba bla ma la maN+Dal phul nas dang po'am tha ma gang gsal bzla'o/ /
<p>150a.5</p>brtag pa ni rmi lam bzang ba la sogs pa dang / ngan pa mar nag gis lus byugs sam/ spre'u dang 'bu sbrang dang / sdig sbrul gyi sos btab pa rmis na zhi sogs man ngag gis sbyin sreg bya/ gzhan yang chus khyer ba la sogs pa rmis na sngags mang du bzla/ gzhan
<p>150a.6</p>gyis bdag gi nor sogs khyer na bzang ba'o/ /gzhan yang bzang ba mang / ngan yang sgyu mar shes na zlogs so/ /thig la rgyu dang / byin gyis brlab pa dang gdab pa'o/ /rgyu dkar po la sogs pa lnga'o/ /byin gyis brlab pa thig skud 'khal ba bdag lha gtso bo'i ngo bor gsal/ 'khal mkhan
<p>150a.7</p>shar gyi lhar gsal/ nag po dkar po ser dmar ljang gu gtso bo'i 'od kyis ltar gsal/ 'od kyis rigs kyi thugs dam bskul sa sbyang ba dang snod du lha bskyed pa dang / ye shes kyi lha dgug /mchod bsgril/ gnyis med thig tu gyur pa'o/ /gdab pa ye shes kyi mkha' la gdab pa dang / 
<p>150b</p>
<p>150b.1</p>dam tshig gi skud pas dkyil 'khor dngos la gdab pa dang / ye shes kyi skud pas bsre ba'o/ /tshon la rgyu dang byin gyis brlab pa dang dgye ba'o/ /rgyu rin po che'am 'bru'am dur khrod kyi rdzas sam/ sa dngos dang lnga'o/ /byin gyis brlabs pa lha'i kha dog gis phyogs ma nor bar snod du
<p>150b.2</p>yi ge bris la gzhag pa dang / ye shes pa dgug pa dang / mchod pa dang / mchod pa dang / gnyis med tshon du gyur pa'o/ /dgye ba la bsrung ba dang / dgye ba dngos so/ /bsrung ba byang shar du gtso bo'i rim pas sor bzhi dgye ba dang / lha lnga bskyed pa dang / ye shes dgug pa dang / mchod
<p>150b.3</p>pa dang / gnyis med du gyur nas bgegs mthar byed kyis bsrungs te ka pA la bkang la gzhag go/ /dgye ba tshon phyogs dang sa la ma nor bar dgye ba dang / tshon pra brtag pa'o/ /rtsig pa lnga nas re khA bar ma chod par phyogs nas bris te sngon gyis bsrung ba nas bar tshad dam de
<p>150b.4</p>bas sboms sam/ phras sam phyi nang du yo na slob dpon 'chi ba dang / nad dang / nor nyams pa dang / cho ga 'khrugs pa la sogs pa rim pa bzhin 'ong bar shes par bya'o/ /de las log pa bzang ba'o/ /rtog pa med pa'am mi shes pas bris na nyes pa med/ rgyan dgram pa ni
<p>150b.5</p>bla bre la sogs pas dkyil 'khor gyi nam mkha' brgyan pa dang / phyi nang gi mchod pas dkyil 'khor sa gzhi brgyan pa'o/ /cho ga dngos dbang bskur ba la bzhi las/ bum pa'i dbang la/ bum pa la bsgrub pa dang / bskur ba dngos gnyis las/ bsgrub pa la rnal 'byor gsum bzhi'o/ 
<p>150b.6</p>bskur ba dngos la slob dpon gyis blang ba dang / slob ma la bskur ba gnyis las/ slob dpon gyis blang ba la dkyil 'khor du 'jug pa dang dbang dngos gnyis kyi dkyil 'khor du 'jug pa la zhugs pa dang / zhugs nas phyir shar sgor byung ba dang / phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas
<p>150b.7</p>dang / bla ma de'i sa bon gyi 'od kyis spyan drangs te/ de nyid la gzhag pa dang / bdag gi sa bon las spros la phyi nang de nyid kyi mchod pa dbul ba dang / dga' chen zhes gsol ba gdab pa dang / bdud rtsi btung ba dang / mkhyen par gsol ba dang / khyod su zhes dris nas/ slob
<p>151a</p>
<p>151a.1</p>dpon dang mi bskyod pa spyi bo na yod pa'i ngo bos bskul nas shar gyi sgo bas nang du bcug pa dang / sdom pa sbyin pa dang / bdag gis kyang sangs rgyas chos dang zhes khas blang ba dang / phyogs bcu nas yang ngo bos bskul/ shar sgor bkug mchod nas bdag
<p>151a.2</p>la phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas thams cad 'khor lor gyur nas bcug pa dang / mchog gi ye shes byin nas thun mong du las rnams kyang 'grub par lung bstan pa dang / sku'i rdo rje bkug nas bcug pa dang / thugs rdo rje bcug pa dang / gsung rdo rje bkug nas bcug pa dang / 
<p>151a.3</p>de thams cad slob dpon las byung bas mnyan par shes pa dang / sku gsung thugs kyi ye shes man ngag ltar dbab pa dang / de nas bskor ba bya ba dang / phyag bya ba dang / de nas yi dam gyi lha ngo shes pa dang / lha de rnams ngo bo gcig pas tha dad pa ma yin par kun shes pa dang / 
<p>151a.4</p>bdag la de rnams legs pa brjod pa'o/ /dbang la byang chub ces zhu ba dang / bskur ba gnyis las/ bskur ba la bgegs khro bos bskrad pa dang / bdag la pad sogs gdan dang / gdugs sogs rgyan dang / bskur ba ste gsum mo/ /bskur ba dngos la bum sogs slob mas
<p>151a.5</p>blang ba dang / rdo rje'i de nyid dang / dril bu'i de nyid dang / phyag rgya'i de nyid bskur ba ltar man ngag gis byin gyis brlabs la dbang blang ngo / /gsang dbang man ngag bzhin byin gyis brlab/ gtang / blang ngo / /shes rab ye shes kyang de bzhin no/ /bzhi pa yang de bzhin no/ /slob ma la dbang
<p>151a.6</p>bskur ba yang de'i rim pas te/ de yang dkyil 'khor du gzhug pa dang dbang bskur ba'o/ /gzhug pa la nang du gzhug pa dang / gsang ba bsgo ba dang / dkyil 'khor du gzhug pa'o/ /nang du gzhug pa ni las bum chus bsangs pa'i mig ras A khaM gis byin gyis brlabs la bcing ba dang / 
<p>151a.7</p>A khaM zlos su gzhug pa dang / dga' chen zhes gsol ba gdab pa dang / las kyi slob dpon gyis rdo rje dang me tog su ra ta s+t+waM/ zhes snying gar sbyin/ A khaM gis nang du gzhug /gang yin zhes dri/ nang du gzhug pa'o/ /gsang ba bsgo ba la gsum ste/ rgyud sbyang ba/ bsgo ba
<p>151b</p>
<p>151b.1</p>dngos dang ye shes dbab pa'o/ /rgyud sbyang ba la lnga ste/ thog ma zhes pa sdig pa sbyang ba dang / ut+pA da yas sems bskyed pa dang / sdom pa 'dzin du gzhug pa dang / mkha' gsang nas dbyung ba dang / bgegs bsal ba'o/ /bsgo ba dngos la bdun te/ 'dod chags chen po las byung
<p>151b.2</p>ba'i/ /'khor lo'i de nyid gzugs brnyan bzhin/ /zhes byin gyis brlab cing gnang ba nod pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis brlabs pas smrar mi gzhug pa dang / mchog gi dngos grub thob pa dang / 'di ni khyod kyi dam tshig gi rdo rje zhes rdo rjer byin gyis brlabs pa dang / 
<p>151b.3</p>rdo rje sems dpa' zhes thugs rdo rje dang / 'di ni khyod kyi dmyal ba'i zhes gsung rdo rjer byin gyis brlabs la smrar mi rung bar bsgo ba dang / de rnams slob dpon las byung bas brnyas pa ma byed par bsgo ba'o/ /ye shes dbab pa la slob mas ye shes zhu ba dang / slob ma'i ye shes dbab pa dang / 
<p>151b.4</p>babs na zhes lus ngag yid brtag pa'o/ /dkyil 'khor du gzhug pa la dgu ste/ snying po'i zhes dam bcas pa dang / 'khor lo bskor ba dang / pra ti zhes me tog dor ba dang / snang ba dri ba dang / gtsug tor la sogs pa dngos grub rab 'bring brtag pa dang / stobs po che zhes me tog
<p>151b.5</p>mgor bcing ba dang / oM rdo rje sems dpa' zhes mig dbye ba dang / ltos shig ces dkyil 'khor bstan pa dang / shar sgo nas dbus kyi bar du lha bstan pa'o/ /la la de kho na nyid 'dir ston te de ni ma yin te/ saM gra ha nas dbang bskur nas ni de nyid bstan/ gzhan du na ni dngos grub dag/ 
<p>151b.6</p>shin tu ring bar 'gyur ro zhes/ /rdo rje 'dzin pas yang dag gsungs/ /zhes pas dbang rdzogs nas 'khor lo de nyid bstan par bya'o/ /dbang bskur ba la slob dpon mnyes par bya ba dang bskur ba gnyis so/ /mnyes pa la phyi nang de nyid gsum mchod pa las phyi'i mchod pa yon
<p>151b.7</p>du lus ngag yid gsum dang bcas pa dbul ba man ngag gis so/ /nang sha lnga bdud rtsi lnga'am byin gyis brlabs la nang gi sbyin sreg tu bya'o/ /de kho na nyid ni dbang gi ye shes pas ga bur ma nyams pa'o/ /bskul ba la bum pa la sogs pa bzhi las bum pa la sbyor
<p>152a</p>
<p>152a.1</p>ba dang / dngos gnyis las sbyor ba rdo rje zhes nod pa dang / gdan bsham pa dang / rin po che la sogs pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa dang / gdugs la sogs pa bkra shis kyi rdzas dang / mchod pa bsham pa dang / til la sogs pas bgegs bskrad pa dang / 
<p>152a.2</p>phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas thams cad spyan drangs te bcug nas mchod pa dang / phun sum zhes bkra shis brjod pa'o/ /dngos la phyi nang gsang ba gsum gyis 'khor lo mchod lha mo lnga dang rigs lngar gyur te/ sangs rgyas spyan gyis las bum gyis phyi ltar zhes bkrus pas dri ma
<p>152a.3</p>rkang par bud par bsam pa dang / he ru ka dang rnam par snang mdzad kyis phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyis gsang ba gsum zhes pas gtso bo dang / shar bum bskur bas sku'i rigs thams cad dang bcas pas lus la bcug nas bdud rtsis lus rgyas te dpral bar
<p>152a.4</p>rnam snang byon pa'o/ /de nas chus bsangs te cod pan dang / thor tshugs la rin chen 'byung ldan bskyed de/ ye shes kyi 'khor lo bkug mchod bstims nas thor tshugs su gyur/ mA ma kI sa ji ltar zhes bskrus pas dri ma dang sgrib pa rkang par bud par bsam pa dang / he ru ka ra rin
<p>152a.5</p>chen 'byung ldan gyis/ phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi/ /gsang ba gsum las byung ba yis/ /zhes gtso bo dang lha mo'i bum pa thogs nas bskur bas yon tan gyi rigs thams cad dang bcas pa lus la bcud pas bdud rtsis lus brgyan te rna ltag g.yas su rin chen
<p>152a.6</p>'byung ldan du gyur pa'o/ /de bzhin du rdo rje dang bdag po dang / ming rnams la yang go bar bya'o/ /rdo rje slob dpon gyi dbang ni slob dpon kha cig 'dir 'dod mod kyi/ rje ri khrod zhabs kyis 'dir bzhi pa yan chad bskur nas so/ /de la 'dir rdo rje'i de nyid sbyin pa ni/ rdo rje la gong ltar
<p>152a.7</p>byin gyis brlabs pa rdo rjer gyur pa de tshigs bcad dang sngags kyis sbyin te/ slob ma'i lag pa g.yas su ma las nyi ma hUM gser gyi rdo rjer gyur par bsgom du bcug la de gnyis med du gzung zhes pas sbyin pa'o/ /dril bu'i de nyid kyang de bzhin nyid du byas la/ lag pa g.yon par a dang khaM
<p>152b</p>
<p>152b.1</p>las zla ba dang dril bur gyur pa dang gnyis med du sbyin no/ /thog mtha' med ces pa dang / 'di ni sangs rgyas zhes pas gsor ba dang dkrol ba gsum gsum byed du gzhug go/ /phyag rgya'i de nyid dngos sam bskyed pa yang dam tshig dang ye shes pa mchod pa dang gnyis med du gyur nas
<p>152b.2</p>sbyin no/ /rigs gang yin pa bsgom du yang gzhug go/ /de nas phyi nang de nyid kyis mchod do/ /de nas gsang dbang dang shes rab ye shes dang / bzhi pa brgyud pa'i man ngag las blang ba'o/ /de nas rjes gnang rigs lnga sbyin de nas lung bstan te/ slob dpon sku cha lugs
<p>152b.3</p>phyag rgya sngags des sangs rgyas thams cad kyis byin gyis brlab cing lung ston pa'o/ /de nas gsang ba bsgrag /de nas dbugs dbyung ba dang / de nas de nyid bstan pa'o/ /bcud du bya ba la phyag rgya bzhi'i don shes par bya ba dang / bsgom par bya ba dang / bsrung bar bya ba dang / 
<p>152b.4</p>spyad par bya ba dang bzhi'o/ /phyag rgya bzhi'i don shes par bya ba dang / dbang gi dgos pa shes par bya ba dang / rgyud kyi don dang dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga shes par bya ba'o/ /dbang gi dgos pa la bzhi/ bum pa'i dbang brtags pa/ rig pa'i lha mos bkrus pa dang / ma rig pa byang
<p>152b.5</p>nas ye shes lnga skyes pa dang / phung po la lha lngar rig pa'o/ /bum pa zlum pas dbye ba med pa chos sku 'byung ba dang / chu 'dzin pas bde ba chen po'i sku 'byung ba dang / kha khyer che bas longs sku 'byung ba dang / dri ma med pas sprul sku 'byung ba dang / bcud mgul rgyan mtshan ma gsum
<p>152b.6</p>rigs gsum gyi bdag nyid 'byung ba dang / kha rgyan gzungs thag gnyis med kyis 'gro ba 'dren pa dang / thor tshugs rigs lnga byung nas las lnga byed pa dang / cod pan gyis ngo bo gcig cing rtog pa med pa'o/ /rdo rje dril bu dang / bdag po dang ming ni dbang nas shes par bya'o/ /
<p>152b.7</p>de nyid gsum yang tshig gi don ltar nyid do/ /des lus kyi nyes pa dag sprul sku thob pa'i rten byed pa'o/ /gsang dbang gis ngag gi nyes pa dag /sangs rgyas nas brgyud pas longs sku'i rten byed pa'o/ /shes rab ye shes kyis yid kyi nyes pa dag /shes rab la brten pas
<p>153a</p>
<p>153a.1</p>bde chen sku'i rten byed pa'o/ /bzhi pas lus ngag yid gsum gyi sgrib pa dag /chos sku'i ngo bo rtogs brdas bstan te bla ma las byung bas so/ /rgyud don shes par bya ba ni lta ba ste/ 'di rab tu mi gnas pa yin te/ sems tsam du 'dod pa dang / sgyu mar 'dod pa
<p>153a.2</p>yang nyes pa med par brjod do/ /de la rgal ba bye brag tu smra ba dang / gzhan don byed ma btub na mdo sde pa theg pa chen por 'dod la sngags su cis ma btub ce na/ yul sems so sor 'dod pas zhe'o/ /'o na zla ba grags pas sgron gsal du gnyis bshad pa zhe na/ de kun
<p>153a.3</p>rdzob tu bstan zhe'o/ /'o na dngos por 'dzin pa skyon nam don dam skyon rnam pa bcas kyang zhe na/ de rnams sems su 'dod pas zhes so/ /'o na mdo sde pa rnams dang / sems tsam pa rten 'brel zer ba zhe na/ rten 'brel du 'dod pa tha dad ces so/ /rgyud kyi rgyu mtshan gzhan
<p>153a.4</p>ltar yang shes par bya ba/ 'dir rgyu'i rgyud sems can/ thabs kyi rgyud rgyud sde bzhi/ 'bras bu'i rgyud sku bzhi'o/ /de yang brgyud pas rgyud de/ sems can las brgyud pas sku bzhi/ 'brel pas rgyud/ thabs rgyu des 'brel nas ma nor bas rgyud sku bzhi 'dod pa 'byung la/ /
<p>153a.5</p>de ltar rgyu thabs dang 'bras bur brgyud nas 'brel zhing ma nor bar 'dus pas rgyud du gdags so/ /'dus pa las 'bras bu 'dus pa ni 'di lta ste/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro nas/ rgyud kyi don ni gnyis yin te/ /don dam pa dang kun rdzob bden/ /don dam brjod du mi nus te/ /kun
<p>153a.6</p>rdzob chu yi zla ltar bstan/ /zhes pas don dam la brjod du med do/ /kun rdzob la kun rdzob dngos dang / don dam la spyang du med pa'o/ /kun rdzob dngos la gnyis te/ kun rdzob la gong bzhin gnyis/ rnal 'byor pa'i yang sngags dang mtshan nyid gnyis/ sngags la yang
<p>153a.7</p>gzugs sku dang / chos sku gnyis/ chos sku la yang bde ba chen po dang / stong pa gnyis so/ /de yang kun spyod nas/ 'gro ba 'di kun sangs rgyas lnga bdag nyid/ /gar mkhan dag dang ri mo bzang ltar snang / /gang du bde chen zhes pa gcig po nyid/ /gcig po nyams ni
<p>153b</p>
<p>153b.1</p>du mas gar mdzad do/ /zhes pas so/ /des don dam brjod du med kyang / kun rdzob tu bde ba chen po'i ngo bo kho na yin la/ chos thams cad gsang sngags yin la/ gsang sngags kyis 'tshang rgya ba'o/ /de ltar na shAkya thub pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa gzhan yang sangs rgyas pa
<p>153b.2</p>sngags kyis yin par bstan la/ bskal pa grangs med gsum du pha rol tu phyin pa drug ston pas sangs rgyas so zhe na/ kun spyod nas/ rgyud rnams kun du gsang ba yang / /rgyud 'di yis ni rnal 'byor pa/ /bden pa gnyis la yang dag bsten/ /sprul pa dngos la de nyid bstan/ /
<p>153b.3</p>zhes pas bde ba chen po brjod du med pa mu bzhi dang bral te/ phyi rabs la bden gnyis zhes pha rol tu phyin par sprul skur bstan yang / sprul sku nyid sems can la sngags dang / pha rol tu phyin par snang ste/ sprul sku nyid bde ba chen po nyid do/ /snang ba de sngon du rgyu dang / rkyen song bas 'byung ste/ 
<p>153b.4</p>tsa ri ka pa bzhin mkha' ltar yas phub ces rgyu med min no/ /des na bde ba chen po yin yang sems can gyi don du pha rol tu phyin pa bstan nas bde ba chen po thob nas tshogs chung zhing sangs rgyas pa'o/ /thams cad gsang ba'i rgyud nas/ dper na sgra yi mkhan po dag /sgra yi skyon med don
<p>153b.5</p>tshol te/ /ma shes pa la ka kA dang / /ki kI dbyangs yig ston par byed/ /ces pas 'dir yang sangs rgyas thams cad bde ba chen por gnas la 'gro ba'i khyad par gyi theg pa'i rim par bstan pa'o/ /lam 'dus par bstan pa'o/ /chos kyi phung por 'dus pa yang / /chos kyi phung po
<p>153b.6</p>brgyad khri dang / /bzhi stong gi ni grangs snyed kun/ /yi ge gnyis su de bzhin 'dus/ /zhes pas gsang sngags kyang thabs gzugs sku bskyed rim dam tshig gi phyag rgya dang / las kyi phyag rgyar 'dus la/ shes rab chos sku dang bde ba chen por 'byung bas phyag rgya chen por 'dus pas so/ /
<p>153b.7</p>de yang e waM ma yA shru ta me ka smin/ zhes pa dang / 'di skad bdag gis thos pa'i dus gcig na/ zhes rgyud sde bzhi/ phyag rgya bzhi sku bzhi'o/ /de yang e las kyi phyag rgya/ 'di skad ces dngos min te las kyi phyag rgyas dpe mtshon pa'o/ /baM chos kyi phyag rgya 'di lta ste/ don chos kyi phyag
<p>154a</p>
<p>154a.1</p>rgya rnyed pa'o/ /ma phyag rgya chen po skad ces pas brdas mtshon pa'o/ /rigs pas mi rnyed pa'o/ /yA dam tshig gi phyag rgyas 'di skad ces pas sprul pa sgyu mar snang ba'o/ /de bzhin dang sgra'i stobs kyis/ shrU ta me ka smin bdag gis thos pa'i dus gcig la sbyar
<p>154a.2</p>nas d+harma kA ya/ saM b+ho ga kA ya/ nir ma Na kA ya/ ma hA su kha kA ya ni rim pa ltar chos dang / longs spyod rdzogs pa dang / sprul pa dang / bde ba chen po'i skur 'byung ba'o/ /rgyu 'dus pas sems can gyi bsam pas 'dul ba dang / theg pa chung ba kr-i yog tu 'dus la/ mngon
<p>154a.3</p>pa dang theg pa chen po nang par 'dus so/ /rdo rje phreng ba nas/ thabs chung bya mang don ring bas/ /phyi pa kr-i yog spyod lam ste/ /thabs che bya nyung don nye bas/ /de phyir nang ste bla na med/ /ces so/ /de yang drang don nges don du 'dus te/ 'jam dpal gyis zhus pa'i mdo nas/ 'og ma
<p>154a.4</p>gong du 'gro bas drang ba ste/ /ma nor de nyid 'byung bas nges pa yin/ /zhes pas de yang mtshan nyid thams cad drang don/ sangs rgyas bde ba chen por 'gro bas gsang sngags thams cad nges don/ sangs rgyas thams cad bde ba chen por gnas pas 'dul ba dang / theg pa chung ngu'i mdo drang
<p>154a.5</p>don chen po dang mngon par 'gro bas mngon pa dang / theg pa chen po'i mdo thams cad nges don/ 'gro don du nges pas 'dul ba drang don/ chung ba'i mdo sde nges don/ rgyu las dang 'bras bu ston pas pha rol tu phyin pa lnga gong du 'gro bas theg pa chen po'i drang don/ rgyu de rnams shes rab
<p>154a.6</p>kyi pha rol tu phyin par nges don no/ /rgyu las dang 'bras bur 'dod pas kr-i yog drang don/ ma nor ba'i 'bras bu nyid la spyod pas nang pa nges don/ thabs la brten nas 'gro bas pha rgyud drang don/ shes rab rgyud la gtogs pas ma rgyud nges don/ de rnams rim par brgyud pas rgyud rnams
<p>154a.7</p>drang don/ rgyud don sku bzhir nges pas nges don te/ sku bzhi sgyu ma kun rdzob yin pas drang ba'i don/ /don dam mtshon du med pas nges par shes par gyis/ /zhes mtshon pas grub med nyams dga' tsam sku bzhi 'grub par rig par bya'o/ /dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga shes par bya ba la sgra don
<p>154b</p>
<p>154b.1</p>gnyis las/ sgra la bsnyen pa dang / dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga dang / dbang bskur gyi cho ga dang / dbang bskur ba gong ltar ram/ gzhan ltar shes par bya'o/ /don gyi khyad par la nges don dang drang don du shes par bya ba dang / drang don nges don du sgrub pa la gnyis las nges don dang drang don du shes par
<p>154b.2</p>bya ba la gnyis te/ nges don ni dkyil zhes bya/ dbu ma zhes bya ba dang / ma d+h+ya ma ste/ dbu ma mu bzhi dang bral ba la/ gang mu bzhi dang bral na 'khor zhes bya/ g.yog ces bya'o/ /ka bya d+ha ra ste/ dngos por 'dzin pa mu bzhi dang bral la/ che ge zhes bya/ sgrub pa zhes bya'o/ /sA d+ha sa ha dza
<p>154b.3</p>ste/ lhan cig gdod nas gnyis med du yod par shes pa'o/ /drang don du snod du bya ba shes pa dang / bcud du bya ba la yang bsnyen pa dang dkyil 'khor cho ga dang / dbang bskur ba shes par bya'o/ /nges don dang drang don du shes par bya ba de yang dgyes pa'i rdo rje nas/ ston pa po nga chos kyang
<p>154b.4</p>nga / /nyan pa'i tshogs ldan zhu ba nga / /zhes pas de dag thams cad nges par bcom ldan 'das nyid sems can drang ba'i don du mdzad pa ste/ nyan thos dang / so so'i skye bo dang mu stegs pa rnams la ni mdo dang 'dul ba ltar yang snang ste/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams la gong ltar sdom
<p>154b.5</p>pa gsum ldan de snang ba'o/ /bsnyen pa'i dus na slob dpon gyi mtshan nyid bzhir brtag ces pa sku bzhi dang ldan pa'o/ /brgyud pa dang ldan zhes pa chos skur gnas pa'o/ /dam tshig ces pa bde ba chen po'i skur gnas pa'o/ /rgyud sde zhes pa longs skur gnas pa'o/ /gzhan don
<p>154b.6</p>zhes pa sprul skur ston pa'o/ /zhu 'bul zhes pa byang chub mchog tu sems bskyed pa'o/ /'og min du longs sku la zhu ba phul ba bum pa'i dbang bskur ba'i snang ba de rgyal po zas gtsang gi sras btsas nas khrus gsol ba na bla ma la me tog ces pa ni chos sku bde ba chen po las ma g.yos
<p>154b.7</p>par sprul sku ston pa'o/ /rdzas byams pa'i stobs phan chad kyis bsags te spos kyi glang po la sogs pa skor mang ba la phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' dang / chos skyong thams cad kyis mchod nas 'dzam bu'i gling du lung bstan pa de phyi'i mchod pa'o/ /yab yum gyi
<p>155a</p>
<p>155a.1</p>gnas su bcas nas yi ge lnga las mngon byang lngar nyams su myong ba de nang mchod do/ /de'i dus na yum gyi lhums na bzhugs pa de de kho na'i mchod pa'o/ /yab yum gyi skor spos kyi glang po la sogs par snang ba de chos skyong la gtor ma ster ba'o/ /rigs bzhi la nor
<p>155a.2</p>zas kyi sbyin pa gtong bar snang ba de slob ma yongs su skyob pa yin la/ dmangs la nye ring med par pha rol tu phyin pa drug tu spyod par snang ba de dang gzhan rjes su smon pa de gnyis ka slob dpon las sdom pa len pa'o/ /sku skyo nas grong khyer du 'chag pa la skye rga la sogs pa'i snang ba mthong
<p>155a.3</p>ba la de 'khor ba la yi mug par ston pa de so so thar pa'i bslab pa srung ba'o/ /de'i dus su rgyal bu ming sring phan chad sbyin pa byas pa'i snang ba de theg pa chen po'i sdom pa srung ba'o/ /yum las bltams par snang ba de mkha' gsang byin gyis brlab pa'o/ /rgyal rigs dang bram
<p>155a.4</p>ze'i rigs che bas bstod pa'i snang ba de rgyu gang bsnyen gyi sngags zlo ba'o/ /rdzas kyi bye brag la ma chags pa'i snang ba de/ dpa' bo dga' ston byed pa'o/ /de nas khyim spong zhes yab yum la zhu ba'i snang ba de sangs rgyas 'das pa la zhu ba'o/ /maN+Dal gong ltar ro/ /longs sku la zhu
<p>155a.5</p>ba'i snang ba de slob dpon/ shes pa la zhu ba de 'das pa'i sangs rgyas so/ /brgyud pa zhes pa 'das pa'i sangs rgyas de yang sku bzhi dang ldan pa'o/ /der rgyal srid gzung ba'i snang ba de rdzas kyis lha bsnyen pa'o/ /rgyal po chen po bzhis bteg pa'i snang ba de rnal 'byor bzhis lha
<p>155a.6</p>bsnyen pa'o/ /dpal lha las babs pa'i rtser phyin pa'i snang ba de chos skyong bsnyen pa'o/ /mchod rten la mkhan po byas pa dang / bcom ldan 'das nyid las med la/ sdom pa len pa'i rjod byed gtso bo dang 'khor la bsnyen pa'o/ /dbu skra nyid kyis bzhar ba'i snang ba de yi
<p>155a.7</p>ge brgya pas mtshams sbyar ba'o/ /der chos gos dang khyim pa'i rtags spangs shing sdom pa dang ldan pa'i snang ba de bsnyen pa'i rtags/ mtshan ma grangs kyi bsnyen pa sngon du skyel ba'o/ /de nas shar du ma ga d+hAr byon pa'i snang ba de dkyil 'khor gyi sa bslang ba'o/ /de yang mis ma mthong bar
<p>155b</p>
<p>155b.1</p>nyid snang ba la 'khor gyis bskor zhes grags pa ting nge 'dzin dang ldan pa'o/ /shar du gzigs nas byon pa'i snang ba de sangs rgyas zhi bas sgrub pa'o/ /thams cad spangs par snang ba de dben pa btsal ba'o/ /phi li par pa tar bzhugs pa'i snang ba de phyi rabs la brtags pa
<p>155b.2</p>dgos par bstan pa'o/ /bram ze mo bzang ldan la dris nas bram ze ga ya las g.yar ba de bdag po la bslang ba'o/ /lha ma yin gyis bar chod byed par bsgrags pa de bdag po dngos snang ba med pa la bslang ba'o/ /bar ma chod par snang ba de rnal 'byor ba zhis gzung ba'o/ /sa'i lha mo sku
<p>155b.3</p>stod bton pa de dpang du gsol ba'o/ /der 'gyur ba mang du snang ba de ji tsam 'dod pa thugs kyis bcad pa'o/ /de'i zur bzhir rdo rje phur pa bzhi btab ste khro bos mtshams bsrung ba'o/ /lhung bzed bsgyur bas sa la thim pa'i snang ba des gtar bcug pa'o/ /klu u bi ka gnyid sad pa
<p>155b.4</p>la lhung bzed du shes nas nyal ba'i snang ba de/ sa bdag ma dga' nas sa gta' ma chags pa'o/ /bdud rnams kyi mda' mtshon me tog tu song ba'i snang ba de gtor mas lan chags 'jal zhing bar chad zlog pa'o/ /rgyal po bzhis bzhengs par bskul ba'i snang ba de slob ma rigs
<p>155b.5</p>bzhis bskul ba'o/ /bzhengs nas spyan bltas pas bdud mo rnams 'dod pas steg par mthong ste/ spyan g.yas pa bstan nas se gol gtogs pas rgan mor song ba'i snang ba de spyan g.yas pa'i Ta las nyi ma bskal ba'i me ltar sreg pa'o/ /'gyod nas bdud mos gus pa phul bas
<p>155b.6</p>sngar bzhin song ba'i snang ba de spyan g.yon pa a las zla ba'i 'od kyis snying rjes nyams pa gsos pa'o/ /de nas dbang ldan nas phur pa'i mtshams nas phyogs bzhir g.yas skor du byang chub shing la dbyangs dang ldan pas lan gsum bskor bas rdo rje la sogs pa bzhi zhabs rjes la byung ba'i
<p>155b.7</p>snang ba de/ rdo rje brkyang bskum gyi dra gur du byas pa'o/ /dbyangs rak+Sha ste/ rdo rje'i mda'i dra bar gyur pa'o/ /rdo rje'i gdan mi 'gyur zhes grags pa de/ de ltar bsrung ba'i byin rlabs dang bsam pa'o/ /sa yul de phyogs gzhan pas mtho bar grags pa de tshad ldan du brtsigs pa la
<p>156a</p>
<p>156a.1</p>sogs pa'o/ /shin tu dri zhim zhing nyams dga' ba de dri dang ba'i rnam lngas byug pa'o/ /sa'i lha mo de nyid du thim pa'i snang ba de sa'i lha mo lhag par gnas pa'o/ /byang chub kyi shing de sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rten yin pa'i snang ba de me tog bkod pa'o/ /'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa
<p>156a.2</p>kun gyi yang rten pa'i yang rten zhes grags pa'i snang ba de lha grangs kyi me tog bkod pa'o/ /byang chub kyi shing las 'od zer byung nas sangs rgyas thams cad kyis byin gyis brlabs par grags pa de maN+Dal bkod pa la rnal 'byor bzhis bskyed pa'o/ /de la sangs rgyas kyi tshigs bcad bzhi
<p>156a.3</p>'don pa'i snang ba de 'khor lo dang / gzhan la gsol ba gdab pa'o/ /des 'khor gyi mu stegs kun dga' nas yi rang ba de chos kyis skyong ba gsol ba gdab pa'o/ /'od zer de sangs rgyas pa'i snang ba de 'khor lo mkhan la brten pa'o/ /phyogs skyong bzhis bum pa phul ba'i snang ba de
<p>156a.4</p>bum pa sta gon no/ /bum pa gcig tu byin gyis brlabs pa'i snang ba de dkar pos byugs pa'o/ /khong rang gis so sor mthong la gzhan gyis gcig tu mthong ba'i snang ba de rin po che dang sa las byas pa'o/ /byin gyis brlabs pas mdzes shing che ba'i snang ba de mu stegs kyis spangs pa'o/ /
<p>156a.5</p>tshangs pa la sogs pas rang rang gi nor gyis dogs pas mtshan ma btab pa de mtshan ma btab pa'o/ /phyi dro gsol du ma rung nas ras bkang nas ku sha'i khar gzhag pa'i snang ba de mgul chings dang gdan la gzhag pa'o/ /khyim bdag gi bu mos 'o ma drangs pa yang der blugs pa'i snang ba de
<p>156a.6</p>bcud blugs pa'o/ /de blugs pas byang chub kyi shing gi gzugs der shar ba'i snang ba de lha bskyed pa'o/ /de las blangs pa byung nas/ byang chub kyi shing la phog pas 'dab ma gcig der lhung ba'i snang ba de ye shes kyi lha spyan drangs pa'o/ /de la kun ngo mtshar skyes nas mchod pa'i snang ba de spyan
<p>156a.7</p>drangs pa de la mchod pa'o/ /bcom ldan 'das kyis na mo bud+hA ya/ zhes brjod nas shing lo der bcug nas thams cad 'o mar gyur te gzhag pa'i snang ba de lha mchod bsnyen bsgrub tu zhu ba'o/ /de la kun dga' nas spro la sangs rgyas nyid kyang dgyes pa'i snang ba de sta gon la 'jug pas dga'
<p>156b</p>
<p>156b.1</p>ba'o/ /bcom ldan 'das kyis bkyed nas shing la gzigs pa'i snang ba de dga' chen zhus pa'o/ /shing las yang 'od zer byung bas bcom ldan 'das dang bum pa la phog pa'i snang ba de bu tshur zhes pa dang / bum pa sngags kyi gzungs thag gdags pa'o/ /sangs rgyas kyis na mo bud+hA ya/ na mo d+harmA ya/ 
<p>156b.2</p>na maHsaM g+hA ya/ zhes brjod pas phyogs skyong la sogs pas phyag byas pa dang / nerany+dza na'i nya che chung dang phrad cing mu stegs rnams 'khor du gyur pa'i snang ba des sangs rgyas sprul pa'i sku ste/ de ltar snang ba dang / rgyal po'i khab bya rgod phung po'i ri la shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa gsung
<p>156b.3</p>pa dang / shrI da na pha rgyud gsungs pa la sogs pa gcig yin pas sangs rgyas rdo rje sems dpa'i rnam 'phrul rgyud re re nyid la chos rgyud ltar la de ltar yo gsungs pa yo rgyud do/ /dge 'dun 'khor de yo 'khor lo'i lhar ston pa nyid do/ /gong na ston pa po zhes pas so/ /de ltar yang ldan sngags
<p>156b.4</p>su shes pas thams cad sangs rgyas 'jig rten na bzhugs pa dang / thams cad chos ltar gyur pas srog mi gcod pa dang / thams cad grogs dang dge 'dun yin pas phyir mi ldog pa'i yon tan ston pa'o/ /de nas sangs rgyas 'khor rnam bzhi la rang rang gi spyod lam gyis chos ston
<p>156b.5</p>pa rigs kyi sdom pa 'dzin pa'o/ /klu kha la me 'bar gyis sangs rgyas bsdigs pas sangs rgyas kyi sku las me dpung dpag tu med pas klu byed pa de zhi sogs kyi sbyin sreg byed pa'o/ /rtswa ku sha la mnyel bso ba de mkha' gsang byin gyis brlabs pa'o/ /tshangs pas me tog gtor ba
<p>156b.6</p>dang / mchod pa'i snang ba de mchod pa'i gnas su mdzad pa'o/ /pad+ma'i skud pa g.yas kyi dpung pa la bcings pas rlung zhi ba dang / khyim bdag gi bu mo'i g.yon la btags pas rlung zhi ba'i snang ba de srung skud g.yon du btags pa'o/ /khyim bdag gi bu mos 'o thug gi lhung bzed
<p>156b.7</p>blangs nas drangs pas gsol ba'i lhag ma 'khor la byin pa'i snang ba de gtor ma gtong ba'o/ /zhal du tshems shing gis dri ma phyis nas dor bas n+ya gro d+har gyur pa de so shing dor ba'o/ /ku sha sngon du bor bas snga phyir byin gyis brlabs nas/ stan byas pa'i snang ba de ku sha'i sngas la gtso bo'i sngags
<p>157a</p>
<p>157a.1</p>btab pa dang / stan la sngags kyis btab pa gding ba'o/ /yo bskrad nas byang chub kyi shing la dbu gtad nas g.yas sa la phab nas gzims par snang ba de lus ngag yid tha mal min pas 'khor lo mgo gtad seng ge'i nyal stabs su gzims pa'o/ /srod
<p>157a.2</p>la bdud kyis sprul pa byas pa las/ 'od zer sku las byung ba'i snang ba de rmi lam ngan pa bzlog pa'o/ /lha mo rnams kyi mchod pa bzhes nas mnyes pa'i snang ba de rmi lam bzang nas mnyes pa'o/ /de nas shing drung du gshegs pas sku las 'od lnga byung ba'i snang ba de thig
<p>157a.3</p>skud lnga bkal ba'o/ /'od tshur 'dus byang chub shing las 'od lnga byung ba ni thig skud snod du bcug nas lha lnga bskyed pa'o/ /'od des phyogs bcur khyab nas sangs rgyas thams cad bkug pa'i snang ba de ye shes kyi lha bkug pa'o/ /phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas byon nas nam
<p>157a.4</p>mkha'i mdun na bzhugs pa la mchod nas shing la bzhugs pa'i snang ba de thig skud kyi lha mchod nas thig skud du byas pa'o/ /shin tu bsal nas sangs rgyas gnas su gshegs pa'i snang ba de thig btab nas skud pa bsal ba'o/ /tshon yang de bzhin du 'od lnga po phyogs kyi snang ba
<p>157a.5</p>tshig lnga'i rgyu 'od lnga phyogs nas spros/ phyogs phyogs su thim/ phyogs phyogs su gsal/ rigs lngar grags pa dang / bcom ldan 'das nyid dbus na gnas pa'i snang ba de lha bskyed bkug mchod bsams bkye gsal bdag gi ting nge 'dzin gyis gtso bor gsal bas
<p>157a.6</p>bsrung ba'o/ /'od zer gyi snang ba la 'khor gyi rtogs tshad ni pra brtags pa'o/ /byang chub kyi shing gi shar nas gzigs pa'i zhabs rjes yod pa de dkyil 'khor du bcug pa'i bye brag /lho phyogs su ku sha'i stan la bzhugs pa dang / shar gyi zhabs rjes la bkra shis rdzas
<p>157a.7</p>brgyad mnga' ba'i snang ba de dbang stegs la gdugs stsogs kyis mchod pa'o/ /sku la me dpung phyung bas bdud dang mu stegs byed bros pa'i snang ba de bgegs bskrad phyir sbyin sreg dang til bsngags pa'o/ /byang phyogs su gshegs pas pad+ma bcu gsum byung ba de dbang la bum pa
<p>157b</p>
<p>157b.1</p>dang / cod pan dang / rdo rje dang / bdag po dang / ming dang / de nyid dang / gsang dbang dang / shes rab ye shes dang / bzhi pa dang / rjes su gnang ba dang / lung bstan pa dang / gsang ba bsgrags pa dang / dbugs dbyung bar bskur ba'o/ /byang chub kyi shing la zla ba gcig tu
<p>157b.2</p>gzigs pa'i snang ba de dkyil 'khor dang / lha'i de kho na nyid lta ba'o/ /nub nas shar du gzigs nas 'od zer bkye ba'i snang ba de dbang rdzogs pas 'gro don byed par shes pa'o/ /lha'i dbang pos ze'u lnga pa phul bas dbu la gsol ba'i snang ba de rig pa'i dbang lnga thob pa'o/ /
<p>157b.3</p>tshangs pas gseg shang dang par bu phul ba phyag g.yas g.yon du gzung ba'i snang ba de rdo rje dang dril bu'i de nyid thob pa'i rtags/ sgrol mas chos gos gsol ba'i snang ba de phyag rgya'i de nyid thob pa'i rtags/ legs skyes mas 'o thug drangs pa gsol nas sku gser du gyur pa de gsang
<p>157b.4</p>dbang thob pa'i rtags/ legs skyes mas sbyin len nor la ston pas gsungs pa de shes rab ye shes thob pa'i rtags/ me long sgra sogs phul ba la ltas sogs byas nas slar gtad pa de bzhi pa thob pa'i rtags/ lha tshangs pas gser gyi 'khor lo phul ba de rjes gnang thob pa'i
<p>157b.5</p>rtags/ de ltar phul yang chos ma gsungs pas nam mkha' la sangs rgyas thams cad mngon sum du mthong nas khyod mngon par rdzogs nas sangs rgyas pas chos ston zhes pa de lung bstan to/ /mya ngan las 'das par bzhed pa la/ tshangs pas zhus pa de gsang ba bsgrags pa'i
<p>157b.6</p>rtags/ de nas shAkya'i rigs shing gi lho phyogs su rab tu byung ba'i snang ba de dbugs phyin pa'i rtags/ de nas bya ba gtong gsungs pa de dkyil 'khor gyi de nyid go ba'i rtags/ bcud du bya ba la phyag rgya bzhi nges don dang drang don du shes par bya ba la yang bzhi ste/ dam tshig gi phyag rgya
<p>157b.7</p>shes par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas de chos gos la sogs par btang ba 'byor pa'i tshogs sogs pa'o/ /po ka rir sku khrus mdzad nas mya ngan las 'da' bar bzhed pa la tshangs pas gsol ba yan chad gdams pas tshogs bsag pa'o/ /rgyal po bzhis chos ston drangs pa bzhes nas
<p>158a</p>
<p>158a.1</p>gcig tu byas tshogs pa la bkye bas tshad med bzhi bstan/ thams cad bzhag nas shing drung du gshegs nas bdud skyes pas bsrung ba'i grwa gur yan chad bstan to/ /shing la sku brten nas zhal shar du gzigs pas mngon byang lnga las rgyu'i rdo rje 'chang sbyor dang po'i
<p>158a.2</p>rnal 'byor ro/ /sku de las 'od phyogs bzhir spros slar 'dus te shing gi zil pa dbu gtsug la phog pas thugs mnyam par gnas pa de rgyu'i rdo rje 'chang zhu ba go la/ sgrol ma la sogs pa lha mo bzhis bskul bas de las bzhengs nas sgrol ma la sogs pa la bltas te/ lha mo
<p>158a.3</p>bzhis bskul nas rdo rje 'chang bzhengs pa go ste rjes kyi rnal 'byor ro/ /sku las 'od byung phyogs bcur spros pas sangs rgyas thams cad mdun du snang bar gyur nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi sku la thim pa de 'khor lo rdzogs par bskyed pa ste/ rdzogs pa'i rnal 'byor ram/ dkyil
<p>158a.4</p>'khor rgyal mchog tu go ba'o/ /de nas thugs ka nas 'od 'phros nas snang bas khyab nas slar thim pa de ye shes sems dpa' bcug pa'o/ /de nas dbang po rnams nas 'od byung snang bar byas slar 'dus skye mched byin gyis brlabs pa'o/ /yang mdzod spu dang / ljags dang / thugs
<p>158a.5</p>ka nas de bzhin du rim gyis 'od 'phros slar bsdus pa de sku gsung thugs byin gyis brlabs pa'o/ /gtsug nas 'od byung nas snang ba ni dbang bskur ba'o/ /khyim bdag gi bu mos yang 'o thug drangs pa ma gsol bar mdun du gzhag pas sku gsal bar gyur pa de bdud rtsi myang ba'o/ /
<p>158a.6</p>'on kyang thugs ka nas 'phros 'dus lha mi'i tshogs kyis mchod pa byed de phyi nang gsang ba'i mchod par go la/ de nas tshangs pa la sogs pas bstod par go ba'o/ /de nas 'od zer de thams cad sku la thim nas gnas pa bskyed pa rdzogs par go'o/ /de ltar mnyam par gnas pa de dam
<p>158a.7</p>tshig gi phyag rgyar bsgom par go/ /las kyi phyag rgya nges don dang drang don du shes par bya ba ni de ltar gnas pa shing la sku rgyab gtad par a wa d+hU tre+e la dbugs yod la sa la ba na yod pa'o/ /rtsa ba me rlung la zug pa yang / rtsa de'i zhabs go ba'o/ /rtse mo lho nub tu 'ong zhing zil pa 'bab pa de
<p>158b</p>
<p>158b.1</p>bdud rtsir sa nA g.yas nas 'bab pa'o/ /yan lag byang chub na yar 'ong ba la la nA'o/ /yal ga phra la mang ba de rtsa phran mang po'o/ /dud de lo ma brje ba de nyon mongs ye shes su song ba'o/ /me tog nub mo gsal ba kun la gsang ba'o/ /'bras bu phra zhing shing la thang chu med pa ni ro nyams su
<p>158b.2</p>myong zhing nyon mongs pa med pa'o/ /sku de grib ma la zhugs bde mi spong ba'o/ /chos kyi phyag rgya'i nges don dang drang don du shes par bya ba ni sku drang por zhal shar du gzigs nas bzhugs pa de brgyud pa'i man ngag yod cing nyams su lon pa'o/ /phyag gnyis sa gnon dang mnyam pa
<p>158b.3</p>nyid ni rten 'brel thabs shes rab mnyam gzhag dang rjes thob tu bsgom pa'o/ /spyan sna rtser gtad pa de dpes don mtshon cing rnyed pa'o/ /zhabs rdo rje skyil krung du bzhugs pa de ye shes go zhing gdeng dang ldan pa'o/ /phyag rgya chen po sku mi snang bar mdzad nas 'od dang sprul pas kun du
<p>158b.4</p>khyab pa'o/ /de yang dam tshig gi phyag rgya ci dgos she na/ 'byor pa dang / gdams pas bsod nams kyi tshogs bsag pa ni rgyu las 'bras bu 'byung bas sangs rgyas ltar sprul sku 'byung ngo / /de yang tshad med bzhi dang ye shes kyi tshogs sogs pas ma nyams shing 'byung ba'o/ /
<p>158b.5</p>de gnyis rgyu bsod nams med na mi 'byung bas de'i rgyu'i dus so/ /'bras bu rten dang brten pa sangs rgyas re re'i snang ba de bsrungs pas bdud med pa'o/ /de yang stong pas 'chi bdag bcom/ /mes nyon mongs bcom/ dra gur gyis phung po bcom/ khro bos lha'i bu'i bdud
<p>158b.6</p>bcom/ de ltar bdud med pas gzhal yas khang ji tsam 'dod par rang rang gis bstan pa'o/ /mngon byang lnga las sku bzhengs pa sprul sku/ pha dang ma'i si la dang ga pur zla nyi hUM zlum po/ 'phro 'du'i tshogs kyi rgyu mthun de las sku bzhengs pa sngon stong pa yi ge lngar byas pa 'og min
<p>158b.7</p>las chad pa mi 'dod pa thams cad rang gi sems su 'dod pas 'jig rten pa'i snang ba la pha ma las rang gi mngon byang lnga las sku byung ba'o/ /zhu nas bskul bas bskyed pas 'dod chags 'dul ba dang bskul nas yab yum bzhengs pa/ zhu bar gyur pa mi rtog pa/ bzhengs pa
<p>159a</p>
<p>159a.1</p>'gro ba gdul byar bya ba gzhan mdzad pa'o/ /dkyil 'khor rdzogs pa sras bltams pa'o/ /ye shes sems dpa' bkug bcug gnyis med dgyes pa/ bdag dang sangs rgyas thams cad ngo bo gcig pa/ dus mi nyams pas bkug pa/ tha dad med
<p>159a.2</p>pas bcug la/ mi rtog pas gnyis med byas pa'o/ /'gro don nus pas mnyes pa'o/ /skye mched la mngon shes 'byung ba'o/ /rigs gsum 'dus na 'dul bas sku gsum byin gyis brlab pa'o/ /sangs rgyas la dbye ba med cing mi rtog pas dbang ngo / /bde ba chen por
<p>159a.3</p>gnas pas bdud rtsi myang ba'o/ /'jig rten pa thams cad kyis shAkya thub pa la sogs pa mchod pa'o/ /sems can 'dren pas bstod pa'o/ /mi rtog pa'i rang bzhin gyi ngo bos rdzogs rim mo/ /yang na de ltar byas pas ye shes sems dpa' la sogs pa la sems
<p>159a.4</p>can gyi snang bas rdo rje gdan du 'od la sogs pa gong bzhin shes par bya'o/ /gsang sngags bzhin byas pas sgyu ma sogs kyis da ltar bsgom pa de ltar bskyed par shes par bya'o/ /'dir rab tu mi gnas pas byang chub sems dpa'i snang ba la brten nas brten pa'i rnal 'byor
<p>159a.5</p>par snang ba sems la rdo rje gdan ltar snang ba'o/ /de yang las kyi phyag rgya'i rtsa yod pas sangs rgyas thams cad kyi lam rgyab na gnas pas sangs rgyas thams cad kyis brten pa/ me rlung yod pas thabs dgos pa la la nA dang ra sa nA sangs rgyas/ dgos pa spyi bo nas 'bab
<p>159a.6</p>pa sangs rgyas rgyud pa'i gsung gi ye shes thob pa dang nyams su myong ba'o/ /rtsa bran dang nyon mongs pa med pa la sogs pa longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku byung ba dngos/ chos kyi phyag rgya'i bde ba chen po gnas pa la sku gnyis 'byung ba dang / pha rol tu phyin pa'i lugs gong gi ltar rdo rje
<p>159a.7</p>gdan du byung ba'o/ /phyag rgya chen pos sku gdod nas mu bzhi dang bral ba de rnams 'byung zhing de nyid yin par pha rol tu phyin pa'i gong ltar mi snang ba 'od du gyur pa'o/ /de yang sprul sku shAkya thub pa dang / he ru ka sems can gyi snang ba longs skur byang chub sems dpa'i snang ba/ 
<p>159b</p>
<p>159b.1</p>bde ba chen po rang gi bde ba myong ba chos kun la khyab pa'o/ /drang don dang nges don du bsgrub pa la snod bsgrub pa dang bcud bsgrub pa'o/ /snod bsgrub pa ni rdo rje mkha' 'gro nas/ /lus nyid dkyil 'khor dag tu bsgrub/ /'bras bu de las 'byung ba'o/ /bsnyen pa gong 'og ltar
<p>159b.2</p>bsgrubs te/ /zhes 'byung ba dkyil 'khor cho ga las btsal ba bsod nams kyi tshogs sogs pa/ brtag pa ye shes kyi tshogs bsags pa/ bslang ba gzhal yas khang dang rgyu bskyed pa/ 'bras bu rdzogs pa ye shes bcug pa'o/ /gzung ba skye mched nas bstod pa yan chad
<p>159b.3</p>do/ /bcad pa phung po khams dang skye mched la sogs pa gang 'dod gdod nas yod pa'o/ /sbyang ba rnam dag shes pa'o/ /rtsig pa lus gru bzhir byung bas phung por chags pa'o/ /thig 'khor lo bzhi la sogs pa'i rtsa/ tshon ga pur snang bas khrag 'bab pa'o/ /rkyen gnas
<p>159b.4</p>snying dbus na/ ming yang a wa d+hU tI gzugs yi ge hUM/ lha gtso bo/ dbyibs thig le/ ngo bo khu ba/ las can gyi rgyu sems kyi 'phrul pa/ bde ba'i rang bzhin mi rtog pa/ nyams stong pa'i ngang / rtogs pa dang ldan pas phun sum tshogs pa lnga dang / sku bzhi de las 'byung bas
<p>159b.5</p>gnas brgyan la/ mi rtag pa'i 'khor ba de las so/ /byang chub kyi phyogs kyi chos sum cu rtsa bdun/ pha rol tu phyin pa drug/ /stong pa bco brgyad yin la/ mngon byang lnga las 'khor lo byung ba'o/ /ma rtogs pa 'khor ba'i gzugs sogs dang / khrag dang khu ba la sogs pa
<p>159b.6</p>sems can gyi lus 'byung ba'o/ /dbang bsgrub pa rgyud ltar man ngag gi rtsa dang rlung dang me bsgom pa dkyil 'khor gyi sta gon no/ /nyams su myong ba'i sgrub pa'o/ /rang las byung ba'i dkyil 'khor du bcug pa mthong ba'o/ /lus rgya nas 'byung bas mi gnod pa bum dbang thob lus kyi
<p>159b.7</p>nyes pa dag pa'o/ /spyi bo nas babs pas gsang dbang thob ngag gi nyes pa dag pa'o/ /yid mnyam par gzhag pas dbang gsum pa thob yid kyi nyes pa dag pa'o/ /thams cad de ltar rtogs pas lus ngag gi nyes pa zhi dbang bzhi thob pa'o/ /bcud bsgrub pa la phyag rgya bzhi'i tshul dang / 
<p>160a</p>
<p>160a.1</p>drang don nges don du bsgrub pa la theg pa che chung gnyis/ chung ba'i skyabs dkon mchog gsum zhes pa gong du bstan pa'i he ru ka phyi nang yor snang ba de dang / rgyud 'khor lor gyur pas so/ /mchod pa dngos po thams cad lhar shes pa'o/ /dus shes pa de nyid do/ /yon tan
<p>160a.2</p>de ltar gnas pas so/ /thams cad lhar gsal bas dge 'dun dang 'grogs/ /lha la lhas srog mi gcod pa bdag nyid lha yin na phyag gang la 'tshal te mi nyams pa'o/ /rten gzhan slob dpon yi dam lha spyi khyad par 'phags pa drug 'gro drug dang bye brag bdun las byung ba'o/ /slob
<p>160a.3</p>dpon pas lhag pa med/ sngags las lhag pa'i chos med/ /rigs lnga'i sdom pa las lhag pa med pas 'grub pa'o/ /so so thar pa'i ris bdun dag pa'o/ /rtsa ba tshad med pa bzhi/ rang bzhin ye shes kyi tshogs/ yan lag rnam par snang mdzad gzhal yas khang rten dang bcas pa lha gtso
<p>160a.4</p>bor brten pa'o/ /rtsa ba bzhi dang yan lag bzhi ste/ brgyad gzhal yas khang dur khrod brgyad dang bcas pa'o/ /srog mi gcod pa dang / rtsa ba gsum sa bon phyag 'tshal 'phros 'dus gcig tu gyur pas yongs su rdzogs pa'i sku bzhengs pa'o/ /chang dang lha bsrung ba mngon byang lnga las grub
<p>160a.5</p>pa'o/ /khyim pa'i rtags spangs pas sangs rgyas kyi sku gsal bar bsgom pa/ rab tu byung ba'i rtags rdo rje pad+ma byin gyis brlabs pa/ mu stegs kyi rtags spangs pa ye shes kyi 'khor lo gzhug pa/ sangs rgyas pa'i rtags bsgrubs pa bdud rtsi zhal du zhugs pa/ dge ba'i rtags spangs pa bsgrub
<p>160a.6</p>pa dge ba'i rtags 'khor lo lngar gyur pa'o/ /rtsa ba bzhi dang yan lag bdun sngon du tshad med bzhi bdun dag pa bsags pas lha mo bzhi 'byung ba'o/ /chang glu zhes pa glus bskul ba'o/ /dge slong gi rtsa ba bzhi blangs pa'o/ /lhag ma bcu gsum gyis yab yum gyi sku rdzogs par bsgom pa'o/ /ma
<p>160a.7</p>nges pa la sogs pa'i sdom pa drug yab kyi thugs kyi sa bon dang / yum gyi thugs ka'i sa bon gsal ba dang / sa bon de spro ba dang / rigs kyi thugs dam bskul ba dang / las sbyang ba dang / gnyis med du spyan drang ba dang / yi ge lnga dang 'dres nas zhu ba dang / zhal du zhugs pa dang / rtsa rnams
<p>160b</p>
<p>160b.1</p>nas babs pa dang / bsrubs pa dang / gzhal yas khang bskyed pa dang / gtso bo la sogs pa'i gdan bskyed pa dang / gtso bo dang / 'khor bskyed pa dang / gtso bo dang rigs lnga'i las byas nas gzhag pa'o/ /rtsa ba lnga zhes pa 'khor lo rdzogs par bsgom pa rgyu 'bras mngon byang lnga
<p>160b.2</p>las bskyed pa'o/ /rtsa ba'i sbyor ba dbang ma bskur ba/ dngos ma mnyan pa/ mjug ma bsgoms pa'o/ /de gsum ka med pa las nyan thos kyi sdom pa med na nyams pa chen po'o/ /ma mnyam pa sgom na nyams pa sbom po'o/ /dbang med par nyams pa chung ngu'o/ /ma mnyan na nyams pa sgom
<p>160b.3</p>po'o/ /dbang dang bsgom pa med na phra mo'o/ /gcig las med na ltung byed do/ /yan lag bsod nams kyi tshogs dang rnal 'byor bzhi rdzogs rim sbyor ba dngos mjug go/ /de'i nyes pa yang gong bzhin no/ /rtsa ba'i nyes pa dbang sdom pa dang / bslab pa gsum char blangs na sbom
<p>160b.4</p>po/ /mnyan la bsgoms nas chung ngu byung ba dbang bskur ba ma nyan/ phra mo dang dbang bskur la bsgom/ ltung byed re re med pa blang / /nyes pa la sogs gang spyad de bslang pa'o/ /de yang dbang dang slob dpon la tshogs dbul ba dang / maN+Dal gyis bshags/ /phyin mi byed par bsdams pas
<p>160b.5</p>thub pa'o/ /chang zhes pa bdud rtsi myang ba dang / ga bur ma shor ba'o/ /gtang sems zhes pa sngags gzhag pa'o/ /rgas zhes pa ma nus pa'o/ /bsnyen gnas zhes pa ye shes sems dpa' gzhug pa dang / skye mched dang sku gsung thugs byin gyis brlab pa dang / dbang bdud rtsi bzhi
<p>160b.6</p>dang / dge bsnyen bzhi dang / dge tshul dang dge slong chos bstod pa ste/ skabs zhes pa long yod na legs par bcos/ med na bsgom bya'o/ /bcos thabs nges par bskyed ces pa/ de ltar shes pa'i sngags pa la 'dul ba'i rtsa ba yan lag re re mi gnod/ thabs des slar gsos pas thob bo/ /
<p>160b.7</p>sngon yang sangs rgyas kyang he ru ka dang / rgyud ston par 'khor la snang la/ 'khor yang sdom pa gsum dang ldan pa'o/ /des nyams pa bcos su btub sngags gtso bo'o/ /des na sngags sgrub pa la blo skyed cing brtson par bya'o/ /dus nges zhes sngags las/ in+d+ra b+hU ti dang / Dom+bi la sogs pa
<p>161a</p>
<p>161a.1</p>ltar phrad ma thog dang / rang zhig dang / nges pa med par thob la/ ma grub bar du ngan 'gror mi skye bas ji srid do/ /yon tan yang yi dgas ston pa'i rgyud nas/ dam tshig phyag rgya legs bsgoms na/ /rnal 'byor pa yis gzugs gnyis 'thob/ /ces pas mi'i nang nas
<p>161a.2</p>bram zer skye la/ ngo tsha shes pa dang khrel yod pas sdom pa gsum yang des thub cing sku bzhi yang de las byung ba'o/ /yon tan che ba la sogs pa de ltar gnas pa'o/ /thob nas dbang thob mnyan bsgoms bsod nams kyi tshogs bsags rnal 'byor bzhi rdzogs rim zhes bsgoms pas de nyid
<p>161a.3</p>na'o/ /de ltar yon tan shes na gsum la skyabs su 'gro ba dang / lus ngag yid kyi sdig pa bshags la/ chos 'gro ba'i don du sna tshogs spyod kyang rang nyid sngags don shes pas gzhan du byed pa'o/ /sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyang nyid la rtog pa med par gzhan la
<p>161a.4</p>don mdzad pa'o/ /gso sbyong zhes pa gong ltar sbyor ba dngos mjug la dus thams cad dam dus khyad par can rgyud nas don bstan pa la spyod pa'o/ /dus mchog dang thun mong zhag zla ba na yang 'ong ba'o/ /chos zhes pa bdag gis gong ltar nyes pas 'gro don du lus ngag yid kyis de rnams
<p>161a.5</p>su ha cang ches te/ 'byor nus yod na lha khang la sogs pa bzhengs shing gso ba dang / rgyud dang mdo dang / 'dul ba dang / mngon pa dang / bstan bcos bri ba dang / mchod par bya'o/ /ma 'byor na yang yid kyis spyod lam bzhi la mi dog pas thun bzhir nyams su blang bar bya'o/ /theg pa
<p>161a.6</p>chen po'i yang skyabs pa'i yon tan gong ltar sangs rgyas sprul sku de he ru ka'i bzhu btul spro bsdu yod pa yin zhing chos kyang sems las shes pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yin la/ dge 'dun yang rang la yod pas 'khor lo/ /de ltar shes pas thams cad rang bzhin gyis don
<p>161a.7</p>sangs rgyas kyi las yin na/ sbyor dngos mjug gong ltar dang / de ltar yang mthar thug dpung bzang ngo / /shes rab dang / las dang / smon lam dang / sngon gyi skal ba la ma rmongs pas de ltar spyad pa shes par bya'o/ /blo de ltar med pa la sogs pas re re 'dra bas spyad de/ phan
<p>161b</p>
<p>161b.1</p>sems dang dam tshig thub na byang chub kyi phyogs dang sngags 'grub bo/ /phyag rgya bzhi'i tshul du drang don dang / nges don du bsgrub pa la yang bzhi ste/ dam tshig gi phyag rgya bsgrub pa'i yon tan de ltar shes pas spyad dgos pa dang / zhen pa rnams snying rje bar mthong zhing bya ba btang ba
<p>161b.2</p>'byor ba'i tshogs yin la/ dge ba ci byas pa thams cad sems can gyi ched du sangs rgyas su bsngo zhing / bdun dag pa yid kyis byed pa bsod nams kyi tshogs dang / bdag don la mi re gzhan la mi spyod pa nyid tshad med pa bzhi dang / thams cad sems stong par shes pa ye
<p>161b.3</p>shes kyi tshogs dang / de ltar shes pas gzhan med pas bsrung pa dang / de ltar sems gtso bas gzhal yas khang / shes rab skye bas rgyu'i rdo rje 'chang yin pa sems su dran pas/ sems la spros pa ye shes sems dpa' bstim pa'o/ /de'i dus dbang po yul du snang bas
<p>161b.4</p>skye mched kyi lha dang / de yang bdag gzhan gnyis su med par byas pas sku gsum dang / des 'gro don nus pas dbang dang / nyams su myong bas bdud rtsi myang ba dang / bkag pa med pas mchod pa dang / ngo mtshar che bas bstod par shes pa'o/ /thams cad gsang ba'i rgyud nas/ de las
<p>161b.5</p>byung ba de nyid pa/ /zhes pas de la zhes pas dam tshig gi phyag rgya bsgom pa'o/ /de yang sku las 'byung zhing rtog pa med pa ma zad pa'o/ /brgyud nas 'gro don snang bas dam tshig yin la/ zad pa med pas phyag rgya'o/ /las kyi phyag rgya yang de ltar du shes pas bde ba la bdag gzhan gnyis
<p>161b.6</p>las 'byung bas rtsol ba'i las dang / bden pa'i phyag rgya'o/ /thams cad gsang ba'i rgyud nas/ las ni bdag gzhan bya ba ste/ /nyams med gnas pa rgya ru bshad/ /ces pa'o/ /chos kyi phyag rgya yang de las shes pas thams cad chos su gyur pa re dogs med pas ma yengs pa'o/ /
<p>161b.7</p>rgyud las/ chos las sems 'byung 'khrul pa tshad mnyam mam langs kyang mi g.yo ba/ zhes pas so/ /phyag rgya chen po yang de ltar gsum po shes pas bdag la dus dang ris med par sku bzhi 'byung ba'i phyag rgya bzhi la gnas pa'o/ /rgyud las/ phyag rgya chen po mchog chen po/ /dus gsum
<p>162a</p>
<p>162a.1</p>mi mnyam chos kyi sku/ /zhes so/ /de shes pas mi phan pas bsgom par bya'o/ /yi dgas ston pa'i rgyud nas/ sku bzhi 'dod pas phyag rgya bzhi/ /ma bsgrubs thob pa ma yin te/ /rgyu rkyen med par sa bcus kyang / /rgyu med byang chub sprul mi nus/ /zhes pas so/ /las
<p>162a.2</p>kyi phyag rgya rtsa dang rlung dang ngag gis bsgom pa'o/ /chos kyi sku ma yengs par bsgom pa'o/ /phyag rgya chen po mi 'dzin par bsgom pa'o/ /de yang slob dpon gzhan dag dkyil 'khor 'khor lo rdzogs nas lha bsdus nas nA da dang / phra mo thig le bsgom zhing mi rtog par 'dod la/ rjes thob
<p>162a.3</p>med par phyag rgya chen por 'dod de/ de yang ma yin te/ rim gyis 'og ma 'gags te dgos pa med pa'i skyon ni la la mi dgos brtan byed du 'dod de/ yang mi bden te/ gsum la slob pa bas gcig nyid la brten na skyed par nges te/ 'dir dbang bzhi sngon du song nas lam phyag rgya bzhi ka
<p>162a.4</p>dgos la skad cig la bsgoms te 'bras bu yang sku bzhi 'byung bas bla ma brgyud pa yang dbang bzhi bskur nas shes par bya/ bstan par bya ste/ de nyid nas bzhi ka dgos par dam tshig phyag rgya gcig bsgoms na/ rnal 'byor pa de gzugs gnyis 'thob/ /las kyi phyag rgya gcig bsgoms na/ /
<p>162a.5</p>rnal 'byor pa de 'dod khams skye/ /chos kyi phyag rgya gcig bsgoms na/ /rnal 'byor pa de gzugs khams skye/ /phyag rgya chen po gcig bsgoms na/ /rnal 'byor pa de gzugs med khams/ /de bas sngags dang phyag rgya bzhi/ /lam bzhi sku bzhi bcu gnyis zangs/ /zhes pas man ngag
<p>162a.6</p>las nges par 'byung bar bsgom mo/ /de ltar bsgrubs pa'i 'bras bu la gnyis te/ mthar phyin na sku bzhi 'byung ba la lam ma nor ba bzhi ste/ bum pa'i dbang thob/ lus kyi nyes pa dag /rig pa'i dbang thob/ lha lngar gyur pas dam tshig gi phyag rgya bsgom du rung ste/ de ltar skur shes shing / 
<p>162a.7</p>bsgoms pas sha thams cad sgyu mar snang bas me long lta bu'i ye shes rig ste/ sa'i khams dngos po med de/ sangs rgyas spyan ltar mthong bas sangs rgyas spyan gyis sgrub pa'i grogs dang / grub nas sems can gyi snang ba la sa'i khams sangs rgyas spyan du 'byung ba'o/ /sgyu ma'i snang bas
<p>162b</p>
<p>162b.1</p>'gro don ma 'gags par mdzad la/ gzugs tsam por shes pas gzugs rnam par snang mdzad kyis sgrub pa'i grogs byed la/ grub nas sems can gyi snang ba la gzugs rnam par snang mdzad du byung / khrag gis lus khyab cing sdud la rnam pa de thams cad la stong pa'i rgyas thebs pas mnyam
<p>162b.2</p>pa nyid kyi ye shes rig pa ste/ chu'i khams sdud pas mA ma kI dang lha ltar za mnyam ste/ mA ma kIs sgrub pa'i grogs dang / grub nas sems can gyi snang ba la chu'i khams mA ma kIr 'byung ngo / /skye med du mnyam par 'gro don rtog med du byed pas tshor ba la khyad med dgos pa 'byung bas rin chen
<p>162b.3</p>'byung ldan du grub la grub nas sems can gyi snang ba la tshor ba rin chen 'byung ldan du snang ba'o/ /mes dngos po bsreg cing rnam pa de rnams ma 'dres par shes pas so sor rtog pa'i ye shes rig ste/ mes thams cad gsal bas/ gos dkar mo sgrub pa'i grogs dang / grub nas sems can gyi
<p>162b.4</p>snang ba la gos dkar mor byung ba'o/ /'du shes tshad med cing 'gro don mi 'chad pas 'du shes snang ba mtha' yas su grub cing grub nas sems can gyi snang ba la 'du shes snang ba mtha' yas su byung ba'o/ /rlung gi gnas su skyel ba de thams cad spyad pas bya ba nan tan gyi ye shes rig ste/ rlung gi
<p>162b.5</p>khams bskyod pas sgrol mar gyur te/ sgrub pa'i grogs dang grub nas rlung gi khams sgrol mar 'byung ba'o/ /'gro ba yang ye shes gong nas gong du 'dus byas yod pas don yod grub pa'i grogs su 'du byed cing grub nas 'du byed kyi phung po don yod grub par 'byung ba'o/ /nam mkha'i khams rgya
<p>162b.6</p>chad pas dngos por snang ba thams cad stong zhing bdag med pas chos kyi dbyings kyi ye shes rig ste/ nam mkha'i khams kyis khyab pa reg bya rdo rje mar gyur te sgrub pa'i grogs nam mkha'i khams reg bya rdo rjes byed la grub nas nam mkha'i khams reg bya rdo rjer 'byung ba'o/ /thams cad rang gi
<p>162b.7</p>sems yin zhing stong par rig pas 'byung la de ltar gsal bas rnam par shes pa des grogs byas nas rdo rje sems dpar sgrub la grub nas sems can gyi snang ba la rnam par shes pa'i phung po rdo rje sems dpar 'byung ba'o/ /de ltar shes tsam na yul thams cad longs spyad du btub pas mchod pa'i lha
<p>163a</p>
<p>163a.1</p>mo dang ye shes su 'gyur bas man ngag gis de lha dang bde ba dang mi rtog pa'i ngang stong par yul rnams song bas skye mched lhar 'gyur ba'o/ /de yang dngos po gsal ba myong ba bde ba gnyis med mi rtog pas sku gsung thugs su 'gyur ba'o/ /bdag tu gnas pa mi bskyod pa dbang
<p>163a.2</p>du gyur pa'o/ /nyams su myong ba rdo rje 'dzin pa snang ba mtha' yas bdud rtsir gyur pa'o/ /de bzhin longs spyod ngo mtshar ba rin chen 'byung ldan dang don yod grub pa mchod bstod du gyur pa'o/ /de ltar gcig nyid rnam shes lnga phung po lnga rgyu khams lnga dang de bzhin brgya stong khri 'bum du grub nas
<p>163a.3</p>sems can gyi snang ba la byung ba'o/ /de ltar lus kyi nyes pa dag rig pa'i lha mos bkrus lha lngar gyur pas dam tshig gi phyag rgya mthar phyin pa'o/ /gsang dbang thob pas ngag gi nyes pa dag la shes rab ye shes kyi dbang thob longs spyod las kyi phyag rgya bsgom du rung ste/ sangs rgyas kyi ye shes byang chub
<p>163a.4</p>sems dpas gtor ma byin te lce la gzhag pas a wa d+hU tIr phyin 'khor lo rgyas te/ sangs rgyas kyis byin gyis brlabs pas ngag gi nyes pa dag la/ ye shes nyams su myong zhing 'dod yon spyad pas ye shes thob la/ longs skur gyur nas las kyi phyag rgya mthar phyin pa'o/ /de bzhin du
<p>163a.5</p>klu sgrub nas brgyud pas/ de ltar dag thob gyur nas mthar phyin pa'o/ /gzhan nas brgyud pa yang de bzhin no/ /shes rab ye shes kyi dbang thob nas yid kyi nyes pa dag /shes rab kyi dbang gis mi rtog par gyur nas chos kyi phyag rgya bsgom du rung ste/ sems nyid shes pa de las 'byung zhing
<p>163a.6</p>smrar med pas gong ma rnams der bsdu 'dus pas mthar phyin pa'o/ /bzhi pas lus dang / ngag dang yid kyi sgrib pa dag /tshig gi dbang brjod du med pa brdar bsgom du rung ste/ de ltar de bzhin bzhi pa'o/ /zhes gsungs pas der bzhi'o/ /rgyas par man ngag las shes par bya'o/ /
<p>163a.7</p>snang ba'i chos thams cad kyi spyi'i mtshan nyid kyang de ltar shes pa tsam na phyogs kha dog rten dang / phra rab tu snang ba gzugs la sogs sa sogs man ngag la brten pa dang / 'gro ba re re la yang de bzhin gnas shing snang ba 'byung ba'o/ /de bzhin du bzhi pa dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga dang
<p>163b</p>
<p>163b.1</p>bstan pa dbang bcu bzhir shes par bya'o/ /bsrung bar bya ba la yang rtsa ba dang yan lag ste/ gshin rje'i rgyud nas bstan pa'i rtsa ba bcu bzhi bsrung ste/ slob dpon dbang bskur ba dang / chos ston pa gnyis dang / dbang la las kyi dang / rdo rje slob dpon dang / gsang ba la sogs pa
<p>163b.2</p>lnga'o/ /bsrung bya khyod kyi chos de mi byed khyed rang khyer/ de nas khyod kyi slob ma nga min zhes pa dang / bstan pa mi nyan par sdig las byed pa dang / 'byor pa la gnod pa dang / rku ba dang / btsun mo la spyod pa dang / brnyas sems dang / nyes pa brjod pa dang / mang po'i gseb tu mi
<p>163b.3</p>mdzes pa'o/ /bka' ni sangs rgyas kyis gsungs pa ste/ bsrung ba bka' ltar mi byed pa dang / ma mnyan par rang dgar 'chad pa'o/ /rdo rje spun ni dbang dang rgyud dang man ngag slob dpon gcig pa'am/ dus gcig pa'o/ /bsrung bya zhe sdang gis nyes pa brjod cing nyes pa bsgrags na rung
<p>163b.4</p>sems so/ /byang chub sems ni gong ltar sems can thams cad la bskyed pa dang / kun rdzob lus la bskyed pa'o/ /bsrung ba ni de dag don du sems pa dang / ting nge 'dzin nyams par byed pa'o/ /sems can rnams zhes pa 'gro drug /byams sems spong zhes pa phan mi 'dogs
<p>163b.5</p>pa dang / bdag med pa dang / dge ba mi bsngo ba dang / sems can gyi sdug bsngal ma shes pas rang 'dod byed pa'o/ /ma smin zhes pa dbang ma thob pa dang / mi go ba la bsrung bya sngags dang / gdams ngag zab mo ston pa'o/ /rang ngam zhes pa sangs rgyas pa dang / mu stegs dang
<p>163b.6</p>gnyis/ bsrung bya dang po mi smad par mnyan rab tu lam yin min gyis grub mtha' bcad de/ rab tu mi gnas pas mi smad do/ /tha ma phyag rgya bzhir rang gi snang ba med pas mi smad do/ /sangs rgyas zhes pas gong ltar sgrub shes tsam na'o/ /bsgrub bya sangs rgyas su mi bsgrub pa dang / 
<p>163b.7</p>srog btang ba dang / sdig pa'i las kyis lus sdug bsngal bar spyod pa'o/ /rang bzhin dag pa zhes pa chos thams cad rab tu mi gnas pa/ bsrung bya rtag pa'am chad pa'am/ phung po gsum pa'am/ rten 'brel lam/ rnam pa dang bcas pa'am/ rnam med dam sgyu ma don dam du 'dod pa'o/ /
<p>164a</p>
<p>164a.1</p>gdug la zhes pa bstan pa dang / bla ma la sdang ba dang / bdag grogs po la byams ldan zhes pa/ bsrung bya tshar mi gcod pa ni byams pa dang / shes par dga' zhing kha spyang gis grogs byed pa'o/ /ming sogs zhes pa dang / bdud rtsi sogs/ bsrung bya der zhes
<p>164a.2</p>pa mi gtsang ba dang / don yod pa mi shes pa'o/ /dad ldan zhes pa phyir mi ldog pa sems su zhes pa bsrung bya ste/ blo chos dang ma sbyar ba gong 'og la sun 'byin par byed pa dang / sngags la dad pa'i rigs ngan dang / btsun pa dang bud med mi 'jug pa'o/ /ji bzhin rnyed ces pa ni rdo rje'i
<p>164a.3</p>rigs la sogs pa'o/ /mi sten zhes pa bsrung bya 'dod ngo la gzhan dbang spyod pa dang grogs su gyur pa'o/ /bud med ces thams cad bsrung bya mi lus rten bzang ba la ma brten pa dang / ye shes kyi rten yin pa dang / sprul sku lhu mas su bltams pa dang / mngon byang lnga las byung ba dang / 
<p>164a.4</p>longs sku de las byung ba'i ye shes kyi snang ba yin la/ bde chen gnas pa zhes pa ni smad pa tsam mo/ /rtsa ba dang / yan lag dang / bla ma lnga bcu pa yang blta zhing bsrung ngo / /nyams na skyon te/ rtsa ba nyams na dbang bskur ba dang / tshogs 'khor bya zhing de nyid bslang / /yan lag nyams na
<p>164a.5</p>bshags pa dang / /maN+Dal 'byor pas bla ma dang / /yi dam mchod cing de nyid bsrung / /rtsa bar shes dang bsgom dang bsrung / /spyad par bya ba bzhi po 'di/ /ma yengs gus par bya ba dang / /gzhan don gtang bar mi bya'o/ /spyad par bya ba la gong ma ltar shes pas/ snod dang / gnas dang / rgyal
<p>164a.6</p>po dang / dus dang ldan zhing bla ma la mi gnod pa dang / bstan pa la mi gnod pa dang / rang la mi gnod pas zhi sogs dang / dbang dang chos dang / gtor ma dang / sbyin sreg dag bdag gi tshe 'di dang / phyi ma'i don min par gzhan sgrol ba'i bsam pas sbyin pa dang / spyod pa dang / 'gro ba
<p>164a.7</p>'dul bas 'dul ba dang / /'gro ba sbyor bas byang chub sems/ /rigs la sbyor bas dam tshig ni/ /ma yengs spyod lam bzhis spyad bya'o/ /bdag blo rmongs pas gus pa yis/ /yun rings mgon po bsnyen pa las/ /brgyud pa'i rgyud don nyams myong nas/ /byams pa'i sems kyis nan tan
<p>164b</p>
<p>164b.1</p>byas/ /yi ges gsol btab dpal mo yis/ /de nyid mthong ba'i lam 'di byas/ /'di las bsod nams ci thob des// 'gro bas sku bzhi myur thob shog /de nyid mthong ba'i lam dpal ye shes rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so// //rgya gar gyi mkhan po dpal de nyid dang / lo tsA ba rngog bud+d+ha
<p>164b.2</p>pA las bsgyur te gtan la phab pa'o// //dpal shing kun du tshogs 'khor sar gsol ba btab nas lha khang bi ha rar bsgyur ba'o//[ ]@##/ /rgya gar skad du/ gu ru pa raM pa ra kra mo pa de sha nA ma/ bod skad du/ bla ma brgyud pa'i rim pa'i man ngag ces bya ba/ bla ma dam pa rnams
<p>164b.3</p>la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dngos kun rang bzhin zung 'jug pa'i/ /'od gsal stong pa'i bdag nyid kyi/ /lhun grub de la phyag 'tshal te/ /de nas cung zad bri bar bya/ /shin tu bsdus par 'dod rnams dang / /blo dman skye bos rtogs bya'i phyir/ /de nyid thams cad mdor bsdus nas/ /cung
<p>164b.4</p>zad tsam zhig bri bar bya/ /re zhig gang zag ni gnyis te/ spre'u lta bu dang khwa lta bu'o/ /spre'u lta bu ni rim gyis 'jug pa'o/ /khwa lta bu ni cig car 'jug pa'o/rim gyis 'jug pa'i dbang du byas na theg pa ni gsum ste/ nyan thos kyi theg pa dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa dang / 
<p>164b.5</p>theg pa chen po'o/ /theg pa gsum ni gnas pa bzhi la gnas te/ gnas pa bzhi ni bye brag tu smra bar gnas pa dang / mdo sde par gnas pa dang / rnal 'byor spyod par gnas pa dang / dbu ma par gnas pa'o/ /nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas ni bye brag tu smra ba la gnas so/ /bye brag tu
<p>164b.6</p>smra ba la yang gnyis te/ nub phyogs bye brag tu smra ba dang / kha che bye brag tu smra ba'o/ /nyan thos la gsum ste/ dbang po tha ma dang / 'bring dang rab bo/ de la tha ma dang 'bring po ni nub phyogs kha che bye brag tu smra ba la gnas so/ /rab dang rkyen rtog ni kha che bye brag tu smra ba la gnas so/ /
<p>164b.7</p>theg pa chen po la yang gnyis te/ rgyu mtshan nyid kyi theg pa dang / 'bras bu rdo rje'i theg pa'o/ /de la rgyu mtshan nyid kyi theg pa la gsum ste/ tha ma dang / 'bring dang / rab bo/ /tha ma ni mdo sde pa'o/ /'bring ni rnal 'byor spyod pa'o/ /rab ni dbu ma pa'o/ /rnal 'byor spyod pa la gnyis te/ 
<p>165a</p>
<p>165a.1</p>rnam pa dang bcas pa dang / rnam pa med pa'o/ /dbu ma pa la yang gnyis te/ sgyu ma lta bu gnyis su med par smra ba dang / chos thams cad rab tu mi gnas par smra ba'o/ /de ltar na sbyor ba dgu la dbye ba bzhi bzhi ste/ so sor rtog pa dang / sgom pa dang / sgom pa'i dri ma dang / 
<p>165a.2</p>lta ba'o/ /de la dang por re zhig 'jig rten pa'i grub pa'i mthas bdag gcig pu/ rtag pa/ khyab pa/ tshangs par khas len pa'o/ /ma rtogs pa'i blo la de ltar snang na yang yang dag par grub par mi 'gyur te/ bdag gcig pu yin na gcig shi'am skyes pa thams cad shi'am/ skyes par
<p>165a.3</p>thal ba dang / gcig yin pa'i phyir skad cig ma yang rtag par khas len na 'chi 'pho dang skye ba med par thal bar 'gyur te/ rtag pa yin pa'i phyir ro/ /khyab pa yin na gcig bde ba dang / sdug bsngal bas thams cad bde ba dang sdug bsngal gyis khyab par thal bar 'gyur te/ thams
<p>165a.4</p>cad la khyab pa'i phyir ro/ /de ltar rigs pas brtags na bdag yod pa ma yin pas de dag las drang ba'i don du nyan thos kyi theg pa bstan to/ /de la re zhig nyan thos tha ma'i so sor rtog pa ni phyi'i don dmigs pa'i rkyen mtshan nyid par khas len zhing / gang zag la bdag med pa zhes
<p>165a.5</p>bya ba'i khur khur ba'i gang zag rtag pa yang ma yin mi rtag pa yang ma yin pa'o/ /rtag pa ma yin pa ni skad cig mas mi rtag pa'o/ /mi rtag pa ma yin pa ni rgyun gyis rtag pa'o/ /de lta bu'i gang zag rtag pa dang mi rtag pa las 'das par 'dod pa ni so sor rtog pa'o/ /lus ni 'dod
<p>165a.6</p>chags ma spangs na 'khor bar 'khor bar 'gyur/ spangs na ni grol bas lus kyi 'dod chags spang ba'i phyir lus la mi gtsang ba dang / mi sdug pa dang / dur khrod ltar yan lag 'thor bar lta ba ni bsgom pa'o/ /lus la gtsang bar lta ba dang / gang zag rtag par lta ba ni sgom pa'i dri ma'o/ /
<p>165a.7</p>dus 'di nas bzung ste ji srid 'tsho'i bar du gsum la skyabs su 'gro ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba ci mchis pa bdag nyid kyi don du bsngo ba dang / snying rje dang ma bral ba dang / rgan pa dang / bde bar gshegs pa gnyis la phyag byed pa ni lta ba'o/ /'bring po'i so sor rtog pa dang lta ba ni snga ma bzhin no/ /
<p>165b</p>
<p>165b.1</p>'di ni khyad par cung zad cig tsam sems can gyi don byed pa'o/ /sgom pa ni dbugs la slob ste/ kha dog dang / dbyibs dang / reg bya la slob pa'o/ /kha dog la slob pa ni dbugs dkar po sba lcag gi tshad sor brgyad dam/ bcu gnyis sam/ sor bcu drug gam/ nyi shu rtsa bzhi'am/ 
<p>165b.2</p>brgyad cu'am/ ji tsam 'dod kyi bar du bgrangs la/ tshur 'ong lte bar phyin par slob po/ /dbyibs la slob pa ni ut+pa la'am/ rdo rje lta bu la bya'o/ /reg bya la slob pa ni lte ba dang / sna sgor grang ba'i reg bya la slob cing bsgom pa'o/ /bum pa gang ba ltar gang ba'i rlung gis srog dang rtsol ba
<p>165b.3</p>bkag nas sems dran pa med par gyur pa ni sgom pa'i dri ma'o/ /de ni nub phyogs bye brag tu smra bar bstan pa'o/ /nyan thos dbang po rab kyi so sor rtog pa ni phyi'i don khas len pa sngon du 'gro bas lus bdag med par lta zhing 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi bsgom pas/ gang zag kyang stong pa
<p>165b.4</p>nyid du 'dod cing phyi gzung ba ni stong pa nang 'dzin pa'i sems su 'dod pa ni so sor rtog pa'o/ /de la sdug bsngal ba ni phung po'i rang bzhin te shes par bya'o/ /kun 'byung ba ni rnam par rtog pa ste spang bar bya ba'o/ /'gog pa ni dbang po yul las log pa ste mngon du bya'o/ /khams gsum stong
<p>165b.5</p>pa nyid ni mar me bsad pa ltar bkag nas ci yang mi dmigs pa ni sgom pa'o/ /stong pa nyid dang rtag par sgro 'dogs pa ni bsam gtan gyi dri ma'o/ /gzhan gyi don byed pa'i khyad par ni lta ba'o/ /'di'i 'bras bu yang phung po lhag ma dang bcas pa dang lhag ma med pa'o/ /lhag ma dang bcas
<p>165b.6</p>pa ni 'dod chags spangs la lus nyid ma spangs pa'o/ /lhag ma med pa ni 'dod chags pa dang lus gnyis ka spangs pa'o/ /'di ni nyan thos kyi byang chub bo/ /rang sangs rgyas kyi so sor rtog pa ni nyan thos rab 'bring bzhin no/ /yang 'di'i khyad par ni slob dpon med par rang 'byung gi ye
<p>165b.7</p>shes ngang bsam gyis mi khyab pa'o/ /de yang / rdzogs sangs rgyas ni mi 'byung zhing / /nyan thos rnams dang 'das pa dang / /rang sangs rgyas kyi ye shes ni/ /brten pa med par 'byung bar 'gyur/ /zhe'o/ /'di'i bsam gtan ni zhi gnas dang / lhag mthong ngo / /lhag mthong ni dbang po
<p>166a</p>
<p>166a.1</p>yul gyi grong las bzlog pa'o/ /zhi gnas ni lus dang / ngag dang / yid yang dag par sdom pa 'di ni de'i sgom pa'o/ /gnyid yur ba lta bur phyi'i spyod yul 'gags pa dang / gnyid stug po sems dang sems las byung ba shin tu 'gags pa ni sgom pa'i dri ma'o/ /lta ba ni snga
<p>166a.2</p>ma bzhin no/ /'di'i 'bras bu ni tshogs na spyod pa dang bse ru lta bu'o/ /yang nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi snying rje yang sems can la dmigs pa'i snying rje ste/ 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal dang / sdug bsngal gyi sdug bsngal dang / 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal lo/ /'du byed kyi sdug bsngal ni tshor
<p>166a.3</p>ba btang snyoms kyi ngo bo'o/ /sdug bsngal gyi sdug bsngal ni tshor ba sdug bsngal gyi ngo bo nyid do/ /'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal ni tshor ba bde ba'i ngo bo nyid de/ 'di la dmigs shing snying rje byed pa ni sems can la dmigs pa'i snying rje'o/ /kha che bye brag tu smra ba bstan pa de ste theg pa chung ngu
<p>166a.4</p>mdor bstan pa'o/ /de nas gzhan yang theg pa chen po bstan par bya ste/ de la rgyu mtshan nyid kyi theg pa'i dbang po tha ma ni mdo sde pa'o/ /de'i so sor rtog pa ni phyi rol gyi yul cha shas drug gis gzhigs na/ rags snang gi ngo bo med de/ drug chas gzhigs na rdul lo/ /nyi zer gyi rdul bdun cha
<p>166a.5</p>la glang rdul/ glang rdul bdun cha la lug gi rdul/ lug rdul bdun cha la ri bong gi rdul/ ri bong gi rdul bdun cha la chu rdul/ chu rdul bdun cha la lcags rdul/ lcags rdul bdun cha la rdul phra mo/ rdul phra mo bdun cha la rdul phra rab bo/ /de ltar gzhigs pas phyi rol gyi dngos po thams
<p>166a.6</p>cad rdzas su ma grub par 'dod do/ /de la phyogs snga ma mu stegs pa'i gzhung gi rdul phra rab thams cad 'dus pa cha shas gcig tu 'dod do/ rdul phra rab cha shas can gcig yin na yul kha dog sngon po la dmigs nas shes pa sngon por skye ba'i dus su dkar po dang / ser po'i kha dog
<p>166a.7</p>thams cad gcig par thal bar 'gyur te/ gcig pa yin pa'i phyir ro/ /de bas na rdul phra rab ma 'dres pa cha shas can g.yag rnga ne'u gsing de'i 'dab 'byor pa mi snang ba'i ngo bor 'dod do/ /'on te mi snang na yod par cis mngon zhe na/ 'di mngon sum du rnam pa dang bcas pa'i shes pa yul gyis
<p>166b</p>
<p>166b.1</p>bskyed cing 'dug pa'i phyir rdul phra rab yod par shes so/ /de ltar na phyi'i don ni rdul phra rab rdzas su mi grub pa des skyes pa'i shes pa ni rnam pa dang bcas pa'i shes pa skad cig mar 'dod pa ni so sor rtog pa'o/ /bsgom pa gnyis te/ goms par bya ba'i dus dang / mngon du bya ba'i dus so/ /de la goms
<p>166b.2</p>par bya ba'i dus ni dang por dbang po yul gyi grong las bzlog pa la bsam gyis mi khyab pa'o/ /de la bsam gyis mi khyab pa ni rdo rje sems dpa' sku mdog dkar po'i thugs ka ru nyi mar rdo rje'i lte bar hUM bsam mo/ /de nas rdo rje sems dpa'i thugs kar nyi ma la bsdu'o/ /nyi ma yang rdo rje la'o/ /
<p>166b.3</p>rdo rje hUM la'o/ /hUM yang de bzhin gshegs pa drug gi rang bzhin no/ /zhabs skyed u ni don yod grub pa'i rang bzhin no/ /lus po ha ni 'od dpag tu med pa'o/ /mgo bo rin chen 'byung ldan no/ /zla tshes rnam par snang mdzad do/ /thig le mi bskyod pa'o/ /sgra ni rdo rje sems dpa'o/ /de ltar hUM gi
<p>166b.4</p>zhabs bskyed pa'o/ /ha sgra'i bar du rim par thim pas sgra dngos po med par bsgom/ de ni goms par bya ba'i dus so/ /mngon du bya ba ni skad cig la brten nas/ rdo rje skyil krung bcas nas ni/ /sna rtser g.yo ba'i yid gtad la/ /khyim par gyur kyang bsgom par bya/ /zhe'o/ /de bas na mig gnyis
<p>166b.5</p>dang sems sna'i rtse mor gtad nas bltas pas cir yang mi dmigs pa de nyid bsgom pa'o/ /dri ma ni rang sangs rgyas lta bu'o/ /rdul phra rab lta bur chos thams cad mi dmigs pa ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ste/ des pha rol tu phyin pa lnga mi dmigs pa gsum gyis 'khor gsum yongs su
