<p>207a.2</p>ces bya ba la sogs pa'i smon lam dag kyang brjod par bya'o/ /rnam par thar pa'i sgo gsum ni sngar bstan pa rnams so/ /de la gzhol ba ni lha'i rnal 'byor la 'jug pa'i sngon dang phyis kyang de'i rang bzhin du lta ba'o/ /dmigs pa gcig la brtan pa ni
<p>207a.3</p>dang por dmigs pa gcig la zhi gnas brtan par bya ba'am/ 'dod pa'i lha yang dang yang spong bar mi bya ba'am/ res 'ga' ni lha'i sku bsgom/ res 'ga' ni stong pa nyid bsgom pa la yang dang yang mi spong ba'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' rab byung
<p>207a.4</p>bas/ /rang gi 'dul dang cho ga las/ /ma 'das par ni 'bad pa yis/ /sngags kyi dngos grub la reg bya/ /zhes bya ba 'dis ni/ sdom pa gsum la gnas par byas la dngos grub bsgrub par bstan te/ byang chub sems dpa' rab tu byung ba des
<p>207a.5</p>so sor thar pa'i sdom pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i sdom pa dang / sngags kyi dam tshig gsum la gnas te/ de dag las ma 'das par 'bad la gsang sngags kyi dngos grub myur du bsgrub par bya'o/ /gal te rdo rje slob dpon khyim pa yin la slob ma rab
<p>207a.6</p>tu byung ba yin na/ ji ltar bya zhe na/ khyim par gyur pa'i sngags pa yis/ /rab tu byung ba'i sngags pa dag /bdag gi slob mar gyur pa na/ /rkang pa bkru dang phyag la sogs/ /nam yang bdag gir mi bya'o/ /de dag ni go sla ba'i phyir ma bshad do/ /'o na
<p>207a.7</p>ci ltar bya zhe na/ rtag tu rab tu byung ba la/ /shAkya'i dbang po ltar 'dzin pas/ /gus pas bsnyen bkur bya ba yin/ /zhes bya ba smos te/ rtag tu zhes bya ba dus thams cad du'o/ /shAkya'i dbang po ni shAkya'i rigs kyi gtso bo ste/ bcom ldan 'das shAkya
<p>207b</p>
<p>207b.1</p>thub pa'o/ /de dang 'dra bar bltas la gus pa dang bcas pas bsnyen bkur thams cad bya ba'o/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ sangs rgyas bstan pa rin chen sgron/ /'bar ba'i snod ni dka' thub can/ /ngur smrig 'dzin pa shAkya'i sras/ /dge slong rnams ni yin
<p>207b.2</p>phyir ro/ /zhes bya ba smras te/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dam pa'i chos ni nor bu rin po che dang 'dra ba yin te/ de la brten nas 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i bde ba thams cad 'byung ba'i phyir ro/ /de'i phyir de ni nor bu rin po che 'od 'bar ba lta bu
<p>207b.3</p>yin la/ de 'dzin cing 'chang ba'i snod gser gyi za ma tog lta bu ni shAkya'i sras te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi slob ma dka' thub can ngur smrig gyon pa'i dge slong rnams yin pa'i phyir ro/ /byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la 'jug pa las kyang / bstan rtsa
<p>207b.4</p>dge slong nyid yin na/ /dge slong nyid kyang dka' bar gnas/ /zhes bstan pas/ dge slong ni bstan pa 'dzin pa'i rtsa ba yin par bstan pa yin no/ /gzhan yang rtag tu bya ba'i cho ga ni/ gtor ma gtang ba dang / sAts+tsha gdab pa dang / bzang po spyod
<p>207b.5</p>pa la sogs pa smon lam rgya chen po gdab pa dang / tshad med pa bzhi sgom pa la sogs pa dge ba'i las thams cad bya ba kho na'o/ /de ltar dgongs pa can gyi gsung / /dgongs bcas dgongs min ji lta bar/ /bsdus nas bdag gis bris pa las/ /
<p>207b.6</p>ston ka'i zla ba dkar ba'i/ /dge ba cung zhig gar thob des/ /'gro bas ma nor lam rtogs shog /ces bya la dgongs pa can gyi gsung zhes bya ba ni/ rdo rje'i tshig don sna tshogs ston pa rnams so/ /dgongs bcas dgongs min ji lta bar/ /zhes
<p>207b.7</p>bya ba la/ dgongs bcas ni gsang ba'i rgyan zhes bya ba'i rgyud las/ sangs rgyas thams cad chags las 'khrungs/ /de bzhin sdang dang rmongs las 'khrungs/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / zla gsang thig le las kyang / 'dod chags zhe sdang
<p>208a</p>
<p>208a.1</p>gti mug rnams/ /bsten na dngos grub myur du 'thob/ /ces gsungs pa lta bu'o/ /dgongs pa can ma yin pa ni/ srog chags dag ni gsad mi bya/ /ma byin par yang mi blang ngo / /'dod spyod dag ni mi bya zhing / /brdzun du smra
<p>208a.2</p>bar mi bya'o/ /gnod pa kun gyi rtsa ba yi/ /chang ni rnam par spang bar bya/ /zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o/ /gzhan yang sgra ji bzhin par bstan pa dang / sgra ji bzhin ma yin par bstan pa rnams so/ /mdor bsdus pa ni rgyas par bstan pa'o/ /ston
<p>208a.3</p>ka'i zla ba ltar dkar ba'i/ /zhes bya ba la sogs pa ni go bla'o/ /ma nor rgyud kyi don brtan nas/ /blo chung rnams phyir bris pa la/ /tshig dang don la 'khrul pa dag /mkhas pa rnams kyis bzod par mdzod/ /ces bya ba rgyud ma nor ba gsang
<p>208a.4</p>ba 'dus pa dang / dgongs pa lung ston pa dang / 'jam dpal gyi rgyud la sogs pa'o/ /de dag gi don phyin ci ma log pa la brten nas bdag las blo chung ba dang / shes rab dman pa rnams kyi phyir bris pa ste bstan pa la tshig dang don la 'khrul pa ste/ /tshig
<p>208a.5</p>sdebs ma legs pa dang / don log par bstan pa yod na mkhas pa rnams kyis te/ mang du thos shing mkhyen pa che ba rnams kyis bzod par mdzod cig ces bya ba ni/ so so'i skye bo la 'khrul pa 'byung ba ngo mtshar mi che bas bzod pa mdzad par 'os so zhes bya
<p>208a.6</p>ba'i don te/ /'jig rten gsum gtso thams cad mkhyen pa'i gsung / /bdud rtsi lta bu'i tshig 'bru 'ga' bstan pas/ /gzhan la phan pa byung na dge ba des/ /'gro ba kun gyis sangs rgyas thob par shog /gsang sngags la 'jug pa'i
<p>208a.7</p>rab tu byed pa drug cu pa'i 'grel pa paN+Di ta A tsar+ya dz+nyA na A ka ras mdzad pa rdzogs so// //rgya gar gyi mkhan po dz+nyA na A ka ra nyid dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa// //
